## Access Denied Message

> **Q:**     What do I need to provide to the Service Desk when I get an **Access Denied** message?
> 
> **A:**    The following steps are in the Chrome browser.
> 
> 1.  On the page that displays the Access Denied message, press the F12 key.
> 2.  Select the Network tab. ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/1831503544/image2022-1-21_14-35-8.png?version=1&modificationDate=1642797309638&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=542&height=231)
> 3.  Select the “Doc” tab.  
>     ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/1831503544/image2022-1-21_14-30-5.png?version=1&modificationDate=1642797006398&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=507&height=297)
> 4.  Select the first row to appear under the “Name” column.![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/1831503544/image2022-1-21_14-29-16.png?version=1&modificationDate=1642796957269&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=584&height=337)
> 5.  Select “Headers”.  
>     ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/1831503544/image2022-1-21_14-31-11.png?version=1&modificationDate=1642797072770&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=515&height=329)
> 6.  Scroll down until you see the “Response Headers” section.![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/1831503544/image2022-1-21_14-32-13.png?version=1&modificationDate=1642797134824&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=650&height=393)
> 7.  Send us a screenshot of everything in the “Response Headers” section.![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/1831503544/image2022-1-21_14-33-18.png?version=1&modificationDate=1642797199881&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=650&height=424)

# Attachments - STRATUS Knowledge Base - Confluence

> ## Excerpt
> One or more files can be attached in many places in Stratus including Dashboards and Attachment tabs.

---
-   1 [Add Attachment](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2081619969/Attachments#Add-Attachment)
-   2 [Viewer > Attachments Tab](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2081619969/Attachments#Viewer-%3E-Attachments-Tab)
    -   2.1 [Preview Attachments](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2081619969/Attachments#Preview-Attachments)
    -   2.2 [Preview and Markup](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2081619969/Attachments#Preview-and-Markup)
    -   2.3 [Download](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2081619969/Attachments#Download)
    -   2.4 [Delete](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2081619969/Attachments#Delete)
    -   2.5 [Attachment Download](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2081619969/Attachments#Attachment-Download)
-   3 [Dashboard Attachments](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2081619969/Attachments#Dashboard-Attachments)
    -   3.1 [Preview Attachments](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2081619969/Attachments#Preview-Attachments.1)
    -   3.2 [Download Single Attachment](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2081619969/Attachments#Download-Single-Attachment)
    -   3.3 [Download All or ZIP Attachment](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2081619969/Attachments#Download-All-or-ZIP-Attachment)

## Add Attachment

One or more files can be attached in many places in Stratus including Dashboards and Attachment tabs.

1.  **To attach one file:**
    
    1.  Click the option to **Add Attachment**. A find file dialog similar to the following will display.
        
    2.  Select one file and then click **Open**.
        
    3.  If the selected file has not been previously uploaded, then it will upload with no additional dialogs.
        
    4.  If the selected file has been previously uploaded, then the **Confirm File Names** dialog will display.
        
    5.  **File Name** - Do one of the following:
        
        1.  **Replace** \- Leave the duplicate File Name as is (Ex. Attachment 4) and then click the **Replace** button. The file will be replaced and use the same name.
            
        2.  **New** - Enter a new File Name. The file will be uploaded with the new name.
            
        3.  **Use** \- Click the **Use** button (Ex. Use Attachment 4 (1)) to automatically rename the new file to the name displayed within the button. The file will be uploaded so that both files exist in Stratus.
            
2.  **To attach multiple files:**
    
    1.  Click the option to **Add Attachments**. A find file dialog similar to the following will display.
        
    2.  Select one or more files and then click **Open**.
        
    3.  If none of the selected files have been previously uploaded, then all files will upload with no additional dialogs. The page will automatically refresh after each upload is complete and ready for display.
        
    4.  If any of the selected files have been previously uploaded, then the **Confirm File Names** dialog will display.
        
        1.  **File Name** - Do one of the following:
            
            1.  **Replace** \- Leave the duplicate File Name as is (Ex. Attachment 3) with the **Replace** radio button selected. The file will be replaced and use the same name.
                
            2.  **New** - Enter a new File Name. The file will be uploaded with the new name.
                
            3.  **Use** \- Select the **Use** radio button to automatically rename the new file to be uploaded so that both files exist in Stratus.
                
    5.  If multiple files already exist, a pagination dialog will display (Ex. 1 / 2). Click the arrows to navigate between files.
        
    6.  Click **OK when done.**
        

## Viewer > Attachments Tab

The Attachments tab within the Packages > Viewer or the Assemblies > Viewer includes a versatile table to preview, download, and markup the attachment.

1.  Go to the Attachments tab for Packages or Assemblies.
    
2.  Each attachment row includes a content rollup labeled **Source Type** which can be expanded to display any attachments for its sub source types (Ex. Assembly, Part, Tracking update).
    

## Preview Attachments

1.  Click the expander for the attachment. The following file types can be previewed:
    
    1.  .pdf, .txt, .csv, .gif, .png, .jpg, .jpeg, .xls, .xlsx, .xlsm, .doc, .docx, .zpl
        
2.  The Attachment will automatically display in the preview panel for the following file types:
    
    1.  .pcf, .pdf, .txt, .csv, .zpl, .gif, .jpeg, .jpg, .png
        
    2.  Preview is not available for: .xls, .xlsx, .xlsm, .doc, .docx, .maj, .mp4, .rej, .zip
        

## Preview and Markup

1.  For PDF attachments only, the **Markup** button will display. Click the expander to display the attachment.
    
2.  Click the **Markup** button. The Markup Tools will display and can be used to markup the PDF.
    
3.  See the [**Markup for Viewers Assemblies and Packages**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2309521409 "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2309521409") article for more information.
    

## Download

1.  Click the **Download** button.
    
2.  The file will download to your computer’s default download folder. There is no prompt to select a download folder.
    

## Delete

1.  Click the **Delete** button.
    
2.  The Delete Attachment dialog will display.
    
3.  Click either the **KEEP** button to retain the file or click the **Delete** button to delete the file.
    

## Attachment Download

1.  **Download** \- Click the **Download** button to download the file.
    
2.  **Delete** \- Click the Delete button to delete the attachment.
    
3.  The following file types can be attached:
    
    1.  .pdf, .txt, .csv, .gif, .png, .jpg, .jpeg, .xls, .xlsx, .xlsm, .doc, .docx, .maj, .mp4, .rej, .zip, .zpl
        
4.  The downloaded file name syntax will be:
    
    1.  **Name of the attachment** (Ex. REV-FR-0003)
        
    2.  **Date downloaded** (Ex. 08-28-2023)
        
    3.  **Time stamp** to make each download unique (Ex. 21-33-40)
        
    4.  **File type** (Ex. pcf).
        
5.  **Download Attachment**
    
    1.  To download a single file attachment, click its corresponding **Download Attachment** button. The file will download to your default downloads folder. No prompt or confirmation will display. The file name syntax will be:
        
        1.  **Name of the attachment** (Ex. REV-FR-0003)
            
        2.  **Date downloaded** (Ex. 08-28-2023)
            
        3.  **Time stamp** to make each download unique (Ex. 21-33-40)
            
        4.  **File type** (Ex. pcf)
            

## Dashboard Attachments

The Packages > Dashboard and the Assemblies > Dashboard include an Attachments column on the default report.

## Preview Attachments

1.  Click the **Open Attachment** button. The attached files will display in a fly-out dialog.
    
2.  Click the **Preview Attachment** button.
    
3.  The file will open in a separate browser window for certain file types including:
    
    1.  .pcf, .pdf, .txt, .csv, .zpl, .gif, .jpeg, .jpg, .png.
        

## Download Single Attachment

1.  Click the **Open Attachment** button. The attached files will display in a fly-out dialog.
    
2.  Click the file name link.
    
3.  The file will download to your default downloads folder. No prompt or confirmation will display. The file name syntax will be:
    
    1.  **Name of the attachment** (Ex. REV-FR-0003)
        
    2.  **Date downloaded** (Ex. 08-28-2023)
        
    3.  **Time stamp** to make each download unique (Ex. 21-33-40)
        
    4.  **File type** (Ex. pcf)
        

## Download All or ZIP Attachment

1.  **Download All** - Click the **Download All** button to download each individual file attachments associated with the selected Package, Assembly, or Container to your default download folder. The name of each file will follow the syntax as if the individual file’s Download Attachment (above) button was clicked.
    
2.  **Download All (ZIP)** - To download a single zip file with all of the attachments associated with the selected Package, Assembly, or Container to your default download folder, click the **Download All (ZIP)** button. The file name syntax will be the:
    
    1.  **Name**
        
        1.  **Package** \- Name of the first file in the attachment list
            
        2.  **Assembly** \- Name of the first file in the attachment list
            
        3.  **Container** \- Name of the Container
            
    2.  **Attachments**
        
    3.  **Date downloaded** (Ex. 08-28-2023)
        
    4.  **Time stamp** to make each download unique (Ex. 21-29-21)
        
    5.  **File type** (Ex. .zip)

# BIM 360 Docs: Projects, Users, and Apps Integration - STRATUS Knowledge Base - Confluence

> ## Excerpt
> A project and user must be added to your BIM 360 Docs account before they can be added to your company in STRATUS.

---
A project and user must be added to your BIM 360 Docs account before they can be added to your company in STRATUS.

-   1 [Stratus Apps Integration](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/30900234/BIM+360+Docs+Projects+Users+and+Apps+Integration#Stratus-Apps-Integration)
-   2 [Video](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/30900234/BIM+360+Docs+Projects+Users+and+Apps+Integration#Video)
-   3 [BIM 360 Projects](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/30900234/BIM+360+Docs+Projects+Users+and+Apps+Integration#BIM-360-Projects)
-   4 [BIM 360 Users](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/30900234/BIM+360+Docs+Projects+Users+and+Apps+Integration#BIM-360-Users)
    -   4.1 [Add people to the BIM 360 member directory](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/30900234/BIM+360+Docs+Projects+Users+and+Apps+Integration#Add-people-to-the-BIM-360-member-directory)
    -   4.2 [Add people a BIM 360 project](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/30900234/BIM+360+Docs+Projects+Users+and+Apps+Integration#Add-people-a-BIM-360-project)
-   5 [Permission the Project Files folders and files](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/30900234/BIM+360+Docs+Projects+Users+and+Apps+Integration#Permission-the-Project-Files-folders-and-files)

## Stratus Apps Integration

Before STRATUS can be used with your BIM 360 account, you must activate the STRATUS App integration.

1.  Click the 9 dots, select **Account Admin**.
    
2.  Click the **Apps** tab.
    
3.  If the **Apps** tab does not display, you’ll need to request that the **Apps integrations** tab be enabled by sending an email to [jared.coelho@autodesk.com](mailto:jared.coelho@autodesk.com "mailto:jared.coelho@autodesk.com"). In your email include your company Account ID. 
    
4.  Once enabled, click the Apps tab, click the STRATUS app button, and then click the **Add to BIM 360** button. This will enable STRATUS to sync with Docs.
    
5.  Your STRATUS administrator can now add users to your STRATUS company and to a Project.
    

## Video

**Add Users to a BIM 360 Docs (1:24)**

<iframe allowfullscreen="" allowtransparency="true" data-hasbody="false" data-layout="default" data-local-id="78bbae96-3f19-4c1e-9b56-524ecd8bbec8" data-macro-id="c0cc5bbe-c115-454a-a479-aec99f142578" data-macro-name="widget" frameborder="0" height="364" mozallowfullscreen="" webkitallowfullscreen="" width="640" src="https://player.vimeo.com/video/257044662?h=embed"></iframe>

This video demonstrates:

1.  How a BIM 360 Docs administrator invites users to a BIM 360 project.
    
2.  How to invite the STRATUS team to a BIM 360 project (optional).
    
3.  How to change a user’s access to a BIM 360 project within BIM 360 Docs. Additional access permissions can be managed within STRATUS but are not part of this video.
    
4.  How to enable the Apps tab by sending an email to [jared.coelho@autodesk.com](mailto:jared.coelho@autodesk.com "mailto:jared.coelho@autodesk.com") and include your Account ID (a.k.a. Company Docs URL).
    

## BIM 360 Projects

STRATUS can synchronize BIM 360 project profile information to the STRATUS project.

**To create new BIM 360 Project:**

1.  Login to BIM 360 Docs, click the 9 dots and then select Account Admin.
    
2.  Click the Project tab.
    
3.  Click the **Add** button. The **Create Project Profile** dialog will display. During the link process, BIM 360 Docs project information populates fields like project job number, project type, address, and dates in STRATUS. If a BIM 360 Docs project has already been sync’d at least once with STRATUS, then, fields will only be sync’d to STRATUS when they are empty. STRATUS will not overwrite existing values using the Refresh Projects from BIM 360 button.
    
4.  Below is an example of BIM 360 Docs project information that can be sync'ed to the STRATUS project.
    
5.  Below is an example of BIM 360 Docs information in STRATUS.
    
6.  See the [**Projects (Admin)**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/11534406/Projects+Admin "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/11534406/Projects+Admin") for more information.
    

## BIM 360 Users

## **Add people to the BIM 360 member directory**

1.  Login to BIM 360 Docs, click the 9 dots and then select **Account Admin**.
    
2.  Click the **Members** tab.
    
3.  Click the **Add** drop-down and select add people to the member directory.
    
4.  The **Add People to the Member Directory** dialog will display.
    
5.  Enter **email address**, follow the prompts, and click **Save**.
    
6.  Once added, these users will be available to any project admin who wants to add people to their project.
    

## **Add people a BIM 360 project**

1.  Login to BIM 360 Docs, click the 9 dots and then select Account Admin.
    
2.  Select the Projects tab.
    
3.  The Project Admin page will display.
    

5.  Alternatively, if you are already logged into the project, click the 9 dots and then select Project Admin.
    
6.  Either way make sure the Members tab is selected.
    
7.  The list of project Members displays.
    
8.  Click the **Add** button. The Add Project Members dialog will display.
    
9.  Enter the email addresses of the people you want to invite and then click Select.
    
10.  If you are inviting the STRATUS team to your project to support your installation, enter [STRATUS@gogtp.com](mailto:STRATUS@gogtp.com "mailto:STRATUS@gogtp.com") and click Select.
    
11.  The users will display on the Members page.
    
12.  For each user, assign a company, project role, and at least one service. The Document Management service is required to view published models.
    
13.  Then click the **Add to Project** button.
    
    **Invitation to join the project**
    
14.  An invitation will be sent to the people added to the project.
    
15.  A user **must click Accept** in the email they receive to join the project.
    
16.  Once the user accepts the invitation by clicking the link in the invitation, you will receive an invitation acceptance confirmation email.
    
17.  In addition to adding new members, you can also manage member’s project permissions on this tab. Your STRATUS administrator will configure more granular project roles and permissions within STRATUS.
    
18.  Similarly, in STRATUS, you’ll need to add users to project and set their project role for each project.
    

## Permission the Project Files folders and files

1.  Once a BIM 360 project has been created and BIM 360 users have been added to the project, you may need to permission the folders and / or files depending on how you have configured your document management system. If a STRATUS user has access to your BIM 360 but doesn't have access to the project, project folder, or model / drawing, then they will receive an Unauthorized error in STRATUS when they attempt to view the model.
    
2.  Click the 9 dots and select Document Management.
    
3.  The Plans folder limits the file types that can be stored in it, so STRATUS only allows publishing models to the Project Files folder.
    
4.  Click the **option list button** and select the **Permissions** option.
    
5.  The Folder Settings Permission tab will display. You can assign permission to individuals or you can create a project role and give the project role folder permissions.

# Digital Work Stations - STRATUS Knowledge Base - Confluence

> ## Excerpt
> Wireless or hard wired Internet will work for your shop. For Wi-fi ensure signal is strong in all areas of the shop. A stable, reliable, high-performing internet connection with adequate bandwidth and speed is perhaps the single most important key to success.

---
-   1 [Internet](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2321088513/Digital+Work+Stations#Internet)
-   2 [Software Needs](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2321088513/Digital+Work+Stations#Software-Needs)
-   3 [Station Hardware Recommendations](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2321088513/Digital+Work+Stations#Station-Hardware-Recommendations)
    -   3.1 [Mini Computer or Desktop Option](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2321088513/Digital+Work+Stations#Mini-Computer-or-Desktop-Option)
    -   3.2 [Tablet Options](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2321088513/Digital+Work+Stations#Tablet-Options)
-   4 [Zebra Label Printer](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2321088513/Digital+Work+Stations#Zebra-Label-Printer)
-   5 [Scanner](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2321088513/Digital+Work+Stations#Scanner)
-   6 [Screen Recommendations](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2321088513/Digital+Work+Stations#Screen-Recommendations)
-   7 [Mobile Station Carts](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2321088513/Digital+Work+Stations#Mobile-Station-Carts) 
-   8 [UPS Power Supply](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2321088513/Digital+Work+Stations#UPS-Power-Supply) 

## Internet

Wireless or hard wired Internet will work for your shop. For Wi-fi ensure signal is strong in all areas of the shop. A stable, reliable, high-performing internet connection with adequate bandwidth and speed is perhaps the single most important key to success. 

## Software Needs

Stratus is running on your web browser so no special software is needed except your preferred internet browser. 

## Station Hardware Recommendations

## Mini Computer or Desktop Option

-   See System Requirements for specific details on recommended needs.
    
-   GTP has found the **KAMRUI GK3 Plus Mini PC 16GB RAM 512GB M.2 SSD, Intel 12th Alder Lake N95 (up to 3.4GHz) Micro PC, 2.5''SSD, Gigabit Ethernet, 4K UHD, WiFi, BT, VESA/Home/Business Mini Desktop Computer** to be a very reliable and low price point option for working in your shop.  
    
-   Dust Proof Keyboards are inexpensive and hold up well to the shop environment.
    
-   Corded or Wireless Mouse  
    

## Tablet Options

-   Surface Pro 7 or newer (standard with **TigerStop**) and recommended over iPads
    
    -   Surface Pro is widely used, however, only Surface Pro tablets with Intel processors are compatible with ZPL printers, whereas those with ARM CPUs are not.
        
    -   If using just the tablet we highly recommend using a mouse with the Surface Pro.
        
-   Apple iPad or iPad Pro 
    
    -   Note if choosing to use an iPad in the shop it is highly recommended that you also paid a mouse with the iPad for moving tags and dimensions.
        
-   Stylus Pen and keyboard (recommended)
    

## Zebra Label Printer

-   Windows is required to print labels using the Stratus Workstation and Stratus Print applications.
    
-   Recommended ZPL Printer
    
    -   **ZEBRA ZD421 Thermal Transfer Desktop Printer 203 dpi Print Width 4-inch USB ZD4A042-301M00EZ/**
        
    -   This printer offers both Thermal and Direct Thermal Printing options so it wins the GTP Stratus Customer Success stamp of approval. 
        
-   -   ZT410 - direct thermal printer 
        
    -   TLP2824 Plus - thermal transfer printer  
        
    -   ZT610 series - industrial 
        

## Scanner

To scan a tracking code, the scanner must be integrated with a computer. This is recommended for all work stations and logistics stations.

-   Industrial Grade Strength for a more durable scanner. 
    
    -   Alacrity Upgraded 2D Industrial Barcode Scanner
        
        -   Much more rugged for handling a shop environment. 
            

## Screen Recommendations

-   Mobile Stations - 43" +or- seems to be the sweet spot due to being closer to the screen while referencing Stratus. 
    
-   Wall Mounted Monitors - 60" monitors +or- seems to be the sweet spot here since these are typically mounted on the wall and above the work station 
    
-   4K monitors are recommended for a high resolution. 
    

## Mobile Station Carts 

Mobile Carts can be made out of any cart. We Have seen anything from Plastic Carts, Tool Chests and Nurse stands as mobile stations. The cost can range completely pending on your needs and desires. 

-   Perlegear Mobile TV Cart offers a great cart with a wide base for stability while keeping a low price point.
    

## UPS Power Supply 

Mobile Carts means the need for mobile power. With the low power draw from newer TV's and the mini computers do allow these to be smaller. Sizing these will be based on what hardware you are using and how long that will be away from shower power. Having these mounted to the bottom of a mobile station and cart also increases stability to your station.

Digital Work Station.pdf

# Error: User Journey Went Into A Bad State - STRATUS Knowledge Base - Confluence

> ## Excerpt
> 

---
[

![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/attachments/32771/global.logo?version=3&modificationDate=1516734801783&cacheVersion=1&api=v2)

](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/overview?homepageId=33347)

-   [
    
    All content
    
    ](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages)
-   [
    
    Space settings

Error: User Journey Went Into A Bad State

[Updated Apr 25](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/history/2853601284)

## Error: User Journey Went Into A Bad State

## ![thinking face](https://pf-emoji-service--cdn.us-east-1.prod.public.atl-paas.net/standard/ef8b0642-7523-4e13-9fd3-01b65648acf6/32x32/1f914.png) Problem

![image-20250425-142908.png](https://media-cdn.atlassian.com/file/8c0c0be9-e7d6-4bd3-a4fa-69b79f9e3801/image/cdn?allowAnimated=true&client=5f4a70b1-9d9d-47c3-b388-87235680bb54&collection=contentId-2853601284&height=660&max-age=2592000&mode=full-fit&source=mediaCard&token=eyJhbGciOiJIUzI1NiJ9.eyJpc3MiOiI1ZjRhNzBiMS05ZDlkLTQ3YzMtYjM4OC04NzIzNTY4MGJiNTQiLCJhY2Nlc3MiOnsidXJuOmZpbGVzdG9yZTpjb2xsZWN0aW9uOmNvbnRlbnRJZC0yODUzNjAxMjg0IjpbInJlYWQiXX0sImV4cCI6MTc1MDg2ODc4MCwibmJmIjoxNzUwODY1OTAwfQ.bgpKCgMXbAN69eArVTMr6sAies6VLl56RLsrawY7AJk&width=760)

This is caused by Azure ad caching an errant cookie.

Use this link to force a logout and the issue should resolve:  
[https://www.gtpstratus.com/MicrosoftIdentity/Account/Signout](https://www.gtpstratus.com/MicrosoftIdentity/Account/Signout "https://www.gtpstratus.com/MicrosoftIdentity/Account/Signout")

# Export / Import CSV Data - STRATUS Knowledge Base - Confluence

> ## Excerpt
> Q:     How can I export table data to CSV or Excel File Format.

---
> **Q:**     How can I export table data to CSV or Excel File Format. 
> 
> **A:**     Most data tables include a **CSV** button and an **Excel** button. The exported data will include “All” entries regardless of number selected in the Show entries drop-down list for the table.
> 
> **CSV** - The CSV button exports the data table to the CSV file format. If you intend to import data back into Stratus, the file will need to be saved as a CSV file.
> 
> **Excel** - The Excel exports the data table to an Excel file. If you intend to import data back into Stratus, the file will need to be saved as a CSV file.
> 
> To Export table data:
> 
> 1\. The **CSV** and **Excel** download data table buttons display on many Stratus pages. Notice that **Loaded entries** inform you how many rows have loaded out of how many entries will be loaded.

> 2a. If you click either the **CSV** or **Excel** download data table button before all entries have been loaded, the following message will display.

> 2b. **Generate** \- If the user clicks the **Generate** button, a partial file will download indicated with (Partial) in the file name.

2c. **Cancel** \- Click Cancel to wait for all data table records to load.

> 3\. The file will either download to your Downloads folder or you will be prompted for the output format.
> 
> 3a. **Open with** - To Open with, select **Open with** radio button with Excel selected regardless of which button was clicked. If the CSV button was clicked in Stratus, the file will open in the CSV file format. If the Excel button was clicked in Stratus, the file will open in the Excel file format.
> 
> 3b. **Save File** -To save the file, click the **Save File** radio button. If the CSV button was clicked in Stratus, the file will save in the CSV file format. If the Excel button was clicked in Stratus, the file will save in the Excel file format.

> **Q:** How can I Import CSV table data?
> 
> **A:**     While many data tables can exported, only a few include an **Import CSV** button.
> 
> Admin > Company > Containers
> 
> [**Packages > Dashboard**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/8749118/Packages+Dashboard#Import-Process "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/8749118/Packages+Dashboard#Import-Process")
> 
> Assemblies > Dashboard
> 
> **Containers Example: To export the Containers to CSV:**

1.  **Download the CSV file** - Click the **CSV** button. The CSV is downloaded and can be opened.
    
2.  **Edit Existing Data and Import** - To edit existing containers for import, edit any data value except Division and Id. All Names must be unique. When done Click the **Import CSV** button. In this example, the Name in the highlighted row was edited.
    
3.  **Add a New Row** - To add a new row:
    
    1.  Add the data and leave the Id blank.
        
    2.  Click **Import CSV**. The new rows will display.
        
    3.  Click the **CSV** button to export the table and the new rows will have been assigned an Id.
        
4.  **Duplicate Id** - Copy a row, change the Name to a unique value, but duplicate an Id.
    
    1.  The row will be imported, however it will replace the row that previously had the Id.
        
    2.  After clicking CSV to export, you’ll see that CSG \_ Pallet \_ 005 which had the duplicate Id was overwritten to CSG \_ Pallet \_ 006 and takes over the Id.
        
5.  **Duplicate a Name** - Duplicate a Name and Import. An error similar to the following will display.
---

# Fabrication Job issue creating MAJ or PCF files from the Packages Dashboard - STRATUS Knowledge Base - Confluence

> ## Excerpt
> Q:     What can be done about the Fabrication Job error received when I try to generate a MAJ or PCF file on the Packages Dashboard?

---
## Fabrication Job issue creating MAJ or PCF files from the Packages Dashboard

> **Q:**     What can be done about the Fabrication Job error received when I try to generate a MAJ or PCF file on the Packages Dashboard?
> 
> ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/attachments/246153241/image2019-7-2_14-30-53.png?version=1&modificationDate=1562095854634&cacheVersion=1&api=v2)
> 
> **A:** A Fabrication Job error similar to the one above occurs when files are being created and the Fabrication dll displays "Oversized Parts" dialog popup for oversized patterns (below). The problem is that the files are created on the STRATUS server and users cannot interact with the dialogs.  Autodesk will update the Fabrication dll to supress popup dialogs like these in an upcoming release. Below is a work around until this release is made.
> 
> ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/246153241/image2019-7-2_14-51-23.png?version=1&modificationDate=1562097085655&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=489&height=250)
> 
> To work around this issue, modify your Fabrication Database and republish the model as follows:
> 
> 1.  Open the Fabrication database that the model is using with CADmep, ESTmep or CAMduct.
>     
> 2.  Select to the Manufacturing tab and ensure "Automatically use these setting without prompting" is check On.  
>     ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/246153241/image2019-7-2_14-56-54.png?version=1&modificationDate=1562097416168&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=612&height=489)  
>     
> 3.  Select **OK** to save the changes,
> 4.  Follow publish instructions for your environment:
>     1.  If in AutoCAD CADmep re-publish the model.
>     2.  If the model is in Revit, reload the fabrication database into the model by selecting "Settings" and "Reload Configuration".  
>         ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/246153241/image2019-7-2_15-0-41.png?version=1&modificationDate=1562097642861&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=638&height=583)
>         1.  Once the database is reloaded into the model, re-publish to STRATUS. Re-publish is needed as the ESJ contains a snapshot of the fabrication database.
>             
>         2.  You should now be able to create the output files from the Packages Dashboard without the error.
>
---

# HGG ProCAM - STRATUS Knowledge Base - Confluence

> ## Excerpt
> There are two pieces of the HGG software: the controller software directly connected to the HGG machine (UPC), and then the software running on a separate PC. This article is concerned with the second piece of software, HGG ProCAM.

---
## Stratus Linked to HGG ProCAM

There are two pieces of the HGG software: the controller software directly connected to the HGG machine (UPC), and then the software running on a separate PC. This article is concerned with the second piece of software, HGG ProCAM.

## Get a Key for HGG to Talk to Stratus

Before HGG ProCAM can communicate with Stratus, you will need to create an access key in Stratus that is entered into HGG ProCAM. To do this, in Stratus, go to Admin > Company > AppKeys

To create a new App Key for use with HGG set the Partner App to “HGG ProCAM”, and pick a Run as User who elevated rights. The **Key** is the value pointed to by the red arrow below:

This value will be entered into HGG ProCAM.

Your physical HGG machine must be associated with a Tool and a Station in Stratus. To create a tool in Stratus, go to Admin > Company > Tools. See the [**Tools**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/215220225 "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/215220225") article for more information. Below is an example. 

After creating a tool, you will need to create a Station. To do that, go to Stratus > Admin > Stations, and create a new HGG station that you associate with the tool earlier created.

## Configure Pipe Cuts

Configuration of HGG output relies on Admin > Company > Pipe Cuts settings, where the company's o-let hole sizes, connector bevel angles, etc. are entered. See the [**Pipe Cuts**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/201490457 "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/201490457") article for more information.

## Configure Cut List Mappings 

A Cut List Mappings for each Part Template must be configured to tell Stratus which data fields to use.

**To configure a Cut List Mapping:** 

1.  Got to Admin > Company > Part Templates. 
    
2.  In the Parts section, select or search for Part Template Name.  
    
    1.  **Hint**:  To determine a Part Template Name, in any Stratus viewer, open the Properties tool, select the part, and then locate the Template Name.  
        
        ![](blob:https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/d4750862-c821-44e5-9938-882edf3cf710)
        
3.  **Select** the Part Template and then click the **Cut List Mappings** tab.   
    
    ![](blob:https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/e04c7108-af95-42c3-a0c6-ead08c248258)
    
4.  In the **Consider for Multi-Axis Cut Lists** section, select a part parameter from your database that contains the data for each field. The parameters that need to be selected will vary depending the type of part selected. 
    
    1.  **Straight Pipe** fields:  
        
        ![](blob:https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/a19bbf22-33c1-4a54-a96d-88d45155a1f6)
        
    2.  **Saddle** fields:  
        
        ![](blob:https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/be2d883a-6005-49e7-99fb-f0fd06483afe)
        
    3.  **Revit Family Content - Pipes Pipe Type (No Fabrication Content)**   
        **Create Project Parameters (Required)**  
        Stratus uses the Revit API to extract data from the model. Diameter and Pipe End Connector parameters must be defined in Revit as a project parameter so that the data can be injected into the part. The project parameter tells Stratus where to look for the parameter in your model.
        
        1.  Stratus uses the Inside and Outside Diameter.  
            
            ![](blob:https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/b9e2f1c9-a582-4f64-bb89-7dcf20637cfd)
            
        2.  Companies need to map a project parameter to the Segment and Sizes.  
            
            ![](blob:https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/4c8af707-fe1b-4a96-92a1-298ff80d96da)
            
    4.  **Revit Family Content – Shaped Nipple**   
        The Shaped Nipple is similar to the Pipes Pipe Type but an Olet Type also needs to be selected.  
        
        ![](blob:https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/3cbf982e-4ecc-432a-baee-502ca28877f5)
        

## Generate a .HGG output file

To generate a .HGG file: 

1.  Open a package that includes straight pipe along with Connectors, Saddles, or Olets. 
    
2.  With the package open, click the **Cut Lists** tab.  
    
3.  To enable the **Generate Cut List** button, check that the package is set with a “**Can Cut List**” tracking status. See the [**Tracking Statuses (Admin)**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/10485761 "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/10485761") article for more information.
    
4.  Click the **Generate Cut List** button.  
    
5.  The cut list will display.  
    
    ![](blob:https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/75cadbdd-2bff-4aae-8f04-f4139123d43a)
    
    1.  For each cut list row that will be sent to a HGG ProCAM cutting machine, select the correct **Station.**  See the [**Station (Admin)**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/215220408 "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/215220408") article for more information.
        
    2.  Check the rows that will be sent to the station. 
        
    3.  Click the **Send Cut List to Station** button. 
        
    4.  Click **OK** on the Send Cut Lists dialog box.
        
6.  Cut List files are organized under the **Shops** tab.  
    
7.  On the Shops > Dashboard, select the **Shop.** A list of Stations for the Shop display.   
    
    ![](blob:https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/51a4287b-bba2-4a1f-b6cf-053b76c1a9c6)
    
8.  Click the **Station** name and a list of requested cut lists will display.
    
9.  Click the **Send to Tool** button associated with the Cut List. A HGG file will be created for each material-diameter combination.    
    
    ![](blob:https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/74bd35a8-bee1-4f2a-86f9-ca9f12a6be2b)
    
10.  The .HGG file will be a downloaded by your web browser.
    
11.  The Job Value in the .HGG file with the Stratus Package Name.  
    
    ![](blob:https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/e7d20dc5-f517-4b58-9c23-38d452245963)
    
    **How to use the .HGG file**
    
12.  Locate the downloaded .HGG  file and save it to a location that can be used by the HGG ProCAM software. 
    
13.  The CAD department loads the .HGG file into the HGG ProCAM software. 
    
14.  HGG ProCAM's tools can be used to prepare the pipe to be cut. 
    
15.  Auto-nest the cut list and HGG ProCAM will optimize nesting. 
    
16.  When ready the operator starts the cutting tool. 
    

## Generate a .HGG File after Using Spool Checker

When using Spool Checker under Assemblies > Assembly > Spool Checker Tool, modifications at either end of the pipe will be reconciled with relative dimensional references. For the initiated, lengths can be affected at either the C1 or C2 end. This means that length will be taken up or given on the correct end of the pipe depending on the locked part scenario you are dealing with in the Spool Checker. This delivers feature parity to ITM and Revit pipe for multi-axis pipe cut file generation.

You can see 2” being taken off of either end of what was originally a 60” part in the screenshots below:

## Stratus OpenAPI

For information about how to integrate the [**Stratus OpenAPI**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/1829077164 "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/1829077164") with HGG ProCAM, please contact the [**Stratus Service Desk**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/servicedesk/customer/portal/3 "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/servicedesk/customer/portal/3")**.**

# How to Fix Fabrication Parts that have Duplicate ID's - STRATUS Knowledge Base - Confluence

> ## Excerpt
> Autodesk Revit - STRATUS customers are receiving emails with models identified as having duplicate Fabrication IDs and requiring fixes prior to March 14th.

---
### **\* ALERT \* - Starting with STRATUS v7 release around March 14th, 2024, duplicate Fabrication IDs in Revit models will prevent model publishing.**

**Autodesk Revit - STRATUS customers are receiving emails with models identified as having duplicate Fabrication IDs and requiring fixes prior to March 14th.**

#### **What can you do???**

-   **For Revit 2021 and newer,** be sure to apply all available software updates from Autodesk and make sure you are at least on the versions as indicated in the support article **[Autodesk Support Notes](https://url.avanan.click/v2/___https:/www.autodesk.com/support/technical/article/caas/sfdcarticles/sfdcarticles/Duplicate-GUIDs-are-created-on-fabrication-elements-in-Revit.html___.YXAzOmdvZ3RwOmE6bzpmOTY2MTI1YThlYzM1MjJjOWE5MTFmOGQzOTNjNjUxNTo2OjRmZGQ6NWI1YjdlOTFmOTZlMjRlNWM1MzFjOGRiNjc1YmY3ZmM0OTEyMGQ4NjViMTk1ZDU1ZTEwNzQ0YzRlYTg1MWQ5MjpoOlQ)**, Once done, AUDIT your Revit projects.  The AUDIT command has been enhanced to fix duplicate Fabrication IDs. 
-   **For Revit versions older than 2019 and 2020**, upgrade to the latest patched version. Before contacting [Autodesk support](https://www.autodesk.com/support/contact-support) to request assistance with resolving the duplicate IDs issue in your Revit project, users should fix their ITM files, otherwise the issue will be re-occur. 

**[Autodesk Support Notes](https://www.autodesk.com/support/technical/article/caas/sfdcarticles/sfdcarticles/Duplicate-GUIDs-are-created-on-fabrication-elements-in-Revit.html)**

**IMPORTANT CONSIDERATION**

For customers that used the settings change in the settings.json file for STRATUS to override the publish behavior currently to allow publishing of duplicate IDs, you may wish to undo that change on each computer for users who publish models to STRATUS.  This will ensure you catch models with duplicate IDs prior to the v7 release.  Once v7 is released, this override will no longer be used.

·         Open the Windows File Explorer

·         Enter **%appdata%** into the path bar and hit the enter/return key

·         Navigate to the GTP Software Inc folder and open it

·         Navigate to the STRATUS folder

·         Open the settings.json file in notepad

·         Set the following setting to **false** if it exists (if not, you can leave this file alone)

o   “AllowFabPartsWithDuplicateGuidsToPublish”: true

·         Save the file and close it

**Q:**    Can parts in Revit and CADmep models have duplicate ID's for Fabrication Parts?

**A:**    Yes, both Revit and CADmep models can have duplicate ID's for Fabrication Parts. Models that will be used for fabrication cannot include duplicate Id's, so the issue must fixed. Below there is a Q and A for resolving the issue in Revit and a separate Q and A to resolve the issue in CADmep. 

**Q:** Can a **Revit** model include duplicate Id's or duplicate UniqueId's?

**A:** Yes.  A defect existed in Revit that allowed multiple Fabrication Parts to share the same UniqueId in the model which could break downstream workflows such as creating Package MAJ or PCF files leading to missing or incorrect parts in the Fabrication file. The defect was patched in Revit 2019.2.2, 2020.1, 2021 and later versions to prevent the creation of duplicates, unfortunately there was no automated way provided to fix existing instances of duplicates in models. If a model that was originally authored in an affected version of Revit is upgraded to a newer version that does not contain the defect, the duplicates will unfortunately still exist. To ensure STRATUS is working with validated models this release introduces a check during STRATUS publish to ensure the model does not contain duplicates.

Autodesk has identified additional ways a duplicate GUID can be generated. GTP is working with Autodesk on more flexible ways to correct issues like this in future releases of supported Revit versions.

1.  **GUID may be stored on the ITM** - Some STRATUS customers have noted that their project started with Revit 2022 or later, after the defect was patched, yet they are still having duplicate GUIDs in their published models. Autodesk just informed GTP that the a **duplicate GUID may be stored on the ITM** itself, which results in new instances of those parts being created having that ID. 
    
    1.  **Resolution:** For version 2021-2024, see the support article **[Autodesk Support Notes](https://url.avanan.click/v2/___https:/www.autodesk.com/support/technical/article/caas/sfdcarticles/sfdcarticles/Duplicate-GUIDs-are-created-on-fabrication-elements-in-Revit.html___.YXAzOmdvZ3RwOmE6bzpmOTY2MTI1YThlYzM1MjJjOWE5MTFmOGQzOTNjNjUxNTo2OjRmZGQ6NWI1YjdlOTFmOTZlMjRlNWM1MzFjOGRiNjc1YmY3ZmM0OTEyMGQ4NjViMTk1ZDU1ZTEwNzQ0YzRlYTg1MWQ5MjpoOlQ).**
        
2.  **Revit Type Selector** - A certain sequence of steps with the **Revit Type Selector** can also result in duplicates and sets the GUID to 00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000.
    
    1.  **Resolution**:
        
        1.  For version 2021-2024, see the support article **[Autodesk Support Notes](https://url.avanan.click/v2/___https:/www.autodesk.com/support/technical/article/caas/sfdcarticles/sfdcarticles/Duplicate-GUIDs-are-created-on-fabrication-elements-in-Revit.html___.YXAzOmdvZ3RwOmE6bzpmOTY2MTI1YThlYzM1MjJjOWE5MTFmOGQzOTNjNjUxNTo2OjRmZGQ6NWI1YjdlOTFmOTZlMjRlNWM1MzFjOGRiNjc1YmY3ZmM0OTEyMGQ4NjViMTk1ZDU1ZTEwNzQ0YzRlYTg1MWQ5MjpoOlQ).**
        2.  GTP has provided a macro to address the affected parts. See section 3. Detect Duplicate UniqueIds Using a Revit Module
            
3.  **Moving/Copying parts** – **Moving/Copying parts** caused duplicated GUIDs
    
    1.  **Resolutions:** A fix was released for 2019 through current versions. See the support article **[Autodesk Support Notes](https://url.avanan.click/v2/___https:/www.autodesk.com/support/technical/article/caas/sfdcarticles/sfdcarticles/Duplicate-GUIDs-are-created-on-fabrication-elements-in-Revit.html___.YXAzOmdvZ3RwOmE6bzpmOTY2MTI1YThlYzM1MjJjOWE5MTFmOGQzOTNjNjUxNTo2OjRmZGQ6NWI1YjdlOTFmOTZlMjRlNWM1MzFjOGRiNjc1YmY3ZmM0OTEyMGQ4NjViMTk1ZDU1ZTEwNzQ0YzRlYTg1MWQ5MjpoOlQ).**
        

**STRATUS Message When Duplicate GUID Detected**

Starting on 5/4/23 with release 6.2.189, if any duplicates are detected the publish process will be aborted with a message similar to the following. 

![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/attachments/269680683/image2023-5-5_11-17-18.png?version=1&modificationDate=1683303439577&cacheVersion=1&api=v2)

**Resolutions and Work Arounds**

If duplicates are detected, there are 3 options:

#### 1\. Deduplicate the ElementIds in the Revit model and Publish the Model

1.  After receiving the cancel publish message (above), review the latest Revit publish log file at: **%appdata%/GTP STRATUS Logs/Revit**
    
2.  Copy the ElementIds from the log file and paste them into the Revit model using the “Select by ID” tool.
    
3.  Deduplicate (delete and redraw) each ElementId. A new Id will be associated with the new part. **Note**: Some situations require extra steps to ensure that connected parts are not redrawn which could cause additional problems. One scenario where extra editing steps should be taken is the case where a part like an elbow is connected with a weld on one end, and a pair of flanges on the other, and the elbow’s PartGuid needs to be deduplicated, but the weld and flanges PartGuids are unique, and they are already part of a package or in a workflow where those elements should not have their PartGuid values modified. In this case, the following general steps can be followed to deduplicate the elbow or similar part:
    
    1.  Store the part's rotation / orientation, and the the ID of the parts(s) it is connected to.
        
    2.  Pin the elements it is connected to.
        
    3.  Cut the element.
        
    4.  Paste the element.
        
    5.  For each connection, reconnect. Verify that the orientation is correct.
        
    6.  Unpin the elements pinned previously.
        
4.  Save and republish the model when done.
    

Below is an example of a **GTP STRATUS Log** that includes ElementId’s.![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/attachments/269680683/image2023-5-5_11-20-1.png?version=1&modificationDate=1683303602415&cacheVersion=1&api=v2)

#### 2\. Continue Publishing with Duplicates (Temporary)

For customers who temporarily accept duplicate UniqueIds, the .json publish configuration can be modified to allow Fab parts with Duplicate Ids to be published. This pathway will be eliminated in a future release in Q3 of 23'.

1.  Open settings.json at: **%appdata%/GTP Software Inc/STRATUS**
    
2.  Modify the file by adding the line "AllowFabPartsWithDuplicateGuidsToPublish": true as shown below. **Note**: The lines in your file might be different. Make sure you add a comma to the preceding line Ex… after the “Warning”):  
    "RemoteMinimumLogLevel": "Warning",  
    "AllowFabPartsWithDuplicateGuidsToPublish": true
    
3.  Publish the model. The existing MAJ or PCF file issues will continue.
    

#### 3\. Detect Duplicate UniqueIds Using a Revit Module

Separate from the duplicate UniqueId detection built-in to the STRATUS Addin, duplicate UniqueIds can be detected by running the application macro module below.

_**Update 5/12/23**_

1.  To create and use a Revit duplicate GUIDs Application Module, in STRATUS go to Help > Downloads and click the [**DuplicationCheck**](https://update.gtp.one/downloads/DuplicationCheck.zip "https://update.gtp.one/downloads/DuplicationCheck.zip") link.
    
    1.  **Note: If you downloaded the DuplicationCheck.zip file prior to 5/12/23 at 8:00AM CT, please delete it and download again as it has been edited.**
        
2.  Unzip and open the file. This is a .txt file that will be used to create an **Application Macro** in Revit so that duplicate GUID detection can be run in any Revit model.
    
3.  Open any Revit project.
    
4.  **To Create a New Module** - In Revit click Manage > Macro Manager > Application tab > Module and then paste the name **DuplicationCheck** for the Module name.
    
    ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/attachments/269680683/image2023-5-10_8-4-54.png?version=1&modificationDate=1683723895725&cacheVersion=1&api=v2)
    
5.  Click **OK**.
    
6.  The Module will display.
    
    ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/attachments/269680683/image2023-5-10_8-5-31.png?version=1&modificationDate=1683723933020&cacheVersion=1&api=v2)
    
7.  In addition, a separate window similar to the following will open. Close this window.
    
    ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/attachments/269680683/image2023-5-10_8-5-56.png?version=1&modificationDate=1683723957707&cacheVersion=1&api=v2)
    
8.  **To Create a New Macro** - Within the Macro Manager with the DuplicationCheck Module highlighted, click **Macro** button and then enter the same name, **DuplicationCheck** for the Macro name.
    
    ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/attachments/269680683/image2023-5-10_8-6-27.png?version=1&modificationDate=1683723988328&cacheVersion=1&api=v2)
    
9.  Click **OK**.
    
10.  A separate window similar to the following will open. Highlight everything and delete.
    
    ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/attachments/269680683/image2023-5-10_8-6-47.png?version=1&modificationDate=1683724009192&cacheVersion=1&api=v2)
    
11.  With the [**DuplicationCheck**](https://update.gtp.one/downloads/DuplicationCheck.zip "https://update.gtp.one/downloads/DuplicationCheck.zip") file downloaded, unzipped, and opened from step #1, copy all of the text.
    
    ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/attachments/269680683/image2023-5-10_8-14-46.png?version=1&modificationDate=1683724488223&cacheVersion=1&api=v2)
    
12.  Paste the text it into the Macro in step #10.
    
    ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/attachments/269680683/image2023-5-12_12-23-11.png?version=1&modificationDate=1683912192872&cacheVersion=1&api=v2)
    
13.  Click **Build** > **Build Solution**.
    
    ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/attachments/269680683/image2023-5-10_8-15-35.png?version=1&modificationDate=1683724536534&cacheVersion=1&api=v2)
    

15.  To run the DuplicationCheck macro on any Revit project, click Manage > Macro Manager > Application tab > Expand the DuplicationCheck Module in the Macros column > Select the DuplicationCheck Macro > click **Run**.
    
    ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/attachments/269680683/image2023-5-12_13-55-0.png?version=1&modificationDate=1683917701265&cacheVersion=1&api=v2)
    
16.  When no duplicates GUIDs are found , the following will display.
    
    ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/attachments/269680683/image2023-5-12_12-47-49.png?version=1&modificationDate=1683913670844&cacheVersion=1&api=v2)
    
17.  When duplicate GUIDs are found a message similar to the following will display.
    
18.  Once it is done, save or save as the project.
    
19.  If you re-run the DuplicationCheck macro, a message similar to the following will display depending on what kind of duplicate GUIDs were in the model.  
    ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/attachments/269680683/image2023-5-12_12-49-3.png?version=1&modificationDate=1683913744802&cacheVersion=1&api=v2)
    

**Q:**     Can a **CADmep** model include duplicate Id's?  And after selecting a part with the Properties panel open, why does the message "No data available in tabled" display?

![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/attachments/269680683/image2023-5-5_11-11-13.png?version=1&modificationDate=1683303074495&cacheVersion=1&api=v2)

**A:** The issue is caused by duplicate Id's in the CADmep model. During the STRATUS publish process, Duplicate ID’s are filtered out so no data is published and no data will display under Properties.

To fix this issue in your authoring software, copy and replace the objects in AutoCAD to generate a new UniqueId.

**To copy ALL the CADmep objects in the drawing.**

1.  Type **MAPFILTER**
2.  When prompted, type **ALL** and **Enter**.
3.  When the dialog is displayed, select **Cancel**, this will create a selection set containing all the CADmep objects.
4.  Type **Copy**, when prompted type **P** for **Previous** then press **Enter**
5.  When prompted for a base point type **0,0,0** and press **Enter**
6.  When prompted for second point type **0,0,0** and press **Enter**
7.  Press **Enter** to Exit the command.
8.  A copy of all the CADmep objects has now been made.
9.  Type **E** for **Erase** and press **Enter**
10.  Type **P** for **Previous**, press **Enter** and **Enter** again to finish the command, this will erase the original selection set, i.e. the objects selected to copy, and you are left with the copied objects which all have new UniqueIds.

**To copy ONLY CADmep objects with duplicated IDs in the drawing**

First you'll need to identify which objects have the duplicated IDs, to do this use the Select Filter command to manually identify.

1.  Type **SelectFilter** and **Enter,** when prompted type **All** and **Enter**
2.  Configure the **Columns** to contain the **Item Globally Unique ID** by selecting the **Columns** button and adding the field to the right and press **OK**.  
    ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/269680683/image2019-12-4_9-39-9.png?version=1&modificationDate=1575473951455&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=739&height=420)
3.  Select all the entries in the dialog (highlight one entry and press **Ctrl A**)
4.  **Uncheck** the check box for one entry and all will entries will uncheck.
5.  Click on the **Item Globally Unique ID** column heading so that the entries are sorted and that the ones with duplications will be next to each other.
6.  Scan the list looking for duplications and **check** one of each duplicated entry.  
    ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/269680683/image2019-12-4_9-40-32.png?version=1&modificationDate=1575474035098&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=739&height=416)
7.  Once all entries have been identified and selected, press **OK** on the dialog. The entries will now be highlighted in the model.
8.  With the objects selected type **MASKVIEW** and **Enter**, this will isolate all the selected objects.
9.  You can now make a **Copy** of these by following from **Step 4** as detailed above.
10.  Type **SHOWALL** and **Enter** to restore the display of all the CADmep objects.

# IP Addresses for Allow Lists - STRATUS Knowledge Base - Confluence

> ## Excerpt
> In most cases you should not need to configure an allow list for GTP Services. However, if you’re having issues with connectivity to some GTP Services you should add the following IPs to your firewall allow list. We’ve included IPs for GTP Services as well as those used for our service provider Microsoft Azure. In all cases we use a minimum of TLS 1.2 and port 443.

---
In most cases you should not need to configure an allow list for GTP Services. However, if you’re having issues with connectivity to some GTP Services you should add the following IPs to your firewall allow list. We’ve included IPs for GTP Services as well as those used for our service provider Microsoft Azure. In all cases we use a minimum of TLS 1.2 and port 443.

## Inbound Calls

When you are connecting to our services the following IP addresses can be used:

### Stratus

128.203.150.82

### Microsoft Azure

20.40.229.4/32

## Outbound Responses

When you are receiving a response from our services the following IP addresses can be used:

### Stratus

128.203.150.82/32

20.12.134.48/28

172.168.16.48/28

### Microsoft Azure

20.40.229.4/32

> ## Excerpt
> A: Use the ZPL Label Preview while editing the label content.

-   2 [Q: Is there a webinar on configuring ZPL labels and Stratus reports?](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/157974545/Label+Printing+for+Zebra+ZPL+Compatible+Printers#Q%3A-Is-there-a-webinar-on-configuring-ZPL-labels-and-Stratus-reports%3F)

-   5 [Q: How can the TigerStop label include the next part in the spool?](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/157974545/Label+Printing+for+Zebra+ZPL+Compatible+Printers#Q%3A-How-can-the-TigerStop-label-include-the-next-part-in-the-spool%3F)

-   12 [Q: Is there a way to print labels using a sort order?](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/157974545/Label+Printing+for+Zebra+ZPL+Compatible+Printers#Q%3A-Is-there-a-way-to-print-labels-using-a-sort-order%3F) 

## **Q:** What is the best way to define label content?

**A:** Use the ZPL Label Preview while editing the label content.

1.  To edit a label under either:
    
    1.  Admin > Company > Tools > Label Template
        
    2.  Admin > Company > Report > Label Template
        
2.  Click the **Edit Label Template** button. A “Label Template for” dialog similar to the following will display.
    
    1.  **Print Density** and **Label Size** should match the target printer's settings in order to the preview how the printed label will display.
        
        1.  **Print Density** - Select the dpi to be used for the label.
            
        2.  **Label Size** - Enter the dimensions of the target label.
            
    2.  **Edit dialog (left)** - Enter the ZPL into the edit dialog.
        
    3.  **Preview dialog (right)** - Edit will immediately display in the preview panel.
        
3.  When done editing the ZPL, click **Save**.
    

## **Q:** Is there a webinar on configuring ZPL labels and Stratus reports?

**A:**   Yes.

**02/18/2021 CSG Webinar: Advanced Label Creation**

**07/11/2019 - Configure ZPL Labels: TigerStop ZPL and Stratus Report ZPL**.

<iframe allowfullscreen="" allowtransparency="true" data-hasbody="false" data-layout="default" data-local-id="11e09740-125f-4eef-95f7-e7d3178b9cf2" data-macro-id="6e2fab94-c151-4dbe-b15f-455a20a980e2" data-macro-name="widget" frameborder="0" height="364" mozallowfullscreen="" webkitallowfullscreen="" width="640" src="https://player.vimeo.com/video/348253844?h=embed"></iframe>

## **Q:** Where can I download the Stratus Print application?

**A:**   Download and install the [**Stratus Print**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2121400321 "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2121400321") application.

## **Q:** What are the steps to print to a Zebra (ZPL) compatible printer?

**A:**   Stratus provides the ability to print labels with a Zebra printer for non-TigerStop cut lists like PypeServer and T-Drill.

1.  Check that you have the latest [**Zebra Setup Utilities for Windows**](https://www.zebra.com/us/en/support-downloads/printer-software/printer-setup-utilities.html#featureforoperatings "https://www.zebra.com/us/en/support-downloads/printer-software/printer-setup-utilities.html#featureforoperatings").
    
2.  To print labels using a ZPL label printer, download and install the [**Stratus Print**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2121400321 "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2121400321") application.
    
3.  Create a printer tool under **Admin** > **Company** > **Tools** and select the **ZPL printer** as the tool type.
    
    1.  You may need to **Edit the Label Template** to configure the label fields. If so, please submit a  [**Stratus Service Desk**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/servicedesk/customer/portal/3 "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/servicedesk/customer/portal/3") request. 
        
    2.  Example Label Fields, depending on your database, might include any of the following case sentitive fields.  
        Note: Not all of these fields are available for labels using the workflow. See [**Import Mapping**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/170196993 "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/170196993") article for more information.
        
        -   **area**  
            **areaPath - includes the full BIM Area tree description with (e.g. Root | Level | Area).**   
            **assemblyId**  
            **assemblyName**  
            **cadId**  
            **description**  
            **fitting1**  
            **fitting2**  
            **index**  
            **itemNumber**  
            **length**  
            **lengthInInches** \- This label field reports the length plus the Spool Checker adjustment  
            **lengthInFeetAndInches** \- This label field reports the length plus the Spool Checker adjustment  
            **level**  
            **material**  
            **modelId**  
            **modelName**  
            **packageId**  
            **packageName**  
            **packageNumber**  
            **projectId**  
            **projectName**  
            **projectNumber**  
            **qrCodeUrl - This code pulls the part QR code for non-assembled parts and the assembly QR code for assembled parts.**  
            **Stratus.Part.HoleInfo - Note: Content can be lengthy and there may not be an easy word wrap option. See this non-Stratus article** [**Creating a ZebraDesigner Field that will wrap text**](https://www.zebra.com/us/en/support-downloads/knowledge-articles/ait/creating-a-zebradesigner-field-that-will-wrap-text.html "https://www.zebra.com/us/en/support-downloads/knowledge-articles/ait/creating-a-zebradesigner-field-that-will-wrap-text.html") **for more information.**  
            **size**  
            **user**  
            **userData1**  
            **userData2**
            
    3.  To print labels:
        
        1.  Launch the **Stratus Print** application.
            
            1.  The first time **Stratus Print** is used, configure it by clicking **Settings** and then select the **Company**, **Tool**, and **Label Printer**.
                
            2.  The Print Workstation application needs to be open whenever you want to print labels but can be minimized. Don’t worry if it is not opened when you send labels to be printed; the application will queue all requests and then print as soon as **Stratus Print** has been opened.
                
    4.  You can print PypeServer/3DPP cut list labels from the Package Cut List Page:
        
    5.  1.  **Define and Generate a Package Cut List.** For information on how to define a Package and Generate a Cut List, see the [**Package Cut Lists**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/166723746 "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/166723746") article in the Stratus Knowledge Base.
            
        2.  Once a package cut list has been generated it will display on the **Packages** > **Package** > **Cut Lists** page. You can print labels from this page by clicking the **Print Labels** button**. Note**: The defined Station for this cut list is the PypeServer Station and not a station that handles TigerStop cut lists.
            
        3.  The Select Printer Tool dialog will display. This is the label printer tool defined under **Admin** > **Company** > **Tools**. Select your label printer and click **OK**.
            
        4.  The labels will print. Below is an example. **Note**: The label print order does not currently synch with the item order in the cut list. 
            
    6.  You can also print labels from the **Shops Tool** page:
        
        1.  To print labels from the Shops Tool page, you’ll need to send the cut list to the Shop Station by checking the cut list and then clicking the **Send Cut List to Station** button on the **Packages** > **Cut Lists** > **Cut List** page.
            
        2.  Once the **Send Cut List to Station** button is clicked, you can locate the cut list under **Shops > Shop** (Ex. PyerServer Station) **> Tool** (the ZPL printer tool defined above) **> Queued Items rows >** click the **Print Labels** button.
            
        3.  The Select Printer Tool dialog will display. This is the label printer tool defined under Admin > Company > Tools. Select your label printer and click **OK**.
            
        4.  The labels will print. Below is an example. Note: The label print order is not currently synched with the items in the cut list.
            
    7.  You can also:
        
        1.  define a label report under **Admin** > **Company** > **Reports** where **Format = ZPL** and check the **Package Viewer checkbox**.
            
        2.  These label reports can be run under **Packages** > **Viewer** > **Actions** > **Reports**.
            

## Q: How can the TigerStop label include the next part in the spool?

A: This feature works when the assembly has two parts in it: a straight pipe segment to be cut and a pipe fitting to put on the end of the cut pipe.  To configure, add the **fitting1** field to your **Admin > Company > Tools > Tool > Label Template**. Send the cut list to the TigerStop tool. When the straight pipe is cut the next part will display. Below is an example where FTG is the label for the next part:   

![](blob:https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/da4e0659-723a-4c08-8f01-483110c463d3)

## Q: What Label Fields can be included on a ZPL label?

A: Depending on your database, the following case sensitive fields are available.   
Note: Not all of these fields are available for labels using the workflow. See [**Import Mapping**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/170196993 "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/170196993") article for more information.

  
**area**  
**assemblyId**  
**assemblyName**  
**cadId**  
**description**  
**fitting1**  
**itemNumber**  
**length**  
**lengthInFeetAndInches**  
**level**  
**material**  
**modelId**  
**modelName**  
**packagerId**  
**packageName**  
**projectId**  
**projectName**  
**projectNumber**  
**qrCodeUrl**  
**size**  
**user**

## Q: How can the ZPL code be tested without printing a label?

A: 

1.  Under either:
    
    1.  Admin > Company > Tools > Label Template
        
    2.  Admin > Company > Report > Label Template
        
2.  Click the **Edit Label Template** button. A “Label Template for” dialog similar to the following will display.
    
3.  **Print Density** and **Label Size** should match the target printer's settings in order to the preview how the printed label will display.
    
    1.  **Print Density** - Select the dpi to be used for the label.
        
    2.  **Label Size** - Enter the dimensions of the target label.
        
4.  **Edit dialog (left)** - Enter the ZPL into the edit dialog.
    
5.  **Preview dialog (right)** - Edit will immediately display in the preview panel.
    
6.  When done editing the ZPL, click **Save**.
    

## **Q:** Is there a way to print labels for connected assemblies? 

**A:**   Yes, see the Stratus.Assembly.Connected Property section in the [**Reports (Admin)**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/10617393 "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/10617393") article.

## **Q:** Is there a way to cancel a print?

**A:**   Yes, cancel the print job in the Windows print queue for the ZPL printer.  

![](blob:https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/c3abf675-09b8-4f4e-916e-c4f01b9c1461)

## **Q:** Is there a way to print labels with special characters? 

**A:**   Yes.

It is going to take some refactoring of your label template code. Please see the forum here for background: [Print characters with an acute in ZPL](https://stackoverflow.com/questions/29437279/print-characters-with-an-acute-in-zpl "https://stackoverflow.com/questions/29437279/print-characters-with-an-acute-in-zpl")

Now the quick and dirty is to just add a “^CI28” to the top of your label template code to tell it to reference UTF-8 encoding.

Here is what it looks like when you do not use the ^CI28 line when there is an Ø in the label text in the size row as well as a value of one referenced description field :

And here when you do:

## **Q:** What Label Printer, Label Stock, and Scanner is recommended? 

## **Q:** Is there a way to print labels using a sort order? 

**A:**   Yes. To control the order of labels printed in a ZPL report:

1.  Create or use a Stratus.Field.x that will be used to designate the sort order where it's Data Type = Integer and Default Value = Empty.
    
2.  Add the  Stratus.Field.x field to a dashboard report where the it can be populated with sort order values.
    
3.  Add the  Stratus.Field.x field to a ZPL report and set its Sort Index = 1.

# Labels, ZPL Printers, Codes, Troubleshooting and Configuration - STRATUS Knowledge Base - Confluence

> ## Excerpt
> If you get the following error, you will need to clear out your cookies by deleting this directory:

---
## **Printing Labels Troubleshooting Steps**

If you get the following error, you will need to clear out your cookies by deleting this directory:

C:\\Users\\\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\\AppData\\Roaming\\EBWebView

where \_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_ is the Windows user name.

## Common Configuration Problems

If your the ZPL won't print, consider the following steps:

1.  Make sure in Windows Settings Printers, that your ZPL is your default printer (go to step [Default Printer](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/edit-v2/2132574209#Set-as-Default-Printer "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/edit-v2/2132574209#Set-as-Default-Printer") Step [4](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/edit-v2/2132574209#Set-as-Default-Printer "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/edit-v2/2132574209#Set-as-Default-Printer") below)
    
2.  If you installed your ZPL printer directly from Windows, it won't work. In that case, uninstall and reinstall as per the following steps.
    
3.  Reinstall as Needed
    
    1.  Start and Stop your Print Spooler under Task Manager > Services.
        
    2.  Right click (or long-press on tablet) and stop, then start this service.
        
    3.  Install the ZPL Setup Utility. [https://www.zebra.com/us/en/support-downloads/printer-software/printer-setup-utilities.html](https://www.zebra.com/us/en/support-downloads/printer-software/printer-setup-utilities.html)
        
    4.  Install your ZPL printer drives from the Zebra Setup Utility.
        
        1.  In Windows under Printers (see image below):
            
        2.  Uninstall your ZPL printer.
            
        3.  Then, using the Zebra Setup Utility, reinstall your printer.
            

## Set as Default Printer

4.  Set Default Printer
    
    1.  Set your ZPL printer as the default printer.
        

d. In Windows 11:

"Let Windows manage my default printer" is ON.  
Turn off (or toggle off) the setting "Let Windows manage my default printer".

5.  In Windows, under Printers, uninstall all unwanted printers from computer (many times, printing issues involve conflicting printer and print drivers).
    
6.  Print a test page from Windows (if that works, try from the Stratus Printer App as well)
    

### It Prints, but not from the Stratus Printer App

If you can print a test label from the Zebra Setup Utility, but not from the Stratus Printer App

7.  Verify that you have the latest version of the Stratus Printer App installed.
    
    1.  To see a list of available versions from GTP, run this command from a command prompt – i.e., type CMD into the Windows search bar, run that, then type in the following command:
        
        winget show GTPSoftware.Print -s GtpSoftware --versions
        
    2.  Compare this to the version of your Printer app.
        
8.  Verify that the Stratus Print application is open.
    
9.  Verify that the printer is not asleep.
    
10.  Verify the computer has a station assigned to it if attempting to print from a station.
    
11.  Read the LOG file generated by the Stratus Print app.
    
    1.  Exit the Stratus Print app first (so that it will flush its remaining log entries),
        
    2.  then go to  
        C:\\Users\\**<Windows User>**\\AppData\\Roaming\\GTP STRATUS Logs\\Print\\
        
    3.  See the Log.Txt file in that folder.
        
    4.  Open with notepad or some other tool.
        
        1.  Note well: The newest activity is at the bottom (the oldest log activity is at the top).
            
    5.  From top down, search for the word “Error” or “Warn”
        
12.  Check Windows User Rights:  You do **not** need to run the Stratus Printer app as an administrator, but IT department must not lock down the user profile's write rights to the %appdata% part of the hard drive. 
    
13.  Check Firewalls: The Workstation app uses SignalR over port 443, therefore your IT department has to allow websockets via your firewall.
    
14.  If you cannot print with a certain user, troubleshoot by trying to print with a user that has elevated rights on the machine and in Stratus.
    
15.  Try to print a label from a computer NOT connected to your network. If you don’t know how to do this, the GTP SD team can impersonate a user in your company and print to one of their ZPL printers. If they are able to print to a ZPL from Stratus via a user from your company, then there is likely a Windows policy on your computer that prevents the app (via that user) from printing.
    
16.  If you still have no success, send the log file from Step 1 above to the GTP Service Desk
