# Markup for PDF Assembly Attachments, PDF Package Attachments, and CAD Sheet - STRATUS Knowledge Base - Confluence

> ## Excerpt
> The Markup tools for Assembly PDF Attachments, Package PDF Attachments, Assembly CAD Sheets, and Package CAD Sheets all share similar functionality as they all can be uploaded to BIM 360 and versioned. Note: Markup is also available within the Package’s Viewer and the Assembly’s Viewer, but these markups cannot be versioned and saved to BIM 360.

---
The Markup tools for Assembly PDF Attachments, Package PDF Attachments, Assembly CAD Sheets, and Package CAD Sheets all share similar functionality as they all can be uploaded to BIM 360 and versioned. **Note**: Markup is also available within the Package’s Viewer and the Assembly’s Viewer, but these markups cannot be versioned and saved to BIM 360.

-   1 [Markup Setup](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2308407297/Markup+for+PDF+Assembly+Attachments+PDF+Package+Attachments+and+CAD+Sheet#Markup-Setup)
-   2 [Markup Permissions](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2308407297/Markup+for+PDF+Assembly+Attachments+PDF+Package+Attachments+and+CAD+Sheet#Markup-Permissions)
-   3 [Markup Tools](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2308407297/Markup+for+PDF+Assembly+Attachments+PDF+Package+Attachments+and+CAD+Sheet#Markup-Tools)
    -   3.1 [Start a Markup](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2308407297/Markup+for+PDF+Assembly+Attachments+PDF+Package+Attachments+and+CAD+Sheet#Start-a-Markup)
    -   3.2 [Place a Markup](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2308407297/Markup+for+PDF+Assembly+Attachments+PDF+Package+Attachments+and+CAD+Sheet#Place-a-Markup)
    -   3.3 [Save Markup](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2308407297/Markup+for+PDF+Assembly+Attachments+PDF+Package+Attachments+and+CAD+Sheet#Save-Markup)
    -   3.4 [Markup a Multipage PDF Attachment](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2308407297/Markup+for+PDF+Assembly+Attachments+PDF+Package+Attachments+and+CAD+Sheet#Markup-a-Multipage-PDF-Attachment)
    -   3.5 [Edit a PDF Markup Attachment](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2308407297/Markup+for+PDF+Assembly+Attachments+PDF+Package+Attachments+and+CAD+Sheet#Edit-a-PDF-Markup-Attachment)
    -   3.6 [View a PDF Markup](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2308407297/Markup+for+PDF+Assembly+Attachments+PDF+Package+Attachments+and+CAD+Sheet#View-a-PDF-Markup)
    -   3.7 [Delete an Individual Markup from the PDF Viewer](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2308407297/Markup+for+PDF+Assembly+Attachments+PDF+Package+Attachments+and+CAD+Sheet#Delete-an-Individual-Markup-from-the-PDF-Viewer)
    -   3.8 [Delete a PDF Markup From the Markup Table](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2308407297/Markup+for+PDF+Assembly+Attachments+PDF+Package+Attachments+and+CAD+Sheet#Delete-a-PDF-Markup-From-the-Markup-Table)
    -   3.9 [Upload Version (Lock)](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2308407297/Markup+for+PDF+Assembly+Attachments+PDF+Package+Attachments+and+CAD+Sheet#Upload-Version-(Lock))
    -   3.10 [Print or View Previous Markup Versions](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2308407297/Markup+for+PDF+Assembly+Attachments+PDF+Package+Attachments+and+CAD+Sheet#Print-or-View-Previous-Markup-Versions)
-   4 [Markup Tool Summary](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2308407297/Markup+for+PDF+Assembly+Attachments+PDF+Package+Attachments+and+CAD+Sheet#Markup-Tool-Summary)

## Markup Setup

For assemblies and packages, a PDF attachment must created.

-   To create a PDF attachment for an Assembly STRATUS Sheet see the [**PDF Assembly**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2144272385/Assembly+STRATUS+Sheet#Generate-PDF "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2144272385/Assembly+STRATUS+Sheet#Generate-PDF") for more information.
    
-   To create a PDF attachment for a Package STRATUS Sheet see the [**PDF Package**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/199884912/Package+STRATUS+Sheet#PDF "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/199884912/Package+STRATUS+Sheet#PDF") for more information.
    

For CAD Sheet, a CAD Sheet must be generated:

-   To generate an Assembly CAD Sheet, see the [**Assembly CAD Sheet**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2146992129 "/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2146992129") for more information.
    
-   To generate a Package CAD Sheet, see the [**Package CAD Sheet**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2136506369 "/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2136506369") for more information.
    

## Markup Permissions

Set Markups permissions for **Create & Edit**, **Delete**, and **View** under:

Admin > Company > Project Roles > **Assemblies** \> Details > Markups

Admin > Company > Project Roles > **Packages** > Details > Markups

The following describes how to use the Markup tools.

## Start a Markup

1.  To access the Markup tools:
    
    1.  **PDF** \- Click the **Markups** icon in the Attachments table.
        
    2.  **CAD Sheet** - Click the **Markup** icon.
        
2.  The Markup tools will flyout and the Markup version number will display.
    
    1.  Optionally, click the expand to full screen button (top right). The PDF or CAD Sheet will display in the viewer and the **Markup Tools** will display.
        
        1.  **V1** displays until a markup is made and the **Upload Version** button is clicked. See the [**Upload Version Markups**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2255814657/03+14+2024+-+v7.1.1#Upload-Version-Markups "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2255814657/03+14+2024+-+v7.1.1#Upload-Version-Markups") section for more information.
            
        2.  In the PDF viewer, the mouse can be used to pan and zoom the PDF.
            

## Place a Markup

1.  Click a Markup Tool (Ex. Cloud). As the user moves the mouse, the mouse will change to indicate where the markup will be placed.
    
2.  Click to place the markup (Ex. For a cloud click and drag to form the cloud).
    
    1.  Whenever a Markup tool is selected the following dialog will display until Cancel or Save Markup is clicked.
        
        1.  **Undo** \- Click this button (arrow pointing left) to undo markup edits since the last time Save Markup was clicked.
            
        2.  **Redo** \- Click this button (arrow pointing right) to redo markup edits since the last time Save Markup was clicked.
            
        3.  **Cancel** \- Cancel will cancel all Markups since the last time Save Markup was clicked.
            
        4.  **Save Markup** - See the [**Save Markup**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/edit-v2/2308407297#Save-Markup "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/edit-v2/2308407297#Save-Markup") section for more information.
            
    2.  **Note**: CAD Sheet Markups are placed in relation to the CAD Sheet. For example:
        
        1.  The screenshot below displays the size of the CAD Sheet when the Markup was added.
            
        2.  After changing the size of the canvas using the mouse wheel, the Markup changes proportionally (smaller in this case) with the canvas.
            
3.  After placing any markup, the following actions can be done to the markup object:
    
    1.  **Select**
        
    2.  **Move**
        
    3.  **Edit**
        
    4.  **Rotated**
        
    5.  **Resize**
        
    6.  **Delete**
        
4.  **Unsaved Markup Note**: If a markup is added to a page and before it is saved the user clicks either the **Next Page** or **Previous page** button, or the **X** in the top right corner of the the Markup Tools panel, any unsaved Markups will be lost. See the [**Save Markup**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/edit-v2/2308407297#Save-Markup "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/edit-v2/2308407297#Save-Markup") section for more information.
    

## Save Markup

1.  When done placing a Markup, click the **Save Markup** button. As a result:
    
    1.  The Markup will display in the **Markup Tools** table and the initial markup will be automatically named **Markup 1**. This name can be manually edited. The **User** and **Date-Time** will also be automatically entered.
        
    2.  The **Upload Version** button will be enabled.
        
    3.  For the Packages Attachments and Assemblies Attachments table:
        
        1.  The **Markups pencil icon** will change to **green** indicating there is an editable markup associated with the .PDF.
            
            1.  **Note**: When the **Markups pencil icon** is **blue**, it indicates that the PDF can be marked up but there are no active Markups. If the version is V2 or higher, it means that previously active Markups have been Uploaded Versioned to BIM360 and are no longer editable.
                
        2.  The active unversioned Markup will display a number to the left of the Markups pencil icon indicating the number of editable markups on the .PDF (Ex 1).
            
    4.  Anyone with access can view/edit this active unversioned Markup.
        
2.  A separate Markup can be made.
    
    1.  Click a Markup Tool, place it in the viewer, and click **Save Markup**.
        
    2.  As a result:
        
        1.  The new Markup will display in the **table** and will be automatically named **Markup 2**. This name can be manually edited.
            
        2.  The active unversioned Markup will display a number to the left of the Markups pencil icon indicating the number of editable markups on the .PDF (Ex 2).
            

## Markup a Multipage PDF Attachment

For PDF (Package and Assembly) attachments, to Markup a multipage PDF attachment:

1.  From the Attachments tab, click **Markups** pencil icon associated with a PDF that has more than one page.
    
2.  Markup Tools will add a page selector tool.
    
3.  The PDF viewer will only display one page of the PDF at a time. As a result, each page:
    
    1.  Can be marked up individually.
        
    2.  Will have it’s own list of saved markups.
        
4.  To markup a page, use the **Next Page** or **Previous page** buttons to change pages, click a Markup Tool, place it in the viewer, and click **Save Markup**.
    
    1.  **Unsaved Markup Note**: If a markup is added to a page and before it is saved the user clicks either the **Next Page** or **Previous page** button, or the **X** in the top right corner of the the Markup Tools panel, any unsaved Markups will be lost.
        

## Edit a PDF Markup Attachment

1.  Anyone with Project Role permission can view/edit the Markup.
    
2.  From the Attachments tab, click **Markups** pencil icon associated with a PDF that has one or more Markups.
    
3.  Each page that has a markup will display all markups.
    
4.  To edit an individual markup, click the markup row. The markup will display in the viewer in edit mode.
    
    1.  The selected markup will be isolated and will be editable.
        
    2.  The **Save Markup** button will display.
        
5.  Select the markup within the PDF. In this example, a Text markup was selected. The Font Size control displays along with a delete button.
    
6.  In this example, the font size, text, and position have been changed. **Note**: Click **Cancel** to exit edit mode.
    
7.  Before saving, another Markup (Ex. Arrow) can be added. **Note**: Click **Cancel** to exit edit mode.
    
8.  Click **Save Markup**. As a result:
    
    1.  The existing Markup will be saved with the edited information. The selected page now has 2 active markups (Markup 1 has only 1 active markup; Markup 2 has 2 active markups). With no markups selected in the table, all markups for the page are displayed.
        

## View a PDF Markup

1.  Anyone with Project Role permission can view/edit the Markup.
    
2.  Go to the Attachments tab and click the **Markups** pencil icon associated with a PDF.
    
3.  By default, all markups for the page will display.
    
4.  To isolate a markup, select the Markup Tools row (Ex. Markup 2). The selected markup will display and is editable. **Note**: Click **Cancel** to exit edit mode.
    

## Delete an Individual Markup from the PDF Viewer

Use this delete method when you want to delete one of many markups within a single saved markup table row.

1.  Anyone with Project Role permission can delete the Markup.
    
2.  From the Attachments tab, click the **green** **Markups** pencil icon associated with a PDF. The green pencil icon indicates an active markup.
    
3.  Select a Markup row (Ex. Markup 2). In this example, Markup 2 includes 2 markups within the PDF viewer (Text that reads Markup2-2 and a blue arrow).
    
4.  Select one of the markups (Ex. the arrow). The **Delete** button will display in the PDF viewer.
    
5.  Click the **Delete** button and then click the **Save Markup** button. The individual markup will be deleted.
    

## Delete a PDF Markup From the Markup Table

Use this delete method when you want to delete all markups within a single saved markup table row.

1.  Anyone with Project Role permission can delete the Markup.
    
2.  From the Attachments tab, click the **green** **Markups** pencil icon associated with a PDF. The green pencil icon indicates an active markup.
    
3.  In this example, Markup 2 includes 2 markups within the PDF viewer.
    
4.  Click the **Delete** button in the Markups table row associated with the markup to be deleted (Ex. Markup 2). The markup row will be deleted and the markup in the viewer no longer display.
    
5.  As a result:
    
    1.  The Markup row will be deleted.
        
    2.  The Markups within the PDF viewer will be deleted.
        
    3.  The **active unversioned** Markup will change from 2 to 1.
        

## Upload Version (Lock)

A Markup can have more than one Markup version (V1, V2, etc.) using the **Upload Version** button which locks the current version and creates a PDF in BIM 360. Each Markup version (V1, V2, etc.) can include multiple saved Markup sets using the **Save Markup** button which are works-in-progress.

The **Upload Version** button is enabled when a markup has been saved. Once the **Upload Version** button is clicked, the next time the PDF Attachment is opened or previewed, the markups will display, permanently overwriting the original PDF.

1.  To enable the **Upload Version** button, create and save a Markup.
    
2.  Click the **Upload Version** button. Markup V1 is now locked. V2 can be started which will be built upon V1. After the PDF is uploaded to BIM 360 the page will be updated with the following:
    
    1.  **Active Markups** - The **Active Markup** in the Markup table disappear as they are now embedded within the PDF.
        
    2.  **Markup Version** - The **Markup Version** increments (Ex. from V1 to V2). This indicates that the next markup placed in the PDF viewer will be associated with V2.
        
    3.  **Version Selection** - The **Version Selection** button displays at the bottom of the Markup tools.
        
    4.  **Upload Version** - The **Upload Version** button is disabled.
        

## Print or View Previous Markup Versions

1.  From the Attachments tab, click the **Markups pencil icon** associated with a versioned markup (Ex. version is V2 or higher).
    
2.  Click the **Markup Versions** button at the bottom of the Markup Tools toolbar. The toolbar will collapse and **Markup Versions** will display.
    
    1.  Highlight the version to be printed (Ex. V1)
        
    2.  Click the **3-dots** icon.
        
    3.  Click the **View** button.
        
3.  In a separate browser tab, the PDF file will display. Use the browser’s print tool to print the PDF.
    

The following Markup tools are available.

**Note**: To change the color of a tool, select a color using the pencil or paint buck before selecting the Markup tool.

1.  **Freehand**
    
    1.  Click and hold down the mouse to display (2) Freehand options, Freehand and Highlight.
        
    2.  **Freehand (left)** \- Select the tool, then click and drag to draw freehand lines and curves as if you were outlining them on paper with a pen or pencil.
        
    3.  **Highlight (right)**\- Select Freehand > highlight, then click and drag to draw freehand highlighted lines and curves.
        
2.  **Text** \- Select the tool, click in the document, type your text, and press Enter. To set the text color: 1) Select the Line Style color, 2) Click the Text tool, 3) Use the Text tool to enter text.
    
3.  **Callout**
    
    1.  **Callout** \- Select the tool and click in the CAD Sheet canvas. Click and drag the tool to place the arrow. Let go of the mouse and the Callout Text box will display. You can format and resize the text box, as well as select the text box fill color. The Callout Text box and the Arrow are 2 different objects. Therefore, they cannot be moved together but can be moved separately. Click Save Markup.
        
4.  **Cloud**
    
    1.  Click and hold down the mouse to display (2) cloud options, a rectangle and a Polycloud.
        
    2.  **Cloud** \- Select the tool, then click and drag to draw the rectangle cloud. Select the object to use the rotation tool.
        
    3.  **Polycloud** \- Select Cloud > Polycloud, then click to place the first point, and continue clicking to draw cloud segments. Double-click to close the shape.
        
5.  **Shapes**
    
    1.  Click and hold down the mouse to display (3) shape options.
        
    2.  **Rectangle** \- Select Shapes > Rectangle, then click and drag to draw, or click two points to place the top left and bottom right corners.
        
    3.  **Circle** \- Select Shapes > Oval, then click and drag to draw, or click to specify the top right corner, and drag to draw. Drag diagonally a circle or right/left/up/down for an ellipse.
        
    4.  **Line \\ Polyline** \- Select Shapes > Polyline, then click to place first point, and continue clicking to draw line segments. Double-click to close the shape.
        
6.  **Arrow** \- Select the tool, then click and drag to draw.
    
7.  **Line Style (Color)** - Select the tool, then choose the desired line color and Line Thickness. Add a Markup (Ex. Arrow, Cloud, Shape, not Text) and the thickness will display.
    
8.  **Fill Style (Color)** - Select the tool, then choose the desired fill color and the Opacity.
    
    1.  Add a Markup (Ex. Arrow, Cloud, Shape, not Text) and the thickness will display.

# Markup for Viewers Assemblies and Packages - STRATUS Knowledge Base - Confluence

> ## Excerpt
> The Markup tools for the Assemblies Viewer and the Package Viewer share the same functionality. Note: Markup is also available within the Assembly PDF Attachments, Package PDF Attachments, Assembly CAD Sheets, and Package CAD Sheets, but these  markups include the added feature of versioning with BIM 360.

---
The Markup tools for the Assemblies Viewer and the Package Viewer share the same functionality. **Note**: Markup is also available within the Assembly PDF Attachments, Package PDF Attachments, Assembly CAD Sheets, and Package CAD Sheets, but these markups include the added feature of versioning with BIM 360.

-   1 [Markup Setup](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2309521409/Markup+for+Viewers+Assemblies+and+Packages#Markup-Setup)
-   2 [Markup Permissions](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2309521409/Markup+for+Viewers+Assemblies+and+Packages#Markup-Permissions)
-   3 [Markups in the Viewer](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2309521409/Markup+for+Viewers+Assemblies+and+Packages#Markups-in-the-Viewer)
    -   3.1 [New Markup](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2309521409/Markup+for+Viewers+Assemblies+and+Packages#New-Markup)
    -   3.2 [Save Markup](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2309521409/Markup+for+Viewers+Assemblies+and+Packages#Save-Markup)
    -   3.3 [View an Existing Markup](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2309521409/Markup+for+Viewers+Assemblies+and+Packages#View-an-Existing-Markup)
    -   3.4 [Edit a Markup in the Viewer](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2309521409/Markup+for+Viewers+Assemblies+and+Packages#Edit-a-Markup-in-the-Viewer)
    -   3.5 [Delete a Markup in the Viewer](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2309521409/Markup+for+Viewers+Assemblies+and+Packages#Delete-a-Markup-in-the-Viewer)
    -   3.6 [Delete a Markup from the Markups Table](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2309521409/Markup+for+Viewers+Assemblies+and+Packages#Delete-a-Markup-from-the-Markups-Table)

## Markup Setup

Any package or assembly can be marked up in the Viewer.

## Markup Permissions

Set Markups permissions for **Create & Edit**, **Delete**, and **View** under:

Admin > Company > Project Roles > **Assemblies** \> Details > Markups

Admin > Company > Project Roles > **Packages** > Details > Markups

## Markups in the Viewer

## New Markup

The **Markups** tab associated with each assembly or package is used to manage markups made in the Assemblies Viewer and Packages Viewer.

1.  Set the Viewer orientation and zoom before adding a Markup.
    
2.  Go to the **Markups** tab. The Markups table displays.
    
3.  Click the **New Markup** button.
    
4.  The **Markups** tool bar and **Save Markup** display.
    
5.  Click a Markup tool (Ex. Text). For Text, the Font Size control displays (Ex. 16). The Font Size can be changed now or later. See the [**Markup Tool Summary**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2308407297/Markup+for+PDF+Assembly+Attachments+PDF+Package+Attachments+and+CAD+Sheet#Markup-Tool-Summary "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2308407297/Markup+for+PDF+Assembly+Attachments+PDF+Package+Attachments+and+CAD+Sheet#Markup-Tool-Summary") article for more information.
    
    1.  Some markup tools (Ex. Cloud) include an expander arrow on the bottom left. To open the expander, click and hold the mouse on the button until it expands.
        
    2.  Once expanded, select the tool.
        
    3.  **Note**: Use the **Line Style** tool to select the color and line thickness prior to selecting shape and arrow tools.
        
6.  As the user moves the mouse into the Viewer, the mouse will turn to a plus to indicate where the markup will be placed.
    
7.  Click in the Viewer to place the markup.
    
8.  Use the tool to place the markup.
    
    1.  **Move** \- Hover over the markup until the Move tool displays.
        
    2.  **Rotate** - Click the rotate tool on markups that support rotation (Ex. Arrow, Cloud, Circle, Rectangle, Freehand).
        
    3.  **Resize** \- Click the stretch handle to resize.
        
9.  **Add another markup** - Additional markup tools can be selected and placed in the Viewer.
    
10.  When done, see the [**Save Markup**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2309521409/Markup+for+Viewers+Assemblies+and+Packages#Save-Markup "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2309521409/Markup+for+Viewers+Assemblies+and+Packages#Save-Markup") section.
    
11.  **Unsaved Markup Note**: If a Markup is added to the Viewer and before it is saved the user leaves the Markups tab in any way, any unsaved Markups will be lost.
    

## Save Markup

1.  When done click **Save Markup**. The markup will be saved in the Markups table. Each new markup is automatically uniquely named for the selected assembly or package.
    
2.  The Markup **Name** is editable by clicking it.
    
3.  Click **Save** and the edited name will display.
    

## View an Existing Markup

1.  For anyone to view a markup, go to the **Markups** tab.
    
2.  In the Markups table, click the markup row to be viewed (Ex. Markup 1).
    
    1.  The row will be highlighted blue.
        
    2.  The markup will display in the Viewer and the viewpoint will snap to the camera angle and zoom level when the markup was saved.
        
    3.  For users who have **Create & Edit** permission:
        
        1.  The selected markup will be highlighted in the Viewer.
            
        2.  The Save Markup | Cancel dialog will display.
            
        3.  The markup will display in edit mode.
            
3.  When done viewing, click the **Cancel** button to return the Viewer to normal operations including the STRATUS Toolbar and view cube.
    

## Edit a Markup in the Viewer

For users who have **Create & Edit** permission:

1.  Go to the **Markups** tab.
    
2.  In the Markups table, click the Markups row to be edited (Ex. Markup 1).
    
    1.  The row will be highlighted blue.
        
    2.  The Markup will display in the Viewer and the viewpoint will snap to the camera angle and zoom level when the markup was saved.
        
    3.  The selected markup will be highlighted. If the markup was a Text or Callout, the Font Size control will also display.
        
    4.  The Save Markup | Cancel dialog will display.
        
3.  Edit the markup. See the [**Markup Tools**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2152530692/Viewer+CAD+Sheet+Markup#Markup-Tools "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2152530692/Viewer+CAD+Sheet+Markup#Markup-Tools") article for more information about using Markup Tools. Below are some highlights:
    
    2.  **Save Markup** - When done editing, click the **Save Markup** button.
        
4.  **Cancel** - Click the **Cancel** button to display the STRATUS toolbar and orientation cube.
    

## Delete a Markup in the Viewer

Use this delete method when you want to delete one of many markups within a single saved markup table row.

For users who have **Create & Edit** and **Delete** permission:

1.  Go to the **Markups** tab.
    
2.  Select the markup row in the Markup table. Only the selected markup will display in the Viewer. All individual markups saved along with the markup table row will display.
    
3.  In the Viewer, select the markup to be deleted (Ex. Markup 1-3).
    
4.  Click the **Delete** button.
    
    1.  The Markup will be deleted.
        
5.  Click **Save Markup** to save the change. The Markup in the Viewer will not display next time the Markup is loaded.
    

## Delete a Markup from the Markups Table

Use this delete method when you want to delete all markups within a single saved markup table row.

For users who have **Create & Edit** and **Delete** permission:

1.  Go to the Markups tab.
    
2.  If you are not sure which markup row to delete, each row can be clicked to view the markup.
    
3.  Once the markup row to be deleted is identified, click the **Delete** button.
    
    1.  The markup will be deleted.
        
    2.  The Markup row in the table will be deleted.
        
    3.  The Markup in the Viewer will not display next time the page is loaded.

# Multiple Entry Selection and Action - STRATUS Knowledge Base - Confluence

> ## Excerpt
> A:     On the Assemblies > Dashboard and Packages > Items pages multiple entries (rows) can be selected and then an action can be taken on those entries (Ex. Update Tracking Status, edit an editable field, and Delete).

---
> -   1[Q:     How does multiple entry selection and action function?](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/1963720705/Multiple+Entry+Selection+and+Action#MultipleEntrySelectionandAction-Q%3AHowdoesmultipleentryselectionandactionfunction%3F) 
> -   2[Q:     How does multiple entry selection work on the Assemblies > Dashboard?](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/1963720705/Multiple+Entry+Selection+and+Action#MultipleEntrySelectionandAction-Q%3AHowdoesmultipleentryselectionworkontheAssemblies%3EDashboard%3F)
> -   3[Q:     What are some examples of multiple entry selection and action functions?](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/1963720705/Multiple+Entry+Selection+and+Action#MultipleEntrySelectionandAction-Q%3AWhataresomeexamplesofmultipleentryselectionandactionfunctions%3F)
>     -   3.1[Example: Update Tracking Status for Multiple Entries](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/1963720705/Multiple+Entry+Selection+and+Action#MultipleEntrySelectionandAction-Example%3AUpdateTrackingStatusforMultipleEntries)
>     -   3.2[Example: Delete Multiple Entries](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/1963720705/Multiple+Entry+Selection+and+Action#MultipleEntrySelectionandAction-Example%3ADeleteMultipleEntries)
>     -   3.3[Example: Update Editable Field for Multiple Entries](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/1963720705/Multiple+Entry+Selection+and+Action#MultipleEntrySelectionandAction-Example%3AUpdateEditableFieldforMultipleEntries)
>     -   3.4[Example: Add Spools to Packages](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/1963720705/Multiple+Entry+Selection+and+Action#MultipleEntrySelectionandAction-Example%3AAddSpoolstoPackages)
> -   4[Q:     Is multiple entry selection and action functions available in Packages > Items?](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/1963720705/Multiple+Entry+Selection+and+Action#MultipleEntrySelectionandAction-Q%3AIsmultipleentryselectionandactionfunctionsavailableinPackages%3EItems%3F)
>     -   4.1[Example: Packages > Items](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/1963720705/Multiple+Entry+Selection+and+Action#MultipleEntrySelectionandAction-Example%3APackages%3EItems)
> 
> ## **Q:     How does multiple entry selection and action function?** 
> 
> **A:**     On the Assemblies > Dashboard and Packages > Items pages multiple entries (rows) can be selected and then an action can be taken on those entries (Ex. Update Tracking Status, edit an editable field, and Delete). 
> 
> The following rules are applied no matter what action is taken:
> 
> 1.  **Multiple Actions Only Apply to Selected Entries** - When Show is checked for any entry, the action taken will only apply to the selected entries. If the user attempt to edit an entry row outside of the selected rows, the following message will display.
>     
>     ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/attachments/1963720705/image2022-9-9_7-33-14.png?version=1&modificationDate=1662726795424&cacheVersion=1&api=v2)
>     
> 2.  **Attachments** - Cannot attach a file to multiple entries using the multiple entry selection feature.
>     
> 
> ## **Q:     How does multiple entry selection work on the Assemblies > Dashboard?**
> 
> **A:     To use the multiple entry selection feature on the Assemblies > Dashboard:**
> 
> 1.  In the Show column, check multiple entries.
>     
>     1.  Each checked row is highlighted in light blue and the number of entries (rows) selected displays.
>         
>         ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/attachments/1963720705/image2023-9-22_9-5-38.png?version=1&modificationDate=1695391539273&cacheVersion=1&api=v2)
>         
>     2.  For each selected assembly, the Packages column displays the package selected on page refresh.  
>         ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/attachments/1963720705/image2023-9-22_9-6-32.png?version=1&modificationDate=1695391594047&cacheVersion=1&api=v2)
>     3.  In addition, the # Assemblies column is updated on the Packages Dashboard.![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/attachments/1963720705/image2023-9-22_9-7-11.png?version=1&modificationDate=1695391632977&cacheVersion=1&api=v2)
>         
>     4.  Check/Uncheck All
>         
>         1.  To check all checkboxes in the table, check the Show checkbox in the header row. In this case, 3743 rows have been checked.
>             
>             ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/1963720705/image2022-9-9_7-34-12.png?version=1&modificationDate=1662726854216&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=250&height=439)
>             
>         2.  To uncheck all checkboxes in the table, uncheck the Show checkbox in the header row.
>             
> 2.  Most actions that can be taken on one entry can be taken when multiple entries have been checked in the Show column.
>     
>     1.  Follow the edit/update prompts specific to editing the selected field (Ex. Status, Delete, Custom Editable Field, etc.) to make the change to all selected entries. See the examples below.
>         
>     2.  **Note:** Updating 1 row takes between .5 and 2.5 seconds depending on the edited column.
>         
>     3.  **Exception**: The ability to attach a document to multiple entries is disabled.
>         
> 
> ## **Q:     What are some examples of multiple entry selection and action functions?**
> 
> **A:     See below.**
> 
> ### Example: Update Tracking Status for Multiple Entries
> 
> **To simultaneously change the Tracking Status of multiple selected assemblies:**
> 
> 1.  In the **Show** column, check the assemblies to be impacted by the Status change. Each checked row is highlighted in light blue and the number of entries (rows) selected displays.
>     
>     ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/1963720705/image2022-9-9_7-37-7.png?version=1&modificationDate=1662727041416&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=1100&height=352)
>     
> 2.  For one of the selected rows, click the current status (Ex. Packaged). The Update Tracking Status dialog will display.
>     
>     ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/1963720705/image2022-9-9_7-38-0.png?version=1&modificationDate=1662727081503&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=350&height=297)
>     
> 3.  Select the new status and then click the Update button. The Status of all checked rows will change to the new status. **Note**: It takes approximately 1.5 seconds to update a row after a tracking status change. If 100 items are checked and tracking status updated it will take approximately 150 seconds (2.5 minutes) to update the Assemblies table.![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/1963720705/image2022-9-9_7-40-1.png?version=1&modificationDate=1662727202555&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=1100&height=353)
>     
> 
> ### Example: Delete Multiple Entries
> 
> **To simultaneously Delete multiple selected assemblies:**
> 
> 1.  In the **Show** column, check the assemblies to be impacted by the Status change. Each checked row is highlighted in light blue and the number of entries (rows) selected displays. Click the **Delete** button for one of the selected rows. The Delete Assemblies dialog will display.![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/1963720705/image2022-9-9_7-39-47.png?version=1&modificationDate=1662727189444&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=900&height=407)
>     
>     1.  **KEEP** \- Click **KEEP** to cancel the operation and not delete the selected assemblies.
>         
>     2.  **Delete** - Click **Delete** to delete the selected assemblies. **Note**: It takes approximately 2.5 seconds to update a row after a delete action. If 100 items are checked and deleted it will take approximately 250 seconds (4 minutes) to update the Assemblies table.
>         
> 
> ### Example: Update Editable Field for Multiple Entries
> 
> 1.  In the **Show** column, check the assemblies to be impacted by the change to an editable field. Each checked row is highlighted in light blue and the number of entries (rows) selected displays. Click **an editable field** for one of the selected rows. The edit dialog will display.
>     
>     ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/1963720705/image2022-9-9_7-42-33.png?version=1&modificationDate=1662727354567&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=1100&height=504)
>     
> 2.  After saving the change the editable field for the selected entries will be updated.
>     
>     ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/1963720705/image2022-9-9_7-43-2.png?version=1&modificationDate=1662727383743&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=1100&height=512)
>     
> 
> ### Example: Add Spools to Packages
> 
> For companies that spool in Revit and package in STRATUS, multiple spools can be added to the Package in the Assemblies Dashboard.
> 
> 1.  Select Assemblies and click the Packages cell to display the Package selection dialog.
>     
> 2.  Select the Package and Save. A message similar to the following will display.![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/1963720705/image2022-9-9_7-43-31.png?version=1&modificationDate=1662727413225&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=1100&height=557)
>     
> 3.  Click Modify and the select Package name will display for each checked Assembly.
>     
>     ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/1963720705/image2022-9-9_7-44-5.png?version=1&modificationDate=1662727447067&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=650&height=517)
>     
> 
> ## **Q:     Is multiple entry selection and action functions available in Packages > Items?**
> 
> **A:     Yes, see below.**
> 
> ### Example: Packages > Items
> 
> Multi-entry row selection is also available on the Packages > Items tab.
> 
> ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/1963720705/image2022-9-9_7-46-50.png?version=1&modificationDate=1662727612409&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=1100&height=535)

# Novarc - STRATUS Knowledge Base - Confluence

> ## Excerpt
> This article describes the integration between Stratus and Novarc Spool Welding Robot (SWR).

---
This article describes the integration between Stratus and Novarc Spool Welding Robot (SWR).

-   1 [Configure Tool](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/349175812/Novarc#Configure-Tool)
-   2 [Configure App Key](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/349175812/Novarc#Configure-App-Key)
-   3 [Configure Station](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/349175812/Novarc#Configure-Station)
-   4 [Stratus to SWR Workflow](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/349175812/Novarc#Stratus-to-SWR-Workflow)
-   5 [SWR Stratus Dialog](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/349175812/Novarc#SWR-Stratus-Dialog)
-   6 [Troubleshooting](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/349175812/Novarc#Troubleshooting)

## Configure Tool

1.  Configure a **Tool** under Admin > Company > Tools. Note the generated Tool Id. See the [**Tools**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/215220225 "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/215220225") article for more information. Below is an example. 
    
    ![image-20250527-172122.png](blob:https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/ea6b444d-9c3a-4274-96dd-483534755409#media-blob-url=true&id=d23f7d14-925e-4bc8-97e3-7288f8b7709c&collection=contentId-349175812&contextId=349175812&mimeType=image%2Fpng&name=image-20250527-172122.png&size=23749&width=1413&height=182&alt=image-20250527-172122.png)
    

## Configure App Key

1.  Configure an **App Key** selecting the **Novarc** Partner App under Admin > Company > App Key. See the [**App Keys (Admin)**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/201654303 "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/201654303") article for more information. Below is an example. 
    
    ![image-20250527-172337.png](blob:https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/79982888-0156-4a8d-993d-1c55094bc50f#media-blob-url=true&id=7eaf3498-630c-401b-be7d-870e746c9c83&collection=contentId-349175812&contextId=349175812&mimeType=image%2Fpng&name=image-20250527-172337.png&size=16469&width=1050&height=191&alt=image-20250527-172337.png)
    

## Configure Station

1.  Configure a **Station** under Admin > Company > Stations. See the [**Stations**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/215220408 "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/215220408") article for more information. 
    

## Stratus to SWR Workflow

1.  Under Assemblies > Viewer > Parts, the Stratus user selects an assembly. Notice the highlighted Assembly and Part list.
    
    ![image-20250527-161444.png](blob:https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/a77f3135-c5cb-4cee-add6-ec534fd7dabf#media-blob-url=true&id=2fd23038-1958-48b0-ac78-d014f771dd9d&collection=contentId-349175812&contextId=349175812&mimeType=image%2Fpng&name=image-20250527-161444.png&size=98227&width=727&height=501&alt=image-20250527-161444.png)
    
2.  Click the gear icon and make sure the Novarc tool created in the [**Configure Tool**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/349175812/Novarc#Configure-Tool "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/349175812/Novarc#Configure-Tool") section is selected.
    
    ![image-20250527-173251.png](https://media-cdn.atlassian.com/file/0a5397c4-eb44-410e-9ecf-ed07ba92f9c8/image/cdn?allowAnimated=true&client=5f4a70b1-9d9d-47c3-b388-87235680bb54&collection=contentId-349175812&height=262&max-age=2592000&mode=full-fit&source=mediaCard&token=eyJhbGciOiJIUzI1NiJ9.eyJpc3MiOiI1ZjRhNzBiMS05ZDlkLTQ3YzMtYjM4OC04NzIzNTY4MGJiNTQiLCJhY2Nlc3MiOnsidXJuOmZpbGVzdG9yZTpjb2xsZWN0aW9uOmNvbnRlbnRJZC0zNDkxNzU4MTIiOlsicmVhZCJdfSwiZXhwIjoxNzUwODY4NTQ4LCJuYmYiOjE3NTA4NjU2Njh9.48FAKcTsgApTgCA1vZLEHHhrTOBCRN6JOzHTpLWAO9o&width=760)
    
3.  For the selected assembly, select one or more parts and then click **Send # Checked to Tool** button.
    
    ![image-20250527-170522.png](https://media-cdn.atlassian.com/file/4650adda-bfce-433b-8b24-25faa7730ec0/image/cdn?allowAnimated=true&client=5f4a70b1-9d9d-47c3-b388-87235680bb54&collection=contentId-349175812&height=384&max-age=2592000&mode=full-fit&source=mediaCard&token=eyJhbGciOiJIUzI1NiJ9.eyJpc3MiOiI1ZjRhNzBiMS05ZDlkLTQ3YzMtYjM4OC04NzIzNTY4MGJiNTQiLCJhY2Nlc3MiOnsidXJuOmZpbGVzdG9yZTpjb2xsZWN0aW9uOmNvbnRlbnRJZC0zNDkxNzU4MTIiOlsicmVhZCJdfSwiZXhwIjoxNzUwODY4NTQ4LCJuYmYiOjE3NTA4NjU2Njh9.48FAKcTsgApTgCA1vZLEHHhrTOBCRN6JOzHTpLWAO9o&width=760)
    
4.  The part(s) will be queued and automatically loaded into the Spool Welding Robot (SWR) Setup screen.
    
    ![image-20250527-161900.png](https://media-cdn.atlassian.com/file/2dd0fad6-2861-4b32-b894-ba03f8bbae16/image/cdn?allowAnimated=true&client=5f4a70b1-9d9d-47c3-b388-87235680bb54&collection=contentId-349175812&height=470&max-age=2592000&mode=full-fit&source=mediaCard&token=eyJhbGciOiJIUzI1NiJ9.eyJpc3MiOiI1ZjRhNzBiMS05ZDlkLTQ3YzMtYjM4OC04NzIzNTY4MGJiNTQiLCJhY2Nlc3MiOnsidXJuOmZpbGVzdG9yZTpjb2xsZWN0aW9uOmNvbnRlbnRJZC0zNDkxNzU4MTIiOlsicmVhZCJdfSwiZXhwIjoxNzUwODY4NTQ4LCJuYmYiOjE3NTA4NjU2Njh9.48FAKcTsgApTgCA1vZLEHHhrTOBCRN6JOzHTpLWAO9o&width=760)
    
5.  The welder performs the weld.
    
6.  On the **Setup** tab the welder clicks the **Stratus** button.
    
    ![image-20250527-162151.png](https://media-cdn.atlassian.com/file/3a481a73-a596-4063-8f3e-a05ef6883991/image/cdn?allowAnimated=true&client=5f4a70b1-9d9d-47c3-b388-87235680bb54&collection=contentId-349175812&height=477&max-age=2592000&mode=full-fit&source=mediaCard&token=eyJhbGciOiJIUzI1NiJ9.eyJpc3MiOiI1ZjRhNzBiMS05ZDlkLTQ3YzMtYjM4OC04NzIzNTY4MGJiNTQiLCJhY2Nlc3MiOnsidXJuOmZpbGVzdG9yZTpjb2xsZWN0aW9uOmNvbnRlbnRJZC0zNDkxNzU4MTIiOlsicmVhZCJdfSwiZXhwIjoxNzUwODY4NTQ4LCJuYmYiOjE3NTA4NjU2Njh9.48FAKcTsgApTgCA1vZLEHHhrTOBCRN6JOzHTpLWAO9o&width=760)
    
7.  In the Stratus dialog, the welder clicks the **Complete** button.
    
    ![image-20250527-162344.png](https://media-cdn.atlassian.com/file/4e8b1fa3-9c8e-44a8-8a29-f589018997e6/image/cdn?allowAnimated=true&client=5f4a70b1-9d9d-47c3-b388-87235680bb54&collection=contentId-349175812&height=475&max-age=2592000&mode=full-fit&source=mediaCard&token=eyJhbGciOiJIUzI1NiJ9.eyJpc3MiOiI1ZjRhNzBiMS05ZDlkLTQ3YzMtYjM4OC04NzIzNTY4MGJiNTQiLCJhY2Nlc3MiOnsidXJuOmZpbGVzdG9yZTpjb2xsZWN0aW9uOmNvbnRlbnRJZC0zNDkxNzU4MTIiOlsicmVhZCJdfSwiZXhwIjoxNzUwODY4NTQ4LCJuYmYiOjE3NTA4NjU2Njh9.48FAKcTsgApTgCA1vZLEHHhrTOBCRN6JOzHTpLWAO9o&width=760)
    
8.  The part will be moved to **Completed List**.
    
    ![image-20250527-162456.png](https://media-cdn.atlassian.com/file/c069e047-0b99-4aab-a7e5-3b6fb3ec019d/image/cdn?allowAnimated=true&client=5f4a70b1-9d9d-47c3-b388-87235680bb54&collection=contentId-349175812&height=472&max-age=2592000&mode=full-fit&source=mediaCard&token=eyJhbGciOiJIUzI1NiJ9.eyJpc3MiOiI1ZjRhNzBiMS05ZDlkLTQ3YzMtYjM4OC04NzIzNTY4MGJiNTQiLCJhY2Nlc3MiOnsidXJuOmZpbGVzdG9yZTpjb2xsZWN0aW9uOmNvbnRlbnRJZC0zNDkxNzU4MTIiOlsicmVhZCJdfSwiZXhwIjoxNzUwODY4NTQ4LCJuYmYiOjE3NTA4NjU2Njh9.48FAKcTsgApTgCA1vZLEHHhrTOBCRN6JOzHTpLWAO9o&width=760)
    
9.  SWR communicates to Stratus that the weld was successfully completed. The part(s) Tracking Status is updated.
    

## SWR Stratus Dialog

Below is the SWR Stratus dialog mentioned in the [**Stratus to SWR Workflow**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/349175812/Novarc#%5BhardBreak%5DStratus-to-SWR-Workflow "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/349175812/Novarc#%5BhardBreak%5DStratus-to-SWR-Workflow") section.

![image-20250527-162955.png](https://media-cdn.atlassian.com/file/0401d18c-adfd-4c24-b715-8a1c57c6d088/image/cdn?allowAnimated=true&client=5f4a70b1-9d9d-47c3-b388-87235680bb54&collection=contentId-349175812&height=476&max-age=2592000&mode=full-fit&source=mediaCard&token=eyJhbGciOiJIUzI1NiJ9.eyJpc3MiOiI1ZjRhNzBiMS05ZDlkLTQ3YzMtYjM4OC04NzIzNTY4MGJiNTQiLCJhY2Nlc3MiOnsidXJuOmZpbGVzdG9yZTpjb2xsZWN0aW9uOmNvbnRlbnRJZC0zNDkxNzU4MTIiOlsicmVhZCJdfSwiZXhwIjoxNzUwODY4NTQ4LCJuYmYiOjE3NTA4NjU2Njh9.48FAKcTsgApTgCA1vZLEHHhrTOBCRN6JOzHTpLWAO9o&width=760)

1.  **Back** - returns to Setup screen
    
2.  **Waiting list** - List of parts queued to be welded by that SWR
    
3.  **Job information** - Shows the part currently selected to Weld. It matches the part seem  
    in the Setup screen
    
4.  **Completed list** - List of parts where the Weld was completed
    
5.  **Del** - Deletes the selected part from the list
    
6.  **Skip procedure** - Moves the selected part from Job Information to the bottom of the  
    Waiting List and the part on the top of the Waiting List to Job Information
    
7.  **Clear** - Removes all parts from the Waiting List and the part from Job Information
    
8.  **Complete** - Moves the part from Job Information to the Completed List
    
9.  **Completed List** - List of parts completed
    
10.  **Repeat Weld** - Moves the part on top of the Completed List back to Job Information  
    and the part from Job Information to the top of Waiting List
    

## Troubleshooting

**Q:** What if I completed a part by mistake?

**A:** The welder can click **Repeat Weld** if the part is on top of the Completed List. If it’s not, they are  
required to Send the part to the tool again from Stratus website.

**Q:** I see an incorrect tracking status in Stratus  
**A:** Feel free to delete. It does not cause any problem to the SWR

**Q:** The currently selected part is incorrect. How can I select another part?  
**A:** The welder can use the **Skip Procedure** button to switch the part with another one from the  
Waiting List.

**Q:** What happens if I close the SWR?  
**A:** The loaded queue will be lost. The part needs to be resent from Stratus website

# PypeServer - STRATUS Knowledge Base - Confluence

> ## Excerpt
> A .PSVR file can be generated and exported from Stratus and imported into PypeServer.  PSVR works from the Package's Cut Lists tab where a separate cut list PSVR file is generated for each material-diameter combination. Configuration of PSVR output relies on Admin > Company > Pipe Cuts settings, where the company's o-let hole sizes, connector bevel angles, etc. are entered.  PSVR cut list files are sent to a station configured for the PypeServer tool. See the Pipe Cuts (Admin) article for more infomation. The Pipe Cuts page describes the best practice configuration for AutoCAD and Revit and the Pipe Cuts configuration within Stratus. Pipe Cuts configuration is needed because it is difficult for PypeServer to determine whether a connector needs to be a bevel or plain angle cut. The process of downloading PSVR cut list files happens in the Shops > Station view. See the Shops Dashboard article for more information.

---
## Stratus / PypeServer .PSVR Output Workflow

A .PSVR file can be generated and exported from Stratus and imported into PypeServer.  PSVR works from the Package's Cut Lists tab where a separate cut list PSVR file is generated for each material-diameter combination. Configuration of PSVR output relies on Admin > Company > Pipe Cuts settings, where the company's o-let hole sizes, connector bevel angles, etc. are entered.  PSVR cut list files are sent to a station configured for the PypeServer tool. See the [**Pipe Cuts (Admin)**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/201490457 "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/201490457") article for more infomation. The Pipe Cuts page describes the best practice configuration for AutoCAD and Revit and the Pipe Cuts configuration within Stratus. Pipe Cuts configuration is needed because it is difficult for PypeServer to determine whether a connector needs to be a bevel or plain angle cut. The process of downloading PSVR cut list files happens in the Shops > Station view. See the [**Shops Dashboard**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/8913014 "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/8913014") article for more information.

Note: PCF output also works with PypeServer, but will always be a manual file export and relies on setting managed on the PypeServer side.

Before a .PSVR file can be generated, configure a PypeServer tool under Admin > Company > Tools. See the [**Tools**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/215220225 "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/215220225") article for more information. Below is an example. 

## Configure a Station

Before a .PSVR file can be generated, configure a Station that will run the cutting tool under Admin > Company > Stations. See the [**Stations**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/215220408 "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/215220408") article for more information. Below is an example. 

## Configure Pipe Cuts

Configuration of PSVR output relies on Admin > Company > Pipe Cuts settings, where the company's o-let hole sizes, connector bevel angles, etc. are entered. See the [**Pipe Cuts**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/201490457 "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/201490457") article for more information.

## Configure Cut List Mappings 

A Cut List Mappings for each Part Template must be configured to tell Stratus which data fields to use.

**To configure a Cut List Mapping:** 

1.  Got to Admin > Company > Part Templates. 
    
2.  In the Parts section, select or search for Part Template Name.  
    
    1.  **Hint**:  To determine a Part Template Name, in any Stratus viewer, open the Properties tool, select the part, and then locate the Template Name.  
        
        ![](blob:https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/69d273aa-77ed-402a-a957-67f44e16896e)
        
3.  **Select** the Part Template and then click the **Cut List Mappings** tab.   
    
    ![](blob:https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/29e6abcd-59ed-435a-a16c-e3f71b9ee03d)
    
4.  In the **Consider for Multi-Axis Cut Lists** section, select a part parameter from your database that contains the data for each field. The parameters that need to be selected will vary depending the type of part selected. 
    
    1.  **Straight Pipe** fields:  
        
        ![](blob:https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/d5a57187-f622-4fe7-b3d9-3c50b46ce1e2)
        
    2.  **Saddle** fields:  
        
        ![](blob:https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/5f646d28-bb46-4f69-9bcb-cf4443be65c1)
        
    3.  **Revit Family Content - Pipes Pipe Type (No Fabrication Content)**   
        **Create Project Parameters (Required)**  
        Stratus uses the Revit API to extract data from the model. Diameter and Pipe End Connector parameters must be defined in Revit as a project parameter so that the data can be injected into the part. The project parameter tells Stratus where to look for the parameter in your model.
        
        1.  Stratus uses the Inside and Outside Diameter.  
            
            ![](blob:https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/1ed6a4a4-bc27-454f-8a22-0ebebfa44c2a)
            
        2.  Companies need to map a project parameter to the Segment and Sizes.  
            
            ![](blob:https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/8968c198-f6a1-4165-960b-498fbe3ed03e)
            
    4.  **Revit Family Content – Shaped Nipple**   
        The Shaped Nipple is similar to the Pipes Pipe Type but an Olet Type also needs to be selected.  
        
        ![](blob:https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/326c6a5d-22fb-4717-aa57-8d169b738f2b)
        

## Generate a .PSVR output file

To generate a .PSVR file: 

1.  Open a package that includes straight pipe along with Connectors, Saddles, or Olets. 
    
2.  With the package open, click the **Cut Lists** tab.  
    
3.  To enable the **Generate Cut List** button, check that the package is set with a “**Can Cut List**” tracking status. See the [**Tracking Statuses (Admin)**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/10485761 "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/10485761") article for more information.
    
4.  Click the **Generate Cut List** button.  
    
5.  The cut list will display.  
    
    ![](blob:https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/8192750c-bb84-4a6c-b2a0-4933b79092b5)
    
    1.  For each cut list row that will be sent to a PypeServer cutting machine, select the correct **Station.**  See the [**Station (Admin)**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/215220408 "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/215220408") article for more information.
        
    2.  Check the rows that will be sent to the station. 
        
    3.  Click the **Send Cut List to Station** button. 
        
    4.  Click **OK** on the Send Cut Lists dialog box.
        
6.  Cut List files are organized under the **Shops** tab.  
    
7.  On the Shops > Dashboard, select the **Shop.** A list of Stations for the Shop display.   
    
    ![](blob:https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/3b50ffc5-d440-41ae-962c-440c2f1ec4df)
    
8.  Click the **Station** name and a list of requested cut lists will display.
    
9.  Click the **Send to Tool** button associated with the Cut List. A PSVR file will be created for each material-diameter combination.    
    
    ![](blob:https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/3c89027d-cb16-43a5-8741-98bd340a9b0b)
    
10.  The .PSVR file will be a downloaded by your web browser.
    
11.  The Job Value in the .PSVR file with the Stratus Package Name.  
    
    ![](blob:https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/241eea9b-6b0c-447a-bfcb-ea938a1bacec)
    
    **How to use the .PSVR file**
    
12.  Locate the downloaded .PSVR file and save it to a location that can be used by the PypeServer software. 
    
13.  The CAD department loads the .PSVR file into the PypeServer software. 
    
14.  PypeServer’s powerful tools can be used to prepare the pipe to be cut. 
    
15.  Auto-nest the cut list and PypeServer will optimize nesting. 
    
16.  When ready to cut, Load to Machine and enter the Heat number. 
    
17.  The pipe staging tool instructs the operator to Align the torch centerline. 
    
18.  And when ready, the operator starts the cutting tool at the gantry. 
    

## Generate a .PSVR File after Using Spool Checker

When using Spool Checker under Assemblies > Assembly > Spool Checker Tool, modifications at either end of the pipe will be reconciled with relative dimensional references. For the initiated, lengths can be affected at either the C1 or C2 end. This means that length will be taken up or given on the correct end of the pipe depending on the locked part scenario you are dealing with in the Spool Checker. This delivers feature parity to ITM and Revit pipe for multi-axis pipe cut file generation.

You can see 2” being taken off of either end of what was originally a 60” part in the screenshots below:

## Stratus OpenAPI

For information about how to integrate the [**Stratus OpenAPI**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/1829077164/STRATUS+API "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/1829077164/STRATUS+API") with PypeServer, please contact the [**Stratus Service Desk**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/servicedesk/customer/portal/3 "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/servicedesk/customer/portal/3")**.**

# PypeServer Connect Cloudinator - STRATUS Knowledge Base - Confluence

> ## Excerpt
> Stratus is integrated with PypeServer Connect Cloudinator.

---
## PypeServer Connect Cloudinator

Stratus is integrated with **PypeServer Connect Cloudinator.**

To create a Stratus Package using the **PypeServer Connect Cloudinator**:

1.  Configure **PypeServer Connect Cloudinator:**
    
    1.  Install **PypeServer Connect Cloudinator**.
        
    2.  Open **PypeServer Connect Cloudinator**.
        
    3.  Click the **Application Settings** button.  
        
        ![](blob:https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/4db2c503-9753-4dd6-b31d-50e0daafdfd2)
        
    4.  Click **Service Connections** and enter your GTP Stratus APP Key found in Stratus under Admin > Company > App Keys whose Partner App is PypeServer.
        
        ![](blob:https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/3451e056-159e-4ea8-aa49-abed42a33bdd#media-blob-url=true&id=40645f15-48d2-4b04-92d5-38081ba3643c&collection=contentId-2248474625&contextId=2248474625&mimeType=image%2Fpng&name=image2024-9-5_14-46-40.png&size=48424&width=904&height=604&alt=)
        
    5.  When done, click **OK**.
        
2.  **In PypeServer Connect Cloudinator**:
    
    1.  Follow the screen prompts to Browse or drag/drop .PDF, PCF, or other files into the dialog.
        
        ![](blob:https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/aa6866c7-26e0-448d-9404-3dc35086bb07#media-blob-url=true&id=6de8e2e6-fdb3-4974-8871-9096fb99d7ad&collection=contentId-2248474625&contextId=2248474625&mimeType=image%2Fpng&name=image2024-9-5_14-47-9.png&size=50914&width=604&height=604&alt=)
        
    2.  Click **Upload** when done.
        
    3.  The **GTP Stratus** tab will display.
        
        ![](https://media-cdn.atlassian.com/file/26ffc8d6-b9dc-44ee-8d6a-5d876726705c/image/cdn?allowAnimated=true&client=5f4a70b1-9d9d-47c3-b388-87235680bb54&collection=contentId-2248474625&height=737&max-age=2592000&mode=full-fit&source=mediaCard&token=eyJhbGciOiJIUzI1NiJ9.eyJpc3MiOiI1ZjRhNzBiMS05ZDlkLTQ3YzMtYjM4OC04NzIzNTY4MGJiNTQiLCJhY2Nlc3MiOnsidXJuOmZpbGVzdG9yZTpjb2xsZWN0aW9uOmNvbnRlbnRJZC0yMjQ4NDc0NjI1IjpbInJlYWQiXX0sImV4cCI6MTc1MDg2ODU1NSwibmJmIjoxNzUwODY1Njc1fQ.kQztZFk3U7xth3s44I4Td_augAJrCvs-DmtzlPA96ew&width=760)
        
        1.  Select the Stratus **Project**, **Model**, enter **Package Name**, **Package Number (optional)**, and select a **Package Category**.
            
    4.  Click **OK**. When the upload is complete, a message similar to the following will display. Click **OK**.
        
        ![](https://media-cdn.atlassian.com/file/53f1eb21-9c0e-4a69-9713-702ae0b18edd/image/cdn?allowAnimated=true&client=5f4a70b1-9d9d-47c3-b388-87235680bb54&collection=contentId-2248474625&height=278&max-age=2592000&mode=full-fit&source=mediaCard&token=eyJhbGciOiJIUzI1NiJ9.eyJpc3MiOiI1ZjRhNzBiMS05ZDlkLTQ3YzMtYjM4OC04NzIzNTY4MGJiNTQiLCJhY2Nlc3MiOnsidXJuOmZpbGVzdG9yZTpjb2xsZWN0aW9uOmNvbnRlbnRJZC0yMjQ4NDc0NjI1IjpbInJlYWQiXX0sImV4cCI6MTc1MDg2ODU1NSwibmJmIjoxNzUwODY1Njc1fQ.kQztZFk3U7xth3s44I4Td_augAJrCvs-DmtzlPA96ew&width=760)
        
3.  **In Stratus:**
    
    1.  The uploaded package will display on the Packages > Dashboard.
        
        ![](https://media-cdn.atlassian.com/file/035fdfbf-846b-40ef-b267-a584b5ea0b73/image/cdn?allowAnimated=true&client=5f4a70b1-9d9d-47c3-b388-87235680bb54&collection=contentId-2248474625&height=286&max-age=2592000&mode=full-fit&source=mediaCard&token=eyJhbGciOiJIUzI1NiJ9.eyJpc3MiOiI1ZjRhNzBiMS05ZDlkLTQ3YzMtYjM4OC04NzIzNTY4MGJiNTQiLCJhY2Nlc3MiOnsidXJuOmZpbGVzdG9yZTpjb2xsZWN0aW9uOmNvbnRlbnRJZC0yMjQ4NDc0NjI1IjpbInJlYWQiXX0sImV4cCI6MTc1MDg2ODU1NSwibmJmIjoxNzUwODY1Njc1fQ.kQztZFk3U7xth3s44I4Td_augAJrCvs-DmtzlPA96ew&width=1024)
        
    2.  Click the Package Number or Name to open the package.
        
        1.  The PDF file will display in the Packages > Viewer
            
        2.  The uploaded .PDF and .PSVR files will display in the **Attachments** tab. **Note**: A .PSVR file is attached for each material and size.
            
            ![](https://media-cdn.atlassian.com/file/a72b0abc-c46f-4c2f-a6b2-d230cc4b857a/image/cdn?allowAnimated=true&client=5f4a70b1-9d9d-47c3-b388-87235680bb54&collection=contentId-2248474625&height=473&max-age=2592000&mode=full-fit&source=mediaCard&token=eyJhbGciOiJIUzI1NiJ9.eyJpc3MiOiI1ZjRhNzBiMS05ZDlkLTQ3YzMtYjM4OC04NzIzNTY4MGJiNTQiLCJhY2Nlc3MiOnsidXJuOmZpbGVzdG9yZTpjb2xsZWN0aW9uOmNvbnRlbnRJZC0yMjQ4NDc0NjI1IjpbInJlYWQiXX0sImV4cCI6MTc1MDg2ODU1NSwibmJmIjoxNzUwODY1Njc1fQ.kQztZFk3U7xth3s44I4Td_augAJrCvs-DmtzlPA96ew&width=1024)
            
        3.  The uploaded .PSVR files will display in the **Cut Lists** tab. **Note**: A cut list will be created for each material and size.
            
            ![](https://media-cdn.atlassian.com/file/608b8709-a47f-4ace-b560-cfd1d5a5d108/image/cdn?allowAnimated=true&client=5f4a70b1-9d9d-47c3-b388-87235680bb54&collection=contentId-2248474625&height=379&max-age=2592000&mode=full-fit&source=mediaCard&token=eyJhbGciOiJIUzI1NiJ9.eyJpc3MiOiI1ZjRhNzBiMS05ZDlkLTQ3YzMtYjM4OC04NzIzNTY4MGJiNTQiLCJhY2Nlc3MiOnsidXJuOmZpbGVzdG9yZTpjb2xsZWN0aW9uOmNvbnRlbnRJZC0yMjQ4NDc0NjI1IjpbInJlYWQiXX0sImV4cCI6MTc1MDg2ODU1NSwibmJmIjoxNzUwODY1Njc1fQ.kQztZFk3U7xth3s44I4Td_augAJrCvs-DmtzlPA96ew&width=1024)
            
            1.  Select the PypeServer **Station** for each Cut List.
                
                ![](https://media-cdn.atlassian.com/file/200e57f3-c8e0-4b05-8f6d-86542a513779/image/cdn?allowAnimated=true&client=5f4a70b1-9d9d-47c3-b388-87235680bb54&collection=contentId-2248474625&height=430&max-age=2592000&mode=full-fit&source=mediaCard&token=eyJhbGciOiJIUzI1NiJ9.eyJpc3MiOiI1ZjRhNzBiMS05ZDlkLTQ3YzMtYjM4OC04NzIzNTY4MGJiNTQiLCJhY2Nlc3MiOnsidXJuOmZpbGVzdG9yZTpjb2xsZWN0aW9uOmNvbnRlbnRJZC0yMjQ4NDc0NjI1IjpbInJlYWQiXX0sImV4cCI6MTc1MDg2ODU1NSwibmJmIjoxNzUwODY1Njc1fQ.kQztZFk3U7xth3s44I4Td_augAJrCvs-DmtzlPA96ew&width=1024)
                
            2.  Click the **Send Cut List to Station** button. Note: The Package Status may need to be changed to a status that has **Can Cut List** checked before the **Send Cut List to Station** button will be enabled.
                
                ![](https://media-cdn.atlassian.com/file/eef730c5-c561-4dbb-a26c-7f57eff515cb/image/cdn?allowAnimated=true&client=5f4a70b1-9d9d-47c3-b388-87235680bb54&collection=contentId-2248474625&height=437&max-age=2592000&mode=full-fit&source=mediaCard&token=eyJhbGciOiJIUzI1NiJ9.eyJpc3MiOiI1ZjRhNzBiMS05ZDlkLTQ3YzMtYjM4OC04NzIzNTY4MGJiNTQiLCJhY2Nlc3MiOnsidXJuOmZpbGVzdG9yZTpjb2xsZWN0aW9uOmNvbnRlbnRJZC0yMjQ4NDc0NjI1IjpbInJlYWQiXX0sImV4cCI6MTc1MDg2ODU1NSwibmJmIjoxNzUwODY1Njc1fQ.kQztZFk3U7xth3s44I4Td_augAJrCvs-DmtzlPA96ew&width=1024)
                
        4.  Work with the Cut List in the Shops tab where you can Send to Tool, Print Labels, or Unassign from Station.
            
            ![](https://media-cdn.atlassian.com/file/dd1ffebf-75a9-4365-a779-f52505c1b638/image/cdn?allowAnimated=true&client=5f4a70b1-9d9d-47c3-b388-87235680bb54&collection=contentId-2248474625&height=346&max-age=2592000&mode=full-fit&source=mediaCard&token=eyJhbGciOiJIUzI1NiJ9.eyJpc3MiOiI1ZjRhNzBiMS05ZDlkLTQ3YzMtYjM4OC04NzIzNTY4MGJiNTQiLCJhY2Nlc3MiOnsidXJuOmZpbGVzdG9yZTpjb2xsZWN0aW9uOmNvbnRlbnRJZC0yMjQ4NDc0NjI1IjpbInJlYWQiXX0sImV4cCI6MTc1MDg2ODU1NSwibmJmIjoxNzUwODY1Njc1fQ.kQztZFk3U7xth3s44I4Td_augAJrCvs-DmtzlPA96ew&width=1024)
            
        5.  **Send to Tool** - Click **Send to Tool** to download the PSVR file. The package Tracking Status will be updated to **In Progress**.
            
            ![](https://media-cdn.atlassian.com/file/a6bedeee-9559-4b3b-9067-e5d0af07c8be/image/cdn?allowAnimated=true&client=5f4a70b1-9d9d-47c3-b388-87235680bb54&collection=contentId-2248474625&height=365&max-age=2592000&mode=full-fit&source=mediaCard&token=eyJhbGciOiJIUzI1NiJ9.eyJpc3MiOiI1ZjRhNzBiMS05ZDlkLTQ3YzMtYjM4OC04NzIzNTY4MGJiNTQiLCJhY2Nlc3MiOnsidXJuOmZpbGVzdG9yZTpjb2xsZWN0aW9uOmNvbnRlbnRJZC0yMjQ4NDc0NjI1IjpbInJlYWQiXX0sImV4cCI6MTc1MDg2ODU1NSwibmJmIjoxNzUwODY1Njc1fQ.kQztZFk3U7xth3s44I4Td_augAJrCvs-DmtzlPA96ew&width=1024)

# QR Code Scanned Page - STRATUS Knowledge Base - Confluence

> ## Excerpt
> When a QR Code is scanned and the user is not using the Scan page, a QR Code Scanned page will display. Alternatively, a user can copy/paste a QR Code into the browser's address field. Depending on whether the scanned item was a Part, Assembly, Package, or Container will determine which QR Code Scanned page will display.

---
## 

-   1[Part QR Code Scanned](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/1890025473/QR+Code+Scanned+Page#QRCodeScannedPage-PartQRCodeScanned)
-   2[Assembly QR Code Scanned](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/1890025473/QR+Code+Scanned+Page#QRCodeScannedPage-AssemblyQRCodeScanned)
-   3[Package QR Code Scanned](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/1890025473/QR+Code+Scanned+Page#QRCodeScannedPage-PackageQRCodeScanned)
-   4[Container QR Code Scanned](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/1890025473/QR+Code+Scanned+Page#QRCodeScannedPage-ContainerQRCodeScanned)

When a QR Code is scanned and the user is not using the **[Scan](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/158040194/Scan)** page, a **QR Code Scanned** page will display. Alternatively, a user can copy/paste a QR Code into the browser's address field. Depending on whether the scanned item was a Part, Assembly, Package, or Container will determine which QR Code Scanned page will display. 

## Part QR Code Scanned

When a part QR Code is scanned to a web browser address, the Part QR Code Scanned page will display.![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/1890025473/image2022-5-25_12-10-42.png?version=1&modificationDate=1653498643826&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=1200&height=713)

1.  **Project** - The Project name.
2.  **Model** - The Model name.
3.  **Package** \- If the part is included in a Package, the Package name will display.
4.  **Assembly** - If the part is included in an Assembly, the Assembly name will display.
5.  **Description** - The Part Description.
6.  **Number** - The Part Number, if any, will display.
7.  **View Package** - If the part is included in a Package, the **View Package** button will display. When the **View Package** button is clicked, the Packages > Viewer page related to the part will display.
8.  **View Assembly** - If the part is included in an Assembly, the **View Assembly** button will display. When the **View Assembly** button is clicked, the Assemblies > Viewer page related to the part will display.
9.  **Add Assembly on Scan** - The **Add Assembly on Scan** page only displays when the part is included in an assembly. By checking this checkbox, when the part is contained in an assembly, any changes made in Tracking will be applied to all parts in the assembly.
10.  **Tracking** - When the **Apply** button is clicked for a tracking change the change will be applied to the part. If the **Add Assembly on Scan** checkbox is checked, then the tracking change will also be applied to all of the parts in the assembly.
11.  **Attachments** - Displays information about the part attachment and a link to the attachment.

## Assembly QR Code Scanned

When an Assembly QR Code is scanned to a web browser address, the Assembly QR Code Scanned page will display.

![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/1890025473/image2022-5-25_12-19-40.png?version=1&modificationDate=1653499182055&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=1200&height=701)

1.  **Project** - The Project name.
2.  **Model** - The Model name.
3.  **Package** \- If the assembly is included in a Package, the Package name will display.
4.  **Assembly** - If the part is included in an Assembly, the Assembly name will display.
5.  **View Package** - If the assembly is included in a Package, the **View Package** button will display. When the **View Package** button is clicked, the Packages > Viewer page related to the assembly will display.
6.  **View Assembly** - When the **View Assembly** button is clicked, the Assemblies > Viewer page related to the assembly will display.
7.  **View Location** \- When the **View Location** button is clicked, the Models > Viewer page will display.
8.  **Tracking** - When the **Apply** button is clicked for a tracking change the change will be applied to the assembly and all of its parts.
9.  **Attachments** - Displays information about the part and assembly attachments, if any, and a link to the attachment.

## Package QR Code Scanned

When a Package QR Code is scanned to a web browser address, the Package QR Code Scanned page will display.

![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/1890025473/image2022-5-25_13-11-33.png?version=1&modificationDate=1653502294565&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=1200&height=669)

1.  **Project** - The Project name.
2.  **Model** - The Model name.
3.  **Package** \- The Package name will display.
4.  **View Package** - If the assembly is included in a Package, the **View Package** button will display. When the **View Package** button is clicked, the Packages > Viewer page related to the assembly will display.
5.  **Tracking** - When the **Apply** button is clicked for a tracking change the change will be applied to the package and all of its parts.
6.  **Attachments** - Displays information about the part and assembly attachments, if any, and a link to the attachment.

## Container QR Code Scanned

When a Container QR Code is scanned to a web browser address, the Container QR Code Scanned page will display. In this example, the QR Code for the container (Pallet 01) was scanned. Since the Pallet 01 container is included in an Outer Container (Truck B), the View Outer Container information displays.

![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/1890025473/image2022-5-25_13-21-33.png?version=1&modificationDate=1653502894603&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=1200&height=603)

1.  **View Outer Container** - Opens the Outer Container under Containers > Assign.
2.  **Update Contents** - Opens the container under Containers > Assign.
3.  **Empty Container** - Empties the container of all items. The user will be prompted to start a new Tracking Log for the container. Click **OK** to delete Tracking information.
4.  **Tracking** - When the **Apply** button is clicked for a tracking change the change will be applied to the container.
---

# QR Code on CAMduct Label - STRATUS Knowledge Base - Confluence

> ## Excerpt
> Q:     How can I embed a Stratus QR Code on CAMduct labels.

---
> **Q:**     How can I embed a Stratus QR Code on CAMduct labels. 
> 
> **A:**     To print CAMduct labels with a Stratus QR code:
> 
> 1\. In Stratus under **Admin** > **Company** > **Settings**, enter a custom data field name for the **Property to Map to QR Code** setting under the Common to AutoCAD and Revit section (Ex. QR Code).  
> 
> ![](blob:https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/75076e48-caaf-442c-8083-46b2baba5364)
> 
> 2\. In Fabrication, add a custom data field, with the exact same spelling as the Stratus Property to Map to QR Code, under **Edit Main Database** > **Takeoff** > **Custom Data** (Ex. QR Code).  
> 
> ![](blob:https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/1b3d53d5-4d34-4c35-b648-2816e2561be0)
> 
> 3\. In CAMduct, under **File** > **Print Layout** > **Labels**, you can create a new label. In this example, click/drag the Item Custom Data Field onto your label.  
> 
> ![](blob:https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/3832c246-0689-47ca-8a04-485e758fd262)
> 
> 4\. In CAMduct, under Object Properties:
> 
> a. Set the **Data** to the name / index # for the Custom Data field created in Fabrication above (Ex. QR Code).  
> 
> ![](blob:https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/71912c5c-eecf-4809-a11c-11c833441e10)
> 
> ![](blob:https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/c2a2c3ba-e559-4280-85b8-3a53e61a3441)
> 
> 5\. A QR code example will display on the label.  
> 
> ![](blob:https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/ef907dfa-99f3-4f51-a955-0ba3d21571e0)
> 
>   
> 6\. Before you can preview the QR code, open a CADmep drawing that has been published to Stratus. Click the **Import** button on the GTP Stratus add-in to assign the Stratus Property to Map to QR Code to each part’s CADmep Custom Data field defined above.
> 
> 7\. Go to the CAMduct Print Preview and select the label.  A preview similar to the following will display. The QR Code is linked to Stratus. You can scan the QR code to update tracking status or view a Stratus landing page will display where you can view the part in the model.  
> 
> ![](blob:https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/ab8b4c35-4d38-4dde-b035-f8ac80b02aac)
> 
> **Q:**     How can I use the MAJ directly from Stratus? 
> 
> **A:**     The QR Code is written to the External  Link field on the Item at position 1 when the MAJ is generated. Using this requires setting up the Label in a slightly different way where the External Link field is used and set the Data Index to 1.
> 
> ![](blob:https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/969c3eb9-9b05-453e-a3f0-5db7428755f7)
---

author:
