## 05 December 2024 - 7.5.1022 (Release was rolled back to 7.5.1018)

Fixed An issue was causing some reports to take a long time to generate.

Fixed An issue was causing assembly creation to take a long time.

Fixed An issue was popping up an “Object reference not set to the instance of an object” while using Spool Checker.

## 01 December 2024 - 7.5.1018

Fixed When removing an assembly/package from a container, the tracking status of the assembly/package was being reverted to its previous status.

## 20 November 2024 - 7.5.1017

**Please** [**update**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2122022926 "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2122022926") **your Stratus desktop software to version 7.5.1001 or later. Older versions will no longer be supported. This includes the Stratus Addin for publishing, Stratus Workstation, Stratus Print, and Lightning (v7.5.103) apps.**

ADDED The package and assembly viewers now support viewing image files (.png and .jpg) as attachments for packages and assemblies that do not contain parts.

ADDED Updated PDF rendering when an assembly does not include any parts, but does include a PDF attachment, the PDF will render in the viewer. Note: This functionality already exists when a package does not include any parts, but does include a PDF attachment, the PDF renders in the viewer.

update Empty assemblies can now be seen in Package Assembly report tables.

update Filter Rule Conditions:

1.  Added a 'Case Sensitive” option checkbox and removed the rules **ContainsAnyCase** and **DoesNotContainAnyCase**. We swapped any existing filters and checked the corresponding checkboxes during the deployment.
    
2.  Added new Rule Conditions including:
    
    1.  DoesNotStartWith
        
    2.  EndsWith
        
    3.  DoesNotEndWith
        
    4.  Regex (See [https://regex101.com/](https://regex101.com/ "https://regex101.com/") for more information)
        
        1.  RegexMatch
            
        2.  DoesNotRegexMatch
            

Fixed In rare cases, Assembly Stratus Sheets in a Master Report were showing annotation lines from the Package Assembly Tags when run from the package viewer or as an automated report generated by Tracking Status changes configured in the Package Categories tab of the Company Admin.

Fixed Increased performance in the speed of creating assemblies and displaying certain reports.

## 06 November 2024 - 7.5.1014 (Release was rolled back to 7.5.1013)

update The first phase of a long-term effort towards simplifying our reporting engine codebase has gone live.

Increased performance in the speed of creating assemblies and displaying certain reports.

Fixed Fixed an issue running a report that includes a Field with an Alias.

## 24 October 2024 - 7.5.1013

update Updated Part Report > Report Fields where **Aggregate** is either Sum or Average and **Merge Like Values** is set to Yes to ensure that the total is based on having a common Description, Material and Size.

update Updated backend report engine code. This change may impact client code written against our Open API for pulling down reports.

**Warning:** When generating reports with the Open API, some fields will now result in strings being empty vs. null. This change may impact client parsing software that operates on data from our Open API.

Fixed Fixed an issue selecting nested families in a Viewer Filter.

Fixed Fixed an issue adding/removing nested family parts to/from an assembly or package.

Fixed Fixed a Container Details report issue when a Report Fields **Merge Like Values** was set to Yes, the report now displays the merged sum and quantity.

Fixed Fixed an issue where a Filters Grouping was applied to a ZPL (label) report, the alphanumeric order was incorrect.

Fixed Fixed an Admin > Company > Part Templates issue where after selecting 2 or more Parts, then in the **Shared Properties** tab editing a property, the edits now correctly save for the selected parts.

## 14 October 2024 - 7.5.1011

ADDED A new Field format called _QRCode_ has been added to reports. When this format is used in a report, the value of the field/property will be rendered as a QR code in the Stratus UI and in generated PDFs. When the report type is CSV, the value of the field/property will still be rendered as a string.

ADDED New API call for creating a new assembly.

-   POST /v1/model/{id}/assembly
    

ADDED 2 new API endpoints used to automate project import from Autodesk and project creation in Stratus and control over project role assignments for the new project.

-   GET /v1/project/autodesk-projects
    
-   POST /v1/project
    

ADDED A new tool type called “Lockformer Spiral” has been added.

ADDED AsMetric() Field Function which converts a numeric value from feet units to metric mm, cm, or m units and also control the number of decimal places displayed in the resulting string.

Examples:  
AsMetric({Length})

AsMetric({Length},2)

AsMetric({Length},2,2)

where the 2nd and 3rd arguments are optional as specified above

ADDED Markups Project Role permissions (Create & Edit, Delete, and View) in both Assemblies and Packages Attachments.

update Admin > Company > Big Data > Analytics Reports to include Service Principal Authentication fields (Optional).

update Publish to include the Fabrication Data property “Item Drawing Name” value which will display in Stratus Properties.

update Naming conventions part property dropdown performance improvement.

update Attachment filenames that contain invalid characters which will be replaced with an underscore so they can successfully be uploaded to ACC/BIM 360.

## 8 October 2024 - 7.5.1010

update Resolved an issue with authentication access tokens that were causing brief outages.

## 7 October 2024 - 7.5.1008

Fixed An issue where, when editing a field, random characters appeared in the field expression.

## 6 October 2024 - 7.5.1007

-   Both the Stratus Addin and Workstation applications have available updates.
    
-   **Remember, all Stratus software must be on version 7.5.1001 or later by October 18th as previous versions will no longer be supported.**
    

ADDED A checkbox setting called Exclude Imports into Fabrication Item Number Property to the \[Company Admin > Settings > AutoCAD, Revit… > Specific to Revit\] page directly under the Property to Map to Item Number setting.

When enabled the Stratus Revit addin will NOT import your Stratus.Part.Number values into the Fabrication Item Number property. This can be useful when using Revit groups as they do not support unique Item Number values on parts contained within them.

ADDED The Stratus Community feed was added to the homepage.

Fixed 2D views included in the Revit publish set will be visible in the model viewer’s View droplist and visible in Stratus.

Fixed All reports will now honor your defined sort indices.

Fixed An issue where markups were not landing at where expected.

Fixed An issue where the advanced estimating metrics were not showing when creating a package.

Fixed Excel exports of part reports were missing data.

Fixed Groupings in a filter were missing some values in the Company Filters UI.

Fixed Scope box selection was not working in the Project Areas graphical selector.

Fixed Some PDF Reports were not downloading.

Fixed Some reports with multiple groupings were failing when one of those grouper properties had empty values.

Fixed Some tags were not displaying in Stratus Sheets.

Fixed Stratus Sheets were missing the Hidden Parts Shaded content.

Fixed The annotations endpoint for packages were returning no annotations in some cases.

Fixed View orientation between Stratus Sheets and the Model Viewer were not being maintained.

Fixed Workstations filtering was breaking import cut lists.

update Adjusted Length tags were overlapping with their leaders.

update General API Improvements

update Performance improvements on the Fields admin page.

update The JSON type has been removed as a report format.

## 2 September 2024 - 7.4.1010

ADDED A new property called STRATUS.Part.HoleInfoType can now be used that expands what the current STRATUS.Part.HoleInfo property contains by adding the Olet type for each hole using an abbreviation

-   DEF = Default
    
-   COP = Cooplet
    
-   SOC = Sockolet
    
-   THR = Threadolet
    
-   WLD = Weldolet
    
-   SAD = Saddle
    

update Project Roles are now limiting the available statuses that an individual can use when scanning to update tracking statuses

## 19 August 2024 - 7.4.1006

ADDED In data tables such as the package dashboard or parts reports, when certain report fields are merged, the values in the cells of the non-merged report fields will be organized in alpha-numerical order. For example, if there is a report with a column merged based on ‘Stratus.Part.Number’ and another column for ‘Material,’ the values within the ‘Material’ column will be sorted alpha-numerically. This means that within the ‘Material’ column, ‘Carbon Steel’ would be listed before ‘Copper’ due to the alpha-numerical sorting criteria applied to that field.

update Incremental update for Flex model publishing (only required if testing Flex model viewer)

-   [GTP Software Installers](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2122022926)

# Stratus FLEX: Iso Sketch - STRATUS Knowledge Base - Confluence

> ## Excerpt
> The dashboard showcases all of your existing sketches. From here, you can easily delete, duplicate, or create a package using your sketch.

---
The dashboard showcases all of your existing sketches. From here, you can easily delete, duplicate, or create a package using your sketch.

On the right side of the page, you have access to a variety of tools. Currently, you can create tags, add dimensions, insert valves, fittings, and unions, as well as delete, undo, and redo actions.

To draw a pipe, simply ensure no tools are selected and drag your finger between two points. To add annotations or valves/fittings, select the appropriate tool from the right side of the screen and follow the tooltips located at the bottom right corner for guidance.

# Stratus FLEX: Package Dashboard - STRATUS Knowledge Base - Confluence

> ## Excerpt
> 

---
[

![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/attachments/32771/global.logo?version=3&modificationDate=1516734801783&cacheVersion=1&api=v2)

](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/overview?homepageId=33347)

-    This trigger is hidden

Results will update as you type.

You‘re viewing this with anonymous access, so some content might be blocked.

Stratus FLEX: Package Dashboard

## Stratus FLEX: Package Dashboard

With FLEX's Package Dashboard, updating package statuses offline ensures flawless communication between the site and the office. Boost efficiency, reduce errors, and stay on track, regardless of connectivity. Your field operations are now truly uninterrupted with FLEX.

Here is an example of what your _Package Dashboard_ might look like based on the limitations defined in your Stratus _Project Role_

Tap the **Filters** button to display the available filters, which can help you limit the packages displayed in the dashboard.

Tap an individual status button for a package to update the **Stratus** _Tracking Status._

Tap on multiple package rows to highlight them.

With multiple packages highlighted, tap the **Update Status** button at the top-right corner of the screen to update the Stratus _Tracking Status_ on all of them simultaneously.

You can view your package attachments by selecting the three dots on the right of the Package Dashboard. Select an attachment to view it in FLEX.

## Package Creation

The new Package button will be enabled whenever the device is connected to the internet.

The new Package button opens a menu to define your package properties and upload attachments. The package will be available on the Stratus website at the time of creation.

# Stratus FLEX: Scan Page - STRATUS Knowledge Base - Confluence

> ## Excerpt
> FLEX's QR scanning elevates installation tracking to the next level. Field personnel can swiftly update the installation status of Parts, Assemblies, and Packages through seamless scans of QR code labels. This feature enhances field-to-office communication, ensures accurate installation updates, and reduces errors. This feature not only speeds up the process but also ensures tracking accuracy.

---
FLEX's QR scanning elevates installation tracking to the next level. Field personnel can swiftly update the installation status of Parts, Assemblies, and Packages through seamless scans of QR code labels. This feature enhances field-to-office communication, ensures accurate installation updates, and reduces errors. This feature not only speeds up the process but also ensures tracking accuracy.

Tap on the **QR Scan** button on the lefthand navigation bar to enter QR scanning mode.

Scan QR codes for containers, packages, assemblies, or parts. Parts in an assembly will bring up the assembly, and parts that are not will show as standalone parts.

Tap on an individual status button for a card to update the **Stratus** _Tracking Status._

Tap on multiple cards to highlight them.

With multiple cards highlighted, tap on the **Update** button in the top-right corner of the screen to update the Stratus _Tracking Status_ on multiple items simultaneously.

Regardless of what project is active, if you have an internet connection and scan a Stratus QR code, it will populate data similar to the Scan page on Stratus. As you scan QR codes, the data for those codes will be downloaded while you continue to scan. There is no need to wait for the previous scan to finish loading before scanning your next QR code.

# Stratus FLEX: Settings - STRATUS Knowledge Base - Confluence

> ## Excerpt
> The Settings page in Stratus FLEX is a central hub for customizing and optimizing your experience within the application.

---
-   1 [Settings](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2294317075/Stratus+FLEX+Settings#Settings)
    -   1.1 [General Settings](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2294317075/Stratus+FLEX+Settings#General-Settings)
        -   1.1.1 [Date and Time Settings](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2294317075/Stratus+FLEX+Settings#Date-and-Time-Settings)
        -   1.1.2 [QR Scanning Type](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2294317075/Stratus+FLEX+Settings#QR-Scanning-Type)
    -   1.2 [Download Manager](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2294317075/Stratus+FLEX+Settings#Download-Manager)
        -   1.2.1 [QR Codes](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2294317075/Stratus+FLEX+Settings#QR-Codes)
        -   1.2.2 [Package Attachments](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2294317075/Stratus+FLEX+Settings#Package-Attachments)
        -   1.2.3 [Downloaded Projects](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2294317075/Stratus+FLEX+Settings#Downloaded-Projects)

## Settings

The **Settings** page in Stratus FLEX is a central hub for customizing and optimizing your experience within the application.

## General Settings

Within the **General** section of the settings page, users have access to several fundamental settings that affect the overall operation of the application.

### Date and Time Settings

The date and time settings are synchronized with the Date and Time Settings in your Stratus [Account Settings](https://www.gtpstratus.com/account#tab_profile. "https://www.gtpstratus.com/account#tab_profile.").

### QR Scanning Type

Stratus FLEX offers flexibility in how QR codes are scanned within the application. Users can select between using their device's camera or an external hand scanner.

## Download Manager

The **Download Manager** section gives users control over the data types downloaded and stored on their device. This feature optimizes device storage and improves the download process's speed.

### QR Codes

Users can disable the download of specific types of QR codes. This setting is particularly useful for users who want to save space on their device and speed up the download process by only retaining essential QR codes.

### Package Attachments

Similar to QR codes, this setting allows users to restrict downloading specific file types. Users can more effectively manage their device's storage by limiting the types of attachments downloaded and reducing the download time.

### Downloaded Projects

Stratus FLEX updates all downloaded projects automatically whenever the device is connected to the internet. This feature allows users to access current information without manually checking for updates and allows switching projects while offline.

# Stratus FLEX: Viewer (beta) - STRATUS Knowledge Base - Confluence

> ## Excerpt
> To enable publishing to FLEX, you will need the 7.2.1 or newer version of the add-in. There is also a settting on Admin-Company-Projects to enable each project to be published to FLEX. Only Revit models are currently supported on Flex.

---
To enable publishing to FLEX, you will need the 7.2.1 or newer version of the add-in. There is also a settting on Admin-Company-Projects to enable each project to be published to FLEX. Only Revit models are currently supported on Flex.

This initial rollout includes tracking status and package filters. We are working on performance optimizations, particularly for larger models. Additional features will be continuously added in future releases, further refining the model viewer's functionality and user experience.

## View Gridlines

Enable gridlines on the viewer by clicking the grid button on the viewer page's right side.

## View Assembly Display Mode

Enable the assembly display mode on the viewer by clicking the display mode button on the viewer page's right side.

# Stratus Workstation - STRATUS Knowledge Base - Confluence

> ## Excerpt
> The Stratus Workstation application is a Cut List application. It can be used to drive tools including TigerStop and RazorGage. If not connected to a tool, it can still be used to nest cut lists and print labels.

---
The Stratus Workstation application is a Cut List application. It can be used to drive tools including TigerStop and RazorGage. If not connected to a tool, it can still be used to nest cut lists and print labels.

-   1 [Stratus Academy Course Video](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/201687060/Stratus+Workstation#Stratus-Academy-Course-Video)
    -   1.1 [Stratus Academy: ADM-516: Stratus Workstation App Settings](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/201687060/Stratus+Workstation#Stratus-Academy%3A-ADM-516%3A-Stratus-Workstation-App-Settings)
-   2 [System Tool Type Selection](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/201687060/Stratus+Workstation#System-Tool-Type-Selection)
-   3 [TigerStop and RazorGage](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/201687060/Stratus+Workstation#TigerStop-and-RazorGage)
    -   3.1 [Settings](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/201687060/Stratus+Workstation#Settings)
    -   3.2 [Summary: Cut List Interface](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/201687060/Stratus+Workstation#Summary%3A-Cut-List-Interface)
    -   3.3 [Details: Cut List Interface](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/201687060/Stratus+Workstation#Details%3A-Cut-List-Interface)
    -   3.4 [TigerStop Manual Overrides](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/201687060/Stratus+Workstation#TigerStop-Manual-Overrides)
    -   3.5 [Stratus Settings](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/201687060/Stratus+Workstation#Stratus-Settings)
-   4 [Pre-Checks](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/201687060/Stratus+Workstation#Pre-Checks)
    -   4.1 [Hardware Setup](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/201687060/Stratus+Workstation#Hardware-Setup)
    -   4.2 [TigerStop Cabling](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/201687060/Stratus+Workstation#TigerStop-Cabling)
    -   4.3 [Windows OS](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/201687060/Stratus+Workstation#Windows-OS)

    -   5.3 [Printing Labels](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/201687060/Stratus+Workstation#Printing-Labels)

## Stratus Academy Course Video

## Stratus Academy: ADM-516: Stratus Workstation App Settings

To take the **Stratus Workstation App Settings** course, login to [**Stratus Academy**](https://academy.stratus.build/ "https://academy.stratus.build/") and and locate the course **ADM-516: Stratus Workstation App Settings**.

1.  Under System, select the **Tool Type** that is being used at the station. This selection controls the options in the General, Cut, and Workstation tabs. The TigerStop and RazorGage tools have the same options but different backend processing. A Lockformer Spiral tool will have different options.
    
2.  The Stratus Workstation application will need to be restarted after a new Tool Type is selected. Once restarted the selected Tool Types tab options will display. This selection will remain after computer restart until it is changed.
    

## TigerStop and RazorGage

For the TigerStop and RazorGage cutting tools, the settings and user interface are the same. However, the communication with the tool is determined by the selected Tool Type on the System tab. See the [**System Tool Type Selection**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/201687060/Stratus+Workstation#System-Tool-Type-Selection "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/201687060/Stratus+Workstation#System-Tool-Type-Selection") section for instructions on switching to either the TigerStop or RazorGage Tool Type.

## Settings

1.  Start the application through the Windows Start menu or another shortcut.
    
    1.  **Note**: Stratus Workstation can be run from any computer.
        
2.  You may be prompted to enter your Autodesk credentials.
    
3.  Click **Settings** in the bottom right of the app. The following tabs will display.  
    

### General

The General tab is used to select a Tool and other options.

1.  **Company** - Select the company when you have access to more than one BIM 360 hub.
    
2.  **Tool** - Select the tool. Many companies have several tools defined for different materials or sizes and each tool includes it’s own label template defined by the Admin.
    
    1.  **Note: Tools** are configured under Admin > Company > Tools and display in this list when **Type** is set to **Cutlist**. 
        
3.  **Apply Tracking Status on Done** (Optional) - Select the Tracking Status that the **part** should be updated to after it is cut. Only Tracking Statuses under Admin > Company > Tracking Statuses where **Applies to Part** is checked should display as options.
    
4.  **Complete Task on Done** (Optional) - Select the Task that should be updated after the cut. Only Tasks associated with the selected Tool under Admin > Company > Stations > [**Task Definitions**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2146995835 "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2146995835") will display in the drop-down list. See the **Stratus Settings** sub-section [**Complete Task On Done**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/201687060/Stratus+Workstation#STRATUSWorkstation-NewTaskDefinitiontoUpdate "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/201687060/Stratus+Workstation#STRATUSWorkstation-NewTaskDefinitiontoUpdate") below for more information.
    
5.  **Print Labels** (Optional) - Check this box if you are printing to a Zebra compatible label printer immediately following any cut. **Note**: Each tool has its own label defined by the Admin.
    
6.  **Label Printer** (Optional) - Select the **Label Printer** to be used for printing labels. A **Label Printer** Tool is configured under Admin > Company > Tools and display in this list when **Type** is set to **ZPL Printer**. 
    
7.  **SIGN OUT** - **User A** can sign out and then **User B** can sign in.
    
8.  **SAVE** - Click **Save** to save any setting changes.
    
9.  **CANCEL** - Click **Cancel** to cancel and not save any changes.
    
10.  **TEST** - Use the **Test** button to find a TigerStop when the application is already running. If the app is launched after a TigerStop is running, the COM port will be automatically located.
    

### Cut

The Cut tab is used to define how cutting information displays and how the tool is controlled.

1.  **Blade Thickness (in)** - Enter the thickness or kerf of the blade which is the width of material removed by a cutting tool.
    
2.  **Cut Length Display Units** - The **Cut Length Display Units** option toggles the display units to either Fractional Feet-Inches (Default) or Fractional Inches. See the Cut Length Display Units section for more information.
    
3.  **Cut Length Precision** - The **Cut Length Precision** setting (Default = 1/16”) only applies to Length display and to printed labels. See the [**Cut Length Precision**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/201687060/Stratus+Workstation#STRATUSWorkstation-CutLengthPrecision "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/201687060/Stratus+Workstation#STRATUSWorkstation-CutLengthPrecision") section below for more information.
    
4.  **Round Up** - The **Round Up** checkbox setting (Default = Unchecked) applies to the actual cut length value. See the [**Round Cut Length Up**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/201687060/Stratus+Workstation#STRATUSWorkstation-RoundCutLengthUp "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/201687060/Stratus+Workstation#STRATUSWorkstation-RoundCutLengthUp") section below for more information. 
    
5.  **Stock Length** - Enter the nominal stock length in inches.
    
    1.  **Tip**: For precise first cuts, if the stock length varies, pre-cut the stock piece to match the exact Stock Length specified here.
        
6.  **Load Offset (in)** - When in the Push Dimension Mode, every time a new piece of stock is expected to be loaded (moving stop to stock length), this adds the 'Load Offset' length to the distance. This value makes it easier to load the material. Load Offset can be a positive or negative number. A negative number would be used for the Kwik-Snap Cast Iron Pipe Cutter use case where Stratus Workstation Dimension Mode is set for BackStop the first cut is off by 0.125 as it did not account for the Kwik-Snap chains.
    
    1.  The head of stop should be Stock Length (48") + Load Offset (9") = 57" from the blade when a new stock is expected to be loaded.
        
    2.  The first press of move will move the stop to stock length, if the offset is 9", the fence will move 9" on the first push.
        
    3.  A second press of the move button will act as the first press of move does currently and move the stop to make the first cut.
        
7.  **Minimum Length (in)** - The minimum amount of stock material length in inches – meaning the Workstation App cannot move the tool to a position that is less than this minimum. Remaining stock length cannot be less than this minimum.
    
8.  **Maximum Scrap Length (in)** - Filters out uncut material that is **not** long enough to be used for stock in another cut. Only uncut material less <= **Max. Scrap Length** will be considered scrap and included in the calculation for total scrap. Consider making this greater than the Minimum Length of cuts. If the “actual” material remaining should display as scrap, enter the stock length value as the **Max. Scrap Length** and everything uncut will be considered scrap. **Note**: This setting controls the **Scrap Display Units** value.
    
9.  **Scrap Display Units** - For the selected material and size, scrap units can be set to Percentage (Total scrap length over stock length), Fractional Feet-Inches, or Fractional Inches.
    
10.  **Stock Display Units** - Select an option (Ex. Pieces of Stock, Fractional Feet-Inches (below), or Fractional Inches). In Stratus Workstation, the icon and value will display.
    
11.  **Keep Long End Last Stock Cut** - When checked the last cut of a nested series, the tail end, will be the longest piece to cut. This is a good operator safety option to a small piece is not the last to be cut.
    
12.  **Dimension Mode** - Backstop mode or Push Mode.
    
    1.  **BackStop** indicates that the movement of material is towards the cutting tool's backstop. This is a good option for cast iron where the shop has a spring loaded backstop.
        
    2.  **Push** indicates material is pushed in a direction away from the cutting tool's backstop.
        
13.  **Movement Direction** - Display cuts on stock material to match the flow of material on the cutting tool.
    
14.  **Test** - Use the **Test** button to find a TigerStop when the application is already running. If the app is launched after a TigerStop is running, the COM port will be automatically located.
    

### Workstation

**Note**: Configure all items up to **Automated Cutting** unless the shop has an automated cutting saw. Skip these items if the shop has an automated cutting saw.

1.  **Use Trigger** - When checked, the cutting machine’s trigger activates the saw to cut the material.
    
2.  **Trigger Timeout (sec)** - Amount of time to wait for detection of a trigger before notifying the user that the tool did not cycle.
    
3.  **Move on Trigger Cycle** - When checked, automatically marks an item as “Done” and moves the tool to next cut or resets stock length at end nested cuts.
    
4.  **Move Wait Time (sec)** - Amount of time to wait before marking an item as “Done” and automatically moving tool. Be sure that the **Move Wait Time** in seconds is greater than the **Move Delay** in seconds from the TigerStop. It is recommend to add an additional second to make sure there’s no toe stepping.
    
    1.  Validate a cut list:
        
        1.  Validate that you are seeing the proper retract and take-up of that retract distance while the tool is cycling, even on the first cut piece out of a stock length.
            
        2.  Validate that the cut lengths are as expected.
            
5.  **Automated Cutting** – When checked, indicates the shop is using an automatic cutting saw rather than a trigger saw (above settings). The cutting tool will automatically cycle. For TigerStop, the optional Advanced Interconnect Kit - AIK is required.
    
6.  **Homing Timeout (sec)** - The **Homing Timeout** value determines how long it takes to move the sled from blade back to furthest extent. 60 seconds is good for a 20' pusher but can be adjusted for different sized pushers.
    
7.  **Move Retry Enabled** - When checked, the **Move Retry Enabled** feature will detect that the move failed and will retry the move up to 3 times. The cause of failed moves can vary and has been attributed to bad cabling or a loss of information glitch over a noisy line. Additionally, some successful moves were incorrectly reported as failures because the pusher relayed its progress before reaching the destination.
    

### System

1.  **Com Port** - Windows hardware port number used for serial communication to a TigerStop or RazorGage.
    
    1.  Note: On startup, Workstation looks for a Com Port.
        
2.  **Baud Rate** - The RazorGage and TigerStop speed of communication on the given Com Port.
    
3.  **Tool Type** - Select what kind of hardware your Workstation App is talking to. See the [**System Tool Type Selection**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2898362369/Copy+of+Stratus+Workstation#System-Tool-Type-Selection "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2898362369/Copy+of+Stratus+Workstation#System-Tool-Type-Selection") section for instructions on switching to other Tool Types.
    
4.  **Debug Browser** - Turn this on to see more login information in a browser helper window.
    
5.  **Remember Login Session** - Turn this on to have cookies store your login tokens.
    
6.  **Simulation Mode** - Simulates an attached cutting machine and provides the ability to print labels but won't move the sled or automate the saw.
    

## Summary: Cut List Interface

In Stratus under the Package's Cut List tab, as soon as the **Send Cut List to Station** button is clicked, the cut list displays in the Stratus Workstation application associated with that station. Below is an example. 

1.  **Filter and Grouping** \- Filter and Group the cut list queue by Project, Model, Package, Spool/Assembly, Area, or Item Grouping.
    
2.  **Connected to the Remote Hub** \- When grayed out, the computer is not connected to the Stratus. When white, the computer is connected to the Stratus.
    
3.  **Workstation is connected**
    
    1.  **Workstation is connected** - The connectivity icon color will be white.
        
    2.  **Workstation is not connected**:
        
        1.  The connectivity icon color will be red.
            
        2.  The message “**Workstation not connected. Setting Manual Cutting Mode.”** prompt will display.
            
        3.  **Manual Cutting Mode** will display in the bottom left.
            
        4.  **Note**: When cutting in manual mode, the "Remaining" stock length does not change when you press **Done**, as it is up to the person cutting to manage the material and the scrap.
            
4.  **Filter and Grouping Current Settings** \- Displays the selections made under Filters and Groupings.
    
5.  **Tool** - The currently selected tool under Settings.
    
6.  **Scrap Display Units** \- Decimal Inches (shown) or percentage is total scrap length over stock length. This value is controlled by the **Maximum Scrap Length** configured under Settings > Cut.
    
7.  **Reset Stock** - Click **Reset Stock** to set the "Remaining" stock length to configured in Settings. You can also key in a value and press enter or push the reset stock button.
    
8.  **Remaining** - The stock remaining after each cut.  **Note**: When cutting in manual mode, the "Remaining" stock length does not change when you press Done, as it is up to the person cutting to manage the material and the scrap. Manually setting a value will renest the pieces in the table. As a result, the length of a scrap piece of material can be entered and as many pieces as possible will be nested.
    
9.  **Move** - To start cutting a new stick:
    
    1.  The operator must click the **Move** button.
        
    2.  The operator is prevented from making a cut when the part length is longer than the stock length.
        
    3.  The TigerStop will be positioned for the first cut. The operator will make the cut. 
        
    4.  In Settings, if **Print Labels** is checked and a **Label Printer** is selected, then a label will be printed. For label configuration, see the [**Label Printing for Zebra (ZPL) Compatible Printers**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/157974545 "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/157974545") article. **Note**: If labels are modified in Stratus, the updated label will not apply to existing cut lists in Stratus Workstation, rather, the cut list needs to be unassigned from the Cut List tab and then resent to the station.
        
    5.  In Settings, if the **Move on Trigger Cycle is checked**, the TigerStop will be automatically positioned to the next cut after the designated **Move Wait Time** setting.
        
    6.  The top row and Last Cut Item will update.
        
    7.  **Note**: Cut List items cannot be selected out of the nested order.
        
10.  **Done** - If the **Move on Trigger Cycle** is not checked, then the operator can click the Done button to trigger the TigerStop to move to the next position.
    
11.  **Pause** - **Pause** will interrupt the stock material workflow.   When paused, the user can use the green TigerStop keypad to move the tool to a specified length. Then they can resume with an option to keep the current stock length or use the previous one.
    
12.  **Delete** - **Delete** is used more by testers than operators. Delete will delete the selected item(s) from the cut list. The item(s) will be orphaned from the cut list and the status of the cut list in Stratus will not reach 100% complete. Use this option as a last resort. Only the top row can be deleted, a cut list item in the middle of the list cannot be deleted.
    
13.  **Material and size tabs** - Cut lists sent to the tool are organized into tabs by material and size.
    
14.  **Current Stock** - The **top row** is highlighted green and indicates the current cut. 
    
15.  **Length** - The cut length for each item to be cut. **Note**: The cut length display value is impacted by the Cut Length Precision, Round Cut Length Up, and Cut Length Display Units settings.
    
16.  **Stock** - Stock is a visual representation of how the total length of the stock and how it will be cut.
    
    1.  The **Stock** grid indicates the total length of the stock and how each part will be cut. 
        
    2.  **Diagonal stripes** indicate the anticipated scrap material. 
        
    3.  **Gray** indicates parts of the stock that either have been or will be cut. 
        
    4.  **Yellow** indicates the current cut. 
        
17.  **Item** - Displays the part's item number.
    
18.  **Package** - Displays the Stratus Package Name.
    
    1.  **Area** (Not Shown) - Displays the Area (STRATUS.Part.BIMArea), if set in Stratus.
        
19.  **Assembly** - Displays the Stratus Assembly Name.
    
20.  **Project** - Displays the Stratus  Project.
    
21.  **Model** - Displays the Stratus Model.
    
22.  **User** - Displays the User who generated the cut list.
    
23.  **Date/Time** - Displays the Date/Time the cut list was sent to the station tool queue. 
    
24.  **Last Item Cut** - Displays the last cut item. 
    
25.  **Stop** - **Stop** will cause all movement to stop.
    
26.  **Home** - **Home** sends the TigerStop back to the Home position.
    
27.  **Position** - The stock remaining after each cut.
    
28.  **Bundle** - Bundling allows the operator to cut more than one item at a time to the same length. See the Bundle section for more information.
    
29.  **Stock with current cut highlighted** - At the bottom of the screen the current stock displays the currently selected cut.
    
30.  **Count** - The number of cuts associated with the selected project, model, package, spool/assembly, material, and size.
    
31.  **History** - View the history of cut items and re-print labels. If the same computer running the application is used for multiple Stratus tools (Ex. a copper tool, a steel tool, etc.), the history for each selected Stratus tool will be unique. 
    
32.  **Settings** - Open the Settings Panel.
    
33.  **Close** - Close the Stratus Workstation Application.
    
34.  **Stock Display Units** - Select an option under Settings > Cut.
    
35.  **Area** (Not Shown in Screenshot) - Displays the Stratus Area Name.
    

## Details: Cut List Interface

### Filter and Grouping

Filter and Group the cut list queue by Project, Model, Package, Spool/Assembly, Area, or Item Grouping.

1.  **Filter to Individual Items** - Expand Model, Package, Spool / Assembly, Area to select/deselect individual items. As items are checked/unchecked, they are filtered in/out of the tool list. 
    
    **Note**: Click All Packages to select all packages in within the selected Project and Model. Long lists of assemblies or packages can take up to a minute to check or uncheck All items.
    
    1.  **Checked** - When checked, all items will be checked and **All** will display in the drop-down (Ex. All Packages).
        
    2.  **Unchecked** - When unchecked all items will be unchecked and the drop-down will be blank.
        
    3.  **Mix Checked/Unchecked** - When individual items are checked and other items are unchecked, the selected item names will display in the drop-down (Ex. Model reads GTP - ITM - Revit - Mechanical) as to fill the space. The space is not designed to display all checked, just click the drop-down to view.
        
2.  **Item Grouping** - Nested items can be grouped By Package, By Assembly, Item Number, Area, or No Item Grouping.
    
3.  **Batch Size** - The **Batch Size** option creates cut list subgroups that will be cut before moving to the next subgroup. A Batch Size subgroup is used in combination with the Item Grouping (By Package, By Assembly, By Item Number) options. The purpose of a subgroup is to nest parts in a Batch according to the Item Grouping. If the Batch Size is 2 or more, all parts for the first two Item Groupings will be cut before moving to the next batch of 2. Currently, for a large list of cut list items, Stratus Workstation optimizes the cuts to reduce waste which means the order that parts from different assemblies or packages are cut may not be optimal for assembly or shipping.
    
    For example:
    
    1.  With **No Item Grouping**, the Assembly sort order is random.
        
    2.  Set **Item Grouping** to By Assembly. The list is sorted by Assembly.
        
    3.  **Batch Size**
        
        1.  **Unchecked** (default) - When unchecked the cut list will not enforce subgroups.
            
        2.  **Checked** \- When checked, the cut list will be organized in batches specified by the number entered. The cut list order may change.
            
            1.  If Batch Size is 1, all parts for each assembly will be cut before moving to another assembly.
                
            2.  If Batch Size is 2+, all parts for the first two assemblies will be cut before moving to the next batch of 2+ assemblies.
                
                1.  As a result, the cut list will sort assemblies so that all parts for the first two assemblies will be cut before moving to the next batch of 2+ assemblies and a different assembly won’t be inserted in between. Notice that once the last -12 and -13 assembly has been cut, then the -14 assembly can be cut.
                    
                2.  Similarly, in this example with Batch Size = 3, the -12, -13, and -14 assemblies are cut before moving on to the -103 assembly.
                    

### Load Next Stock Material

When the last item from a cut list material and size is cut, a message similar to the following will display. The purpose of the message is to inform the operator that a \*\*\* NEW MATERIAL \*\*\* needs to be loaded. The name of the new material size to load is included.

### Cut Length Precision

The **Cut Length Precision** setting (Default = 1/16”) only applies to Length display and to printed labels. To change the Cut Length Precision:

1.  The cut list displays the Length values.
    
2.  Click Settings > **Cut Length Precision** drop-down. Select a value (Ex. 1/2”) and then click **Save**.
    
3.  The cut list page will refresh and display the cut Length values with the defined precision.
    
4.  When the part is cut, the actual length will be cut, not the precision display value.
    
5.  The label cut length will include the precision display value.
    

### Cut Length Display Units

The Cut Length Display Units option toggles the display units to either Fractional Feet-Inches (Default) or Fractional Inches.

1.  By default, Cut Length Display Units are Fractional Feet-Inches.
    
2.  Under Settings > Cut Length Display Units, select an option (Ex. Fractional Inches).
    
3.  The Cut Length will display Fractional Inches.
    
4.  Configure the Tool label template to use the field lengthInInches. For example:  
    ^FO175,160  
    ^FD{{lengthInInches}}^FS
    
5.  When the label prints the cut length will display as Fractional Inches.
    

### Round Cut Length Up

The **Round Cut** checkbox setting (Default = Unchecked) applies to the actual cut length value.

**To change the Round Cut value:**

1.  The cut list displays the Length values.
    
2.  Under Settings, the **Round Cut** checkbox displays.
    
    1.  **Unchecked** (Default) - When unchecked, the cut length will be the actual cut length value.
        
    2.  **Checked** \- When checked, the actual cut length will be rounded according to the Cut Length Precision setting.
        
3.  Click **Save**.
    
4.  With the Round Cut checkbox checked, the cut list page will refresh and display the actual cut length rounded according to the Cut Length Precision setting.
    
5.  The cut and label will use the new cut length.
    

### History

To re-print a label or re-cut an item:

1.  Click the **History** button.
    
2.  Previously cut items will display. Select an item.
    
    1.  **Print** \- Print the item’s label.
        
    2.  **Move** \- Re-cut the item. You will be informed that the tool position will be moved. The presumptive workflow is that an operator who needs to re-cut a previously cut piece will remove their current in-progress stock, place a different piece of stock on the platform and cut the stock in backstop mode.
        
    3.  Click **OK** to move the tool position and make the cut.
        
    4.  **Close** or **X** \- Click Close or the X button to close the window. The operator will be prompted:
        
        1.  **Continue from previous position** \- Remaining stock will be the previous position value. The operator can place the original stock back on the platform to carry on as though they never stopped cutting. The cut list will not have been changed.
            
        2.  **Reset stock and continue** \- Functions as if the Reset Stock button was clicked, thereby setting Remaining to the Stock Length value and re-nesting the cut list.
            

### Scrap Material

Scrap material from one standard stock can be used for the first cut of the next spool For example, Spool B2 uses the remaining scrap from previous stock and then moves to a new piece of stock to continue nesting cuts.

### Bundle

Bundling allows the operator to cut more than one item at a time to the same length, think of multiple all-thread rods or unistrut strapped together destined for a band-saw. The Bundling feature supports TigerStop, Nesting, and Labels. It's important to note, Bundling will only work in the 'Backstop Mode' with a TigerStop. Bundling is a session-specific task, so if a bundle is made, the Stratus Workstations application is closed and reopened, the bundle will need to be recreated. The Bundle feature can also be used with the TigerStop AIK setup.

To use the Bundle feature:

1.  Under Packages > Package > Cut Lists, send a cut list to a station.
    
2.  At the station, open the **Stratus Workstation** application.
    
3.  Click the cut list. A dialog similar to the following will display. Notice the identical lengths and the **Bundle** button.
    
4.  Click the **Bundle** button. The Maximum Bundle Size dialog will display. Here the Bundle Size can be set to whatever the saw can handle. If the Bundle Size had previously been set and needs to be changed, it can be changed here as well.
    
5.  Once the Bundle Size is set, click **Close**. A message will display that the TigerStop will run in “**backstop mode**.” Click **OK**.
    
    1.  **Note**: If a different cut list is selected where a Bundle Size has not been set, a message will display that the TigerStop will run in “**push mode**”. Click **OK**. Clock **Close** on the Maximum Bundle Size dialog.
        
6.  Now that the Stratus Workstation is setup in “backstop mode” it is ready to move and cut normally. Notice the following:
    
    1.  **Bundle Size** - The Bundle Size is the count of the currently selected bundle.
        
    2.  **Bundle Max** – The Bundle Max is the value entered in the Maximum Bundle Size dialog above.
        
    3.  **Count** – The count column nests the items that will be cut together in a bundle.
        
    4.  **Cut List Bundle Icon** – After a Bundle Max value has been saved for a cut list, the Bundled icon will display on the tab.
        
7.  Move and cut normally. As you cut, bundles will disappear from the screen. Cut bundles, like normal cuts, can be viewed by clicking the **History** button.  If the same computer running the application is used for multiple Stratus tools (Ex. a copper tool, a steel tool, etc.), the history for each selected Stratus tool will be unique. 
    
8.  To “**Unbundle**” a bundle, click the Bundle button and then click the Unbundle button and OK. The dialog informs that the bundle no longer exists and default cutting settings are active.
    
9.  Click **Close**. The page will refresh, and the **Count** column will disappear indicating that all bundles have returned to unique cuts and the Bundle Max and Size data will disappear.
    

## TigerStop Manual Overrides

### Material Retractions with TigerStop

Retractions of material when using a TigerStop are handled by the tool/amp/controller and are not a feature of the Stratus Workstation App. This can be accomplished with a few simple changes to the TigerStop controller settings. Per TigerStop on the functionality of the DM Only option for the Retract Type setting, "The Retract move will happen as soon as the Dead-Man circuit opens when using a TigerStop Interconnect Kit." The following are Settings in the TigerStop controller (the green keypad).

1.  Go to the Options Menu.
    
    1.  Set the **Retract Type** to _DM Only._
        
    2.  Set your **Retract** distance in inches.
        
    3.  Validate that your **Retract Offset** is set to _0.000in_. You should only have a non-zero value here if the cutting operation physically moves the stock material towards the direction of the pusher.
        
2.  Go to the Motion Menu.
    
    1.  Please validate that the **Move Delay** in seconds on the TigerStop is less than the **Move Wait Time** in seconds on the Stratus Workstation App. Any physical restrictions on the tool and in its operational settings should be calculated and accounted for. Do not arbitrarily make your **Move Delay** less than the **Move Wait Time** and beware that the value you enter on the TigerStop is in milliseconds.
        

## Stratus Settings

### Complete Task On Done

See the [**Task Definitions (Admin)**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/217711302 "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/217711302") article for complete information and a link to the [**Stratus Academy**](https://academy.stratus.build/ "https://academy.stratus.build/") course **ADM-518: Task Definitions**.

Companies can use Task Definition for intermediate steps between major tracking status changes.  For example, they may have "In Fabrication" and "Fabrication Completed" as their tracking statuses, but they have a Task Definition associated with parts that include individual tasks for steps like "Cut".

The Stratus Workstation application currently includes the **Apply Tracking Status on Done** setting which is used to update a tracking status when a cut is completed. The **Complete Task On Done** setting is used to update a part Task (if one exists).

To use this feature:

1.  **Configure Task Definitions**.
    
2.  **Configure a Tool.**
    
3.  **Configure a Task Workflow for a part**.
    
    1.  **Apply to Type** = Part
        
    2.  **Initiated by Tracking Status** = Issued for Fabrication (in this case)
        
4.  **Configure a Station**. The Station is associated with the Tool and the Task Definitions. When the Stratus Workstation is opened (below) and this Tool is selected, the Task Definitions will be available in the New Task Definition to Update setting.
    
5.  **Create a Package**.
    
6.  In the Tracking tab, change the Status of the “Package to Issued for Fabrication” which is the setting for the **Initiated by Tracking Status** configured in the Task Workflow created (above).
    
    1.  Tasks are created on the Tasks tab.
        
    2.  The Task Workflow is automatically assigned to each part on the Package’s Items tab.
        
7.  **Generate a Cut Lists -** In the Package’s **Cut List** tab, click the **Generate a Cut Lists** The Cut Lists will display.
    
8.  Check to select one or more Cut Lists and then click the **Send Cut List to Station** button.
    
9.  **Stratus Workstation -** Open the **Stratus Workstation** and click **Settings**.
    
10.  Click the **Complete Task on Done** drop-down. Select a status for the tasks to receive once a part is cut.
    
11.  Once set, make a cut from the cut list.
    
12.  The Package's Item tab will show the task is complete as the task button turns green.
    

### Remove Cut List from a Station

In Stratus under the Package's Cut List tab, as soon as the **Send Cut List to Station** button is clicked, the cut list displays in the Stratus Workstation application associated with that station.

If the cut list was sent to the wrong station or needs to be removed from the Stratus Workstation queue, it can be quickly removed in a couple of ways:

1.  Under the Package's **Cut List** tab either:
    
    1.  Click the **Unassign from Station** button. This will remove the cut list from the station and the Stratus Workstation queue, but will not delete the cut list from the package. This will enable a user to select a different station and **Send Cut List to Station** again.
        
    2.  Click the **Delete** button. This will delete the cut list from the package. A user will need to **Generate Cut Lists** for the package in order for the cut list to be available after being deleted.
        
2.  Under **Shops** > **Station** (select) > **Tools** (select) a list of cut lists for the station and tool will display.
    
    1.  Click the **Unassign from Station** button. This will remove the cut list from the station and the Stratus Workstation queue, but will not delete the cut list from the package.
        

### Rename Package

**Note:**  If a user changes the name of a package after sending a cut list to the Stratus Workstation, the old package name will continue to display in the Stratus Workstation. To resolve this issue, delete the cut list and resend it to the Stratus Workstation.

### Status Update

In Stratus under the Package's Cut List tab, as soon as the **Send Cut List to Station** button is clicked, the cut list displays in the Stratus Workstation application associated with that station. The cut list status changes as items are cut.

1.  Package's Cut List tab - When the **Send Cut List to Station** button is clicked, on the Package's Cut List tab the status of the cut list is changed to **In Progress \[0%\]**. 
    
2.  As soon as any cuts are made, the cut list status is updated.
    
    1.  Package's **Cut List** tab - Status column.
        
    2.  **Shops** > **Station** (select) > **Tools** (select) > Status column.
        

## Pre-Checks

In most cases, users can start using the Stratus Workstation App immediately after installation. However, there are instances where certain steps must be handled manually.

## Hardware Setup

When installing a TigerStop for the first time, ensure it is activated. Failure to activate it can result in a disabled COM port, causing the Workstation app to freeze.

## TigerStop Cabling

Connect a serial cable from your Workstation App to the TigerStop pusher, ensuring the cable length does not exceed 20 feet. A repeater is recommended if using a cable 20-foot or longer. Shorter cables perform better, as 50-foot cables have been known to fail, but switching to shorter lengths resolved the issue. **Do not tie or wrap your serial cable / DB9 cable with any power lines/cords.**

### **Sealevel Cabling (Recommended)**

A tablet or PC runs the Stratus Workstation App and communicates with the TigerStop pusher using the cable labeled "Goes to PC Tablet" in the image above. The recommended DB9 to USB cable is sold by SeaLevel: [https://www.sealevel.com/product/2105r-usb-to-1-port-rs-232-db9-serial-interface-adapter/](https://www.sealevel.com/product/2105r-usb-to-1-port-rs-232-db9-serial-interface-adapter/ "https://www.sealevel.com/product/2105r-usb-to-1-port-rs-232-db9-serial-interface-adapter/")

### **Sealevel Software (Recommended)**

Sea Level software is recommended. Download at: [**Software: SeaCOM – Windows**](https://www.sealevel.com/support/software-seacom-windows/ "https://www.sealevel.com/support/software-seacom-windows/"). **Note**: It will be called Port Manager in Windows when you want to run it. The software, when run, looks something like this:

## **Windows OS**

Running the app as an administrator is not required, but the IT department must ensure that the user profile retains write access to the %appdata% section of the hard drive.

## **Firewalls**

The Workstation app uses SignalR (an application that enables instant data updates between servers and the app), over port 443, so the IT department must enable WebSockets through the firewall

**COM Port**

1.  Do not run **TigerTouch** or **TigerLink** simultaneously with the **Stratus Workstation App** on the same computer, as they will compete for the COM port, causing the Workstation App to fail.
    
2.  To determine if TigerTouch or TigerLink is running, open Windows Task Manager.
    
    1.  On the left side of this program, click on the startup app icon.
        
    2.  **Disable** either the TigerLink or TigerTouch if it is running on startup.
        

## Stratus Workstation App Installation

Download and install the latest [**Stratus Workstation**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2121400321 "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2121400321") software.

## Troubleshooting

## F Keys

Press the “F1” key for a list of other F# shortcuts that will provide diagnostic information. Below are examples of each shortcut key.

1.  F1 - to show this help.
    
2.  F2 - to show the last 8 lines of login/app key support logs.
    
3.  F3 - to show the last 8 lines of Settings.Json change log.
    
4.  F4 - to open the Settings.Json container folder.
    
5.  F5 - to open the Settings.Json file.
    
6.  F6 - to open the Log file containing folder.
    
7.  F7 - to open the Log file.
    
8.  F8 - to toggle the protocol ticker.
    
9.  F9 - to view the your cookies and open the Cookie directory.
    

## General Workstation

1.  If your Workstation App will not move beyond a minimum length, go into Stratus, and edit the max stock length for the tool slightly larger than the actual max length.
    
2.  If the following error message displays:
    
3.  You have two ways to fix this:
    
    1.  Put a copy of the following batch file on your desktop, and click it before launching the workstation app: loginFix.cmd
        
    2.  Press Cancel, then select the \[Sign Out\] button at the bottom of the settings screen.
        
    
    Sign Out from Settings Screen
    

## Printing Labels

# Stratus and Autodesk Log In - STRATUS Knowledge Base - Confluence

> ## Excerpt
> Before attempting to authenticate to Stratus, a user must first be added to the company as a user.

---
-   1 [Prerequisite](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/217907209/Stratus+and+Autodesk+Log+In#Prerequisite)
-   2 [Sign in to Autodesk](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/217907209/Stratus+and+Autodesk+Log+In#Sign-in-to-Autodesk)

## Prerequisite

Before attempting to authenticate to Stratus, a user must first be [**added to the company as a user**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/201130058 "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/201130058").

1.  On the home page at: [![](https://www.gtpstratus.com/favicon.ico)Home](https://www.gtpstratus.com/) , click **LOG IN**.
    
2.  The email credentials dialog will display. **Enter your Email address** and click **Continue**.
    
3.  The password credentials dialog will display. Click the **Forgot your password?** link.
    
4.  The Verification dialog will display. **Enter your Email address** and click **Send verification code**. Do not click the Continue button.
    
5.  The Verification code dialog will display. Check the email account you entered above to retrieve the verification code. Do not click the Continue button.
    
    1.  You should receive an email similar to the following within minutes.  
        **Subject** \= Microsoft on behalf of GTP Services - NPE  
        **From** \= [msonlineservicesteam@microsoftonline.com](mailto:msonlineservicesteam@microsoftonline.com "mailto:msonlineservicesteam@microsoftonline.com")
        
    2.  Copy your code (Ex. 123704).
        
6.  Return to the Verification code dialog and a) **paste the code into the Verification code from the email into the text box (Ex. 123704)** and b) click the **Verify code** button. Do not click the Continue button.
    
    1.  A message will display if your verification has expired. In this case, click the **Send new code** button.
        
7.  The Email address verified message will display. Click the **Continue** button.
    
    1.  **Change Email** - The Change Email button enables users to change their email address if it has changed.
        
8.  The New Password dialog will display. Enter your new password, confirm the new password, and then click **Continue**.  
    **Note**: See the [**Password Requirements**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/1971552257 "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/1971552257") article for more information. GTP Services enforces NIST Guidelines for password requirements.
    
9.  If you entered a password used within the last 3 password changes, the following dialog will prevent you from using that password.
    
10.  If the passwords match you will be logged into Stratus. See the [**Stratus Login**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/217907209/Stratus+and+Autodesk+Log+In#STRATUS-Login "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/217907209/Stratus+and+Autodesk+Log+In#STRATUS-Login") section below.
    

## Sign in to Autodesk

To Sign in to Autodesk, see the [**Sign in to Autodesk**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/1953857537/Autodesk#Sign-in-to-Autodesk "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/1953857537/Autodesk#Sign-in-to-Autodesk") article.

## Autodesk Account and Authentication

Users who need to publish or view models will need to have an Autodesk account and will need to Sign in to this account within Stratus. Users who only need to Stratus to generate reports or view non-model page do not need an Autodesk account.

To create an Autodesk account:

1.  Go to [https://www.autodesk.com/](https://www.autodesk.com/ "https://www.autodesk.com/") click SIGN IN, and then click the CREATE ACCOUNT option.
    
2.  Follow the prompts.
    

To Sign In to Autodesk within Stratus:

1.  Click your **badge** > **My Account** > **Autodesk** and sign into your account. If you don’t sign in to Autodesk, you can still use Stratus, but pages that include models will inform you that you need to login to Autodesk.
    
2.  When your Autodesk credentials have been verified, Stratus will display the **Autodesk blue logo** next to your badge.
    
3.  When signed in to your company and to Autodesk account, your badge drop-down will look similar to the following:
    

## Non-BIM 360 user Login

A company administrator can add a non-BIM 360 user to Stratus by following the **Add New User Not In Your BIM 360 section** of the [Users (Admin)](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/201130058 "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/201130058") article. After the user is setup as a company user in Stratus, the user must follow these steps in order to login to Stratus for the first time.

1.  To login, the user will attempt to login to Stratus at: [https://www.gtpstratus.com/](https://www.gtpstratus.com/ "https://www.gtpstratus.com/") by clicking the **Sign In** button.
    
2.  The user will enter their email in the Login dialog.
    
3.  Once the email is entered, click the “**Don’t remember your password?”** link. The Reset your password dialog will display.
    
4.  Click the **SEND EMAIL** link and then check your email for a **Welcome to Stratus!** email.
    
5.  In the email, click the **Confirm** **my account** link and the **Email Verification** confirmation will display. This step adds your email as a record in Stratus. The next step is to Reset your Password.
    
6.  Attempt to login to Stratus again at: [https://www.gtpstratus.com/](https://www.gtpstratus.com/ "https://www.gtpstratus.com/") by clicking the **Sign In** button.
    
7.  To set your password, click the “**Don’t remember your password?”** link again.
    
8.  The Reset your password dialog will display. Click the **SEND EMAIL** button.
    
9.  When you receive the Password Change Request email, click the **click here** link.
    
10.  The Change Password dialog will display. Enter and confirm your Stratus password.
    
11.  Click the button and the message “Your password has been reset successfully” will display.
    
12.  Login to Stratus at: [https://www.gtpstratus.com/](https://www.gtpstratus.com/ "https://www.gtpstratus.com/") by clicking the **Sign In** button and enter your username and password. The first time you do this the following instruction will display.
    
13.  Click **OK** and the Stratus home page will display.
    
14.  Per the instruction, click your **Badge** and select a **company link**.
    
15.  The Stratus page will refresh, and the user will have access to whatever project and project roles have been granted by the company administrator.
    
16.  To access a model (Ex. Models > Viewer, Assemblies > Viewer, Packages > Viewer), a user must:
    
    1.  Have been given access to the company’s BIM 360 project and folder where the model is stored
        
    2.  Have an Autodesk account (free) where the Autodesk account email matches their Stratus email.
        
17.  If the user has an Autodesk account, login to the account within Stratus.
    
    1.  Click the **Badge** > **My Account**.
        
    2.  Click the **Autodesk** tab and then click **Sign in to Autodesk**.
        
    3.  When your Autodesk credentials have been verified, Stratus will display the Autodesk blue logo next to your badge.
        
    4.  You can change your badge image under your **badge** > **My Account** > **Profile**. Click the **Browse** button and locate an image, then click **Save**.
        
    5.  When signed in to your company and to Autodesk account, your badge drop-down will look similar to the following:
        

## Login Issues

### Publish Message - You are not signed on to Autodesk

1.  **Problem**: In the publish dialog you:
    
    1.  do not see a username
        
    2.  see the message "Problem Connecting to Autodesk Forge"
        
    3.  receive the message "You are not signed on to Autodesk" 
        
2.  **Solution**: 
    
    1.  Open a web browser window and login to Stratus at [https://www.gtpstratus.com](https://www.gtpstratus.com/ "https://www.gtpstratus.com/") 
        
    2.  Click your user image badge in the upper right and click **My Account**
        
    3.  Click the Autodesk tab and make sure you are logged in to your Autodesk account.
        
    4.  Retry the desktop publish
        
    5.  If the issue persists, in the publish dialog, click the "Sign Out" link and then try to sign back in.
        

### Viewer Tab Does Not Display

1.  Problem: I've logged into Stratus but don't see the **Models > Viewer** tab, or the **Assemblies > Viewer** tab, or the **Packages > Viewer** tab.  
    
    ![](blob:https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/fc5a95ce-3d7e-4d30-90b3-1037954b3fc1)
    
     
    
    ![](blob:https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/4ca9e2d1-719e-4fba-81a9-62b2f5428836)
    
     
    
    ![](blob:https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/d4a0b587-cbda-4eb2-95ab-7686094cd52b)
    
2.  Viewing a model requires that you are logged in to your Autodesk account.
    
    1.  Open a web browser window and logged in to Stratus at [https://www.gtpstratus.com](https://www.gtpstratus.com/ "https://www.gtpstratus.com/") 
        
    2.  Click your user image badge in the upper right and click **My Account**
        
    3.  Click the Autodesk tab and make sure you are logged in to your Autodesk account.  
        
        ![](blob:https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/477a1299-cd65-4fec-b77a-28edd556bd8c)
        
    4.  Refresh the page and the Viewer tab will display if your project role has Viewer tab permission.
        

## 3-Legged Authentication

3-Legged Authentication is offered to companies connecting to client BIM 360 Docs accounts. Contact the [**Stratus Service Desk**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/servicedesk/customer/portal/3 "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/servicedesk/customer/portal/3") for more information.

## Single Sign-On

Single Sign-On to Stratus which provides the ability to use your company's identity provider for Stratus authentication. See the [**SSO for**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/1859485697 "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/1859485697") **Stratus** article for more information.

# System Requirements - STRATUS Knowledge Base - Confluence

> ## Excerpt
> A stable, reliable, high-performing internet connection with adequate bandwidth and speed is perhaps the single most important key to success.

---
## Internet

A stable, reliable, high-performing internet connection with adequate bandwidth and speed is perhaps the single most important key to success. 

## Revit / AutoCAD / Fabrication

Revit / AutoCAD versions 2019 or newer are supported.

## Shop Computers

## Desktop/Laptop Minimum

-   64-bit Microsoft® Windows® 10 or Windows 11
-   Intel® i-Series, Xeon®, AMD® Ryzen, Ryzen Threadripper PRO. 2.5 GHz or Higher. The highest affordable CPU speed rating is recommended.
-   16 GB RAM (though more is better)
-   1280 x 1024 with true color (graphics card upgrade with additional RAM is better) 
-   10 GB free disk space 

## Tablet Minimum

-   Surface Pro 7 or newer (standard with **TigerStop**) and recommended over iPads
-   Apple iPad or iPad Pro 
    -   **3/25/22 Note**: The Apple iOS 15.x update includes a memory limit. As a result, in some cases, large models will not load in the STRATUS viewer.  The GTP team has been in communication with Autodesk and tried some changes to get these models to load on the iPad, but these changes have failed. Until this issue is resolved the GTP team recommends to:
        -   simplify geometry for manufacturer-provided part families used within Revit
            
        -   create separate 3D views by area or level and make one of them the default rather than the overall 3D view
            
        -   use non-Apple devices
            
-   16 GB RAM (more is better) 
-   Stylus Pen and keyboard (recommended)

## Zebra Label Printer

-   Windows is required to print labels using the STRATUS Workstation and STRATUS Print applications.
-   [https://www.zebra.com/content/dam/zebra/product-information/en-us/brochures-datasheets/desktop/advanced-desktop-datasheet-en-us.pdf](https://www.zebra.com/content/dam/zebra/product-information/en-us/brochures-datasheets/desktop/advanced-desktop-datasheet-en-us.pdf) 
-   GK-420 – Printer for **TigerStop** Station 
-   GT800 \- desktop printer 
-   ZD410 \- direct thermal printer 
-   TLP2824 Plus \- thermal transfer printer  
-   ZT600 series \- industrial 

## Scanner

To scan a tracking code, the scanner must be integrated with a computer. 

-   NETUM Wireless Barcode Scanner 2.4GHz (need Bluetooth Receiver) 
    -   Example: [NETUM 2D Barcode Scanner, Compatible with 2.4G Wireless & Bluetooth & USB Wired Connection, Connect Smart Phone, Tablet, PC, 1D Bar Code Reader Work for QR PDF417 Data Matrix NT-1228BL](https://www.amazon.com/NETUM-Bluetooth-Handheld-Wireless-NT-1228BL/dp/B07CBS52KJ/ref=sr_1_1?crid=1XJ1B1YQ52P1E&keywords=nt-1228BL&qid=1650635934&s=electronics&sprefix=nt-1228bl%2Celectronics%2C96&sr=1-1)

## Wi-Fi

-   High-speed internet with bandwidth for multiple simultaneous connections is very important. 
-   Business-class internet and WIFI is required for shops. 
-   Wireless must provide adequate coverage to all areas of the facility. 

## BIM 360 Requirements

-   While BIM 360 user accounts can be created for a shared login such as [shopworker1@contractor.com](mailto:shopworker@contractor.com) [shopworker2@contractor.com](mailto:shopworker2@contractor.com) etc., this does limit the level of detail provided in tracking logs, as this user will be associated currently with tracking log entries. 
-   We recommend individual user accounts for all modelers, project managers, and foremen.  Shared accounts are acceptable for most shop and field workers. 
-   Shop computers connected to cutting machines (Ex. TigerStop) should each have their own account. 

## Browsers 

-   Google Chrome (Recommended) 
-   Microsoft Edge 
-   Firefox 
-   Safari 

## Fabrication Machinery Supported 

## Pipe Cutters

-   TigerStop 
-   Snap Cutters 
-   Manual Saws 
-   Automated Saws 
-   T-Drill 

## Multi-Axis Pipe and Hole Cutters

-   PypeServer 
-   Watts 
-   Vernon 
-   T-Drill 
-   HGG 
-   .PCF file export available for other machinery 

## Auto-welding Machinery

-   Novarc
-   T-Drill
