# T-DRILL - STRATUS Knowledge Base - Confluence

> ## Excerpt
> Configure a Tool under Admin > Company > Tools. Note the generated Tool Id. See the Tools article for more information. Below is an example.

---
## Configure Tool

1.  Configure a **Tool** under Admin > Company > Tools. Note the generated Tool Id. See the [**Tools**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/215220225 "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/215220225") article for more information. Below is an example. 
    
    ![image-20250527-220615.png](blob:https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/c87e5211-eea2-4523-94a2-7a93922cfb96#media-blob-url=true&id=5ea1589a-3258-41d0-a03e-49bb114aee5a&collection=contentId-349143080&contextId=349143080&mimeType=image%2Fpng&name=image-20250527-220615.png&size=23370&width=1471&height=177&alt=image-20250527-220615.png)
    
2.  Repeat these steps to create a Tool for T-DRILL Collaring.
    

## Configure Station

1.  Configure a **Station** under Admin > Company > Stations. See the [**Stations**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/215220408 "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/215220408") article for more information. 
    
2.  **Note**: Set the Division so that the cut list displays on the Shops tab.
    
    ![image-20250528-182400.png](blob:https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/395bd310-2bb2-4e01-9684-7b0a38642c17#media-blob-url=true&id=1d3e2aae-2aa2-4904-a6fc-bedaa7b975f3&collection=contentId-349143080&contextId=349143080&mimeType=image%2Fpng&name=image-20250528-182400.png&size=32336&width=1237&height=276&alt=image-20250528-182400.png)
    
3.  Repeat these steps to create a Station for T-DRILL Collaring.
    

## Configure Cut List Mapping

1.  Configure **Cut List Mappings** under Admin > Company > Part Templates > Cut List Mapping. See the [**Cut List Mappings**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/217809750/Part+Templates+Admin#Cut-List-Mappings "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/217809750/Part+Templates+Admin#Cut-List-Mappings") article for more information. 
    
    1.  Example Cut List Mapping for 2041. This Cut List Mapping will be sent to the T-DRILL Cutting tool.
        
        ![image-20250528-204132.png](blob:https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/4790b393-6543-4427-a9ec-45c33938ba4e#media-blob-url=true&id=ca8581eb-92c6-4c8c-9cf4-3ae93c75b043&collection=contentId-349143080&contextId=349143080&mimeType=image%2Fpng&name=image-20250528-204132.png&size=50553&width=1043&height=525&alt=image-20250528-204132.png)
        
    2.  Example Cut List Mapping for 2875. This Cut List Mapping will be sent to the T-DRILL Collaring tool.
        
        ![image-20250528-204028.png](https://media-cdn.atlassian.com/file/ab2c2121-9751-4254-8e80-bb950ae9fc9d/image/cdn?allowAnimated=true&client=5f4a70b1-9d9d-47c3-b388-87235680bb54&collection=contentId-349143080&height=326&max-age=2592000&mode=full-fit&source=mediaCard&token=eyJhbGciOiJIUzI1NiJ9.eyJpc3MiOiI1ZjRhNzBiMS05ZDlkLTQ3YzMtYjM4OC04NzIzNTY4MGJiNTQiLCJhY2Nlc3MiOnsidXJuOmZpbGVzdG9yZTpjb2xsZWN0aW9uOmNvbnRlbnRJZC0zNDkxNDMwODAiOlsicmVhZCJdfSwiZXhwIjoxNzUwODY4NTY0LCJuYmYiOjE3NTA4NjU2ODR9.kiWaHMp7rkaYxzjq-CrseXoznLjUEXg_GD2-lTVvLB4&width=763)
        

## Generate a .CSV Output File for T-DRILL Cutting and T-DRILL Collaring

To generate a .CSV file for the T-DRILL Cutting and T-DRILL Collaring tools: 

1.  Open a package that includes a 2041 part that also has a 2875 part.
    
2.  In the Cut Lists tab:
    
    1.  Click **Generate Cut Lists**. 2 or more cut lists will display.
        
        ![image-20250528-204540.png](https://media-cdn.atlassian.com/file/63da61f8-ca97-4dcf-a2b8-b0cd3af8b174/image/cdn?allowAnimated=true&client=5f4a70b1-9d9d-47c3-b388-87235680bb54&collection=contentId-349143080&height=318&max-age=2592000&mode=full-fit&source=mediaCard&token=eyJhbGciOiJIUzI1NiJ9.eyJpc3MiOiI1ZjRhNzBiMS05ZDlkLTQ3YzMtYjM4OC04NzIzNTY4MGJiNTQiLCJhY2Nlc3MiOnsidXJuOmZpbGVzdG9yZTpjb2xsZWN0aW9uOmNvbnRlbnRJZC0zNDkxNDMwODAiOlsicmVhZCJdfSwiZXhwIjoxNzUwODY4NTY0LCJuYmYiOjE3NTA4NjU2ODR9.kiWaHMp7rkaYxzjq-CrseXoznLjUEXg_GD2-lTVvLB4&width=938)
        
3.  Set cut list that includes the 2875 part to the **T-DRILL Collaring** station.
    
4.  Set cut list that includes the 2041 part to the **T-DRILL Cutting** station.
    
5.  Select the cut lists and then click the **Send Cut List to Station** button.
    
6.  The cut lists will be sent to their respective stations. In addition, the Station will be disabled, the Status will be set to In Progress 0%, and the Send Cut List to Station button will be disabled.
    
    ![image-20250528-204812.png](https://media-cdn.atlassian.com/file/b40d8cd7-dd9d-4e04-b1f0-e4f32443e6a2/image/cdn?allowAnimated=true&client=5f4a70b1-9d9d-47c3-b388-87235680bb54&collection=contentId-349143080&height=318&max-age=2592000&mode=full-fit&source=mediaCard&token=eyJhbGciOiJIUzI1NiJ9.eyJpc3MiOiI1ZjRhNzBiMS05ZDlkLTQ3YzMtYjM4OC04NzIzNTY4MGJiNTQiLCJhY2Nlc3MiOnsidXJuOmZpbGVzdG9yZTpjb2xsZWN0aW9uOmNvbnRlbnRJZC0zNDkxNDMwODAiOlsicmVhZCJdfSwiZXhwIjoxNzUwODY4NTY0LCJuYmYiOjE3NTA4NjU2ODR9.kiWaHMp7rkaYxzjq-CrseXoznLjUEXg_GD2-lTVvLB4&width=947)
    
7.  Click the **Shops** tab.
    
8.  In the Shop drop-down, select the Division set for the station (Ex. Pipe Shop).
    
9.  In this example, both the T-DRILL Cutting station and the T-DRILL Collaring stations include 1 cut list.
    
    ![image-20250528-205012.png](https://media-cdn.atlassian.com/file/1b759f60-356b-4879-a2c4-bfe22dca4682/image/cdn?allowAnimated=true&client=5f4a70b1-9d9d-47c3-b388-87235680bb54&collection=contentId-349143080&height=549&max-age=2592000&mode=full-fit&source=mediaCard&token=eyJhbGciOiJIUzI1NiJ9.eyJpc3MiOiI1ZjRhNzBiMS05ZDlkLTQ3YzMtYjM4OC04NzIzNTY4MGJiNTQiLCJhY2Nlc3MiOnsidXJuOmZpbGVzdG9yZTpjb2xsZWN0aW9uOmNvbnRlbnRJZC0zNDkxNDMwODAiOlsicmVhZCJdfSwiZXhwIjoxNzUwODY4NTY0LCJuYmYiOjE3NTA4NjU2ODR9.kiWaHMp7rkaYxzjq-CrseXoznLjUEXg_GD2-lTVvLB4&width=760)
    
10.  Click the Station name in the list (Ex. T-DRILL Cutting).
    
11.  Click the **Tool** tab. All cut lists sent to the tool will display.
    
    ![image-20250528-205146.png](https://media-cdn.atlassian.com/file/93fa40ec-69bd-452c-9b7f-93af374a9831/image/cdn?allowAnimated=true&client=5f4a70b1-9d9d-47c3-b388-87235680bb54&collection=contentId-349143080&height=414&max-age=2592000&mode=full-fit&source=mediaCard&token=eyJhbGciOiJIUzI1NiJ9.eyJpc3MiOiI1ZjRhNzBiMS05ZDlkLTQ3YzMtYjM4OC04NzIzNTY4MGJiNTQiLCJhY2Nlc3MiOnsidXJuOmZpbGVzdG9yZTpjb2xsZWN0aW9uOmNvbnRlbnRJZC0zNDkxNDMwODAiOlsicmVhZCJdfSwiZXhwIjoxNzUwODY4NTY0LCJuYmYiOjE3NTA4NjU2ODR9.kiWaHMp7rkaYxzjq-CrseXoznLjUEXg_GD2-lTVvLB4&width=1270)
    
12.  To download the .CSV file, click the **Send to Tool** button. The file downloaded to the computer will include the package name, Material, Size, and date followed by .CSV.
    
    1.  **Note:** Since under Admin > Company > Tools, the Tool Type is set to T-DRILL Cutting, the file export will be different than the tool set to T-DRILL Collaring.
        
13.  Repeat from step 7, selecting the **T-DRILL Collaring** station instead.

# Tablet Tools - STRATUS Knowledge Base - Confluence

> ## Excerpt
> This article describes tools and techniques to use Stratus on a Tablet or iPad.

---
This article describes tools and techniques to use Stratus on a Tablet or iPad.

-   1 [Multiple Part Selection and Assembly Selection](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/187400193/Tablet+Tools#Multiple-Part-Selection-and-Assembly-Selection)
-   2 [Assembly Viewer Toggle Orientation](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/187400193/Tablet+Tools#Assembly-Viewer-Toggle-Orientation)
-   3 [Assembly Parts Table Zoom](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/187400193/Tablet+Tools#Assembly-Parts-Table-Zoom)
-   4 [Assembly Stratus Sheet Full Screen and Zoom buttons](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/187400193/Tablet+Tools#Assembly-Stratus-Sheet-Full-Screen-and-Zoom-buttons)
-   5 [Tablet Recommendations](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/187400193/Tablet+Tools#Tablet-Recommendations)
-   6 [Report Won't Generate on iPad](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/187400193/Tablet+Tools#Report-Won't-Generate-on-iPad)

## Multiple Part Selection and Assembly Selection

The **Multiple Part Selection** and the **Assembly Selection** options can be used by Tablet and iPad users to select multiple parts or assemblies in any of the Viewer pages. Both features work the same. Below is an example of how to use the **Multiple Part Selection** feature:

1.  Click the **Click to Change Settings** gear icon and then select the **Multiple Part Selection** checkbox in the sub-menu.
    
2.  Click either a part or space on the canvas and the sub-menu will disappear.
    
3.  Click multiple parts and they will all be selected.
    
4.  Click the first part, the last part, and then the **Select Connected** tool to select all parts between the 2 initially selected parts.
    
5.  Tools like those under **Actions** can be used once parts are selected.
    
6.  Click in empty space to clear your part selections.
    

## Assembly Viewer Toggle Orientation

Use the Toggle Orientation button to give you more screen width when viewing an assembly with a table.

1.  Below is the default side-by-side view where the Viewer is next to the Parts list.
    
2.  Click the **Toggle Orientation** button (top right) to toggle the page layout.
    
3.  The Parts list will re-orient under the Viewer and both views expand to the width of the tablet.
    
4.  Click the Toggle Orientation button again to restore the side-by-side orientation.
    

## Assembly Parts Table Zoom

To zoom the size of the Part's tab table list, click the minus or plus Table buttons.

## Assembly Stratus Sheet Full Screen and Zoom buttons

1.  Once you have generated a Stratus Sheet under Assemblies > Viewer > Stratus Sheet
    
    1.  To maximize the screen size, click the Full Screen Mode 
        
        button.
        
    2.  To zoom the sheet size, click the Zoom Out or Zoom In button. 
        
2.  Click the **Exit Full Screen Mode**
    
    button to return to the normal view.
    

## Tablet Recommendations

Stratus can run on any web-enabled device. Based on customer feedback, the Customer Success Group recommends Microsoft Surface tablets. Below is a summary.

1.  **Finger navigation** - When navigating with your finger, you are either touching the screen or not. Your finger does not provide any functionality when hovering over an object.
    
2.  **Hover Pen navigation** - (Recommended) Surface tablet pens provide the ability to hover over buttons. Hover 1/8" to 1/4" above the object to view options. (Option) Currently, iPad pens do not provide this functionality. The ability to hover over objects enables you to manually pull dimensions using the Stratus Dimensioning tool. Pens enable operators to keep gloves on and still execute many touchscreen functions. There are some work glove brands that enable use of gloved fingers on touchscreens.
    
3.  **Zoom** - (Recommended) Zoom is the same on any tablet whereby 2 fingers are used to zoom in/out.
    
4.  **Pan** - (Recommended) Select the Forge Viewer's Pan tool to pan the viewer. This allows you to pan with one finger. (Option) With 2 fingers pressing the screen, pan the viewer.
    
5.  **Rotate** - (Recommended) Use the dimension cube to rotate the view with a pen; it's difficult to use with your finger. (Option) With 2 fingers pressing the screen, swivel your 2 fingers to rotate.
    
6.  **Select Multiple parts** - (Recommended) Use the Stratus gear as described above to select multiple parts or to use the Select Connected tool.
    
7.  **Full Screen** - (Recommended) Use the **Toggle Orientation** button (top right) to toggle the page layout so that the Viewer and the Parts list are vertically in full screen mode.(Option) Use the Forge Viewer Full Screen tool which puts the Viewer in full screen mode but eliminates the Parts list.
    
8.  **Display Grid and Grid Offset Measurement tools** - Both tools work well to pull dimensions on any tablet.
    
9.  **Move tags** - Touch tag to select and then touch the target position to move and place the tag. There is no click and drag capability on a tablet.
    
10.  **Manual Dimensioning** - (Recommended) Surface tablet pens provide the ability to hover over buttons which will cycle through and select the dimensioning node. Once selected, drag to place the dimension.
    

## Report Won't Generate on iPad

When a report won't generate (Ex. Models > Viewer > Actions > Report > a CSV or PDF report) on an iPad, the problem is usually with the Safari Pop-Up Blocker.

To fix the issue:

1.  Go to Settings > Safari > Block Pop-Ups and turn off the setting to Block Pop-Ups.

# Total Station - STRATUS Knowledge Base - Confluence

> ## Excerpt
> A Total Station tool that can receive CSV points and/or DXF graphics files for hanger and other recognized points scoped out using packages.

---
A Total Station tool that can receive CSV points and/or DXF graphics files for hanger and other recognized points scoped out using packages.

-   1 [Configure Tool](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/345014474/Total+Station#Configure-Tool)
-   2 [Configure Station](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/345014474/Total+Station#Configure-Station)
-   3 [Stratus Workflow](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/345014474/Total+Station#Stratus-Workflow)

## Configure Tool

1.  Configure a **Tool** under Admin > Company > Tools. Note the generated Tool Id. See the [**Tools**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/215220225 "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/215220225") article for more information. Below is an example. 
    
    ![image-20250527-175009.png](blob:https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/0e585bcc-3102-40d1-8f1b-a88b59b65d43#media-blob-url=true&id=00ef250c-173e-46c6-b105-28b89d4516fd&collection=contentId-345014474&contextId=345014474&mimeType=image%2Fpng&name=image-20250527-175009.png&size=24116&width=1492&height=176&alt=image-20250527-175009.png)
    

## Configure Station

1.  Configure a **Station** under Admin > Company > Stations. Set **Division** to a Field division and the **Tool** to the Total Station created in the [**Configure Tool**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/345014474/Total+Station#Configure-Tool "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/345014474/Total+Station#Configure-Tool") section. See the [**Stations**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/215220408 "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/215220408") article for more information. 
    
    ![image-20250527-175307.png](blob:https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/16727f61-adf9-452e-827d-fd5a3d2b18d9#media-blob-url=true&id=9f9cd4bc-f113-4620-9b48-31afb96c5d91&collection=contentId-345014474&contextId=345014474&mimeType=image%2Fpng&name=image-20250527-175307.png&size=25790&width=989&height=258&alt=image-20250527-175307.png)
    

## Stratus Workflow

1.  In Stratus, create a Point List Package as described in the [**Generate Point Lists in Stratus**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/166821968/Package+Point+List#Generate-Point-Lists-in-Stratus "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/166821968/Package+Point+List#Generate-Point-Lists-in-Stratus") section of the Package Point List article.
    
2.  For the package, click the **Point Lists** tab.
    
3.  Click the **Generate Point Lists** button.
    
4.  Select the Total Station station configured in the [**Configure Station**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/345014474/Total+Station#Configure-Station "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/345014474/Total+Station#Configure-Station") section.
    
5.  Click the **Send Point List to Station** button.
    

**To generate the .CSV and DXF files:**

1.  Click the **Jobsites** menu item.
    
2.  Select the Project and Jobsite. One or more stations will display.
    
3.  Select the Total Station station configured in the [**Configure Station**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/345014474/Total+Station#Configure-Station "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/345014474/Total+Station#Configure-Station") section.
    
4.  Click the **Tool** tab. The Point List displays under Queued Items.
    
5.  Click the **Download** button.
    
    ![image-20250527-195548.png](https://media-cdn.atlassian.com/file/8623653c-bb15-48be-9f1f-f6a79ce0f38d/image/cdn?allowAnimated=true&client=5f4a70b1-9d9d-47c3-b388-87235680bb54&collection=contentId-345014474&height=366&max-age=2592000&mode=full-fit&source=mediaCard&token=eyJhbGciOiJIUzI1NiJ9.eyJpc3MiOiI1ZjRhNzBiMS05ZDlkLTQ3YzMtYjM4OC04NzIzNTY4MGJiNTQiLCJhY2Nlc3MiOnsidXJuOmZpbGVzdG9yZTpjb2xsZWN0aW9uOmNvbnRlbnRJZC0zNDUwMTQ0NzQiOlsicmVhZCJdfSwiZXhwIjoxNzUwODY4NTY2LCJuYmYiOjE3NTA4NjU2ODZ9.ejPrHgVdyKcy02aLXm-90YtwhcCi_p-z4KAiCg6oZ1U&width=1297)
    
6.  Two files, a .CSV and a .DXF will be downloaded:
    
    1.  PointList StationName DateTime.csv
        
    2.  Diagram StationName DateTime.dxf
        

___

# Valid Special Characters - STRATUS Knowledge Base - Confluence

> ## Excerpt
> The characters below are valid for names and values. Attempting to use a non-valid character may cause publish errors and failure. Contact the Service Desk if additional characters need to be used. Note: Stratus supports the UTF-8 character encoding and all its characters.

---
-   1 [Valid Characters](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/1794080934/Valid+Special+Characters#Valid-Characters)

## Valid Characters

The characters below are valid for names and values. Attempting to use a non-valid character may cause publish errors and failure. Contact the Service Desk if additional characters need to be used. **Note**: Stratus supports the UTF-8 character encoding and all its characters.

**Alphanumeric Characters**

abcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyzABCDEFGHIJKLMNOPQRSTUVWXYZ0123456789

**Special Characters**

<>|?\*.:!@#$%^&\*-\_+=”'/,

# Viewer Filters Tracking Date Range - STRATUS Knowledge Base - Confluence

> ## Excerpt
> The Models, Packages, and Assemblies viewers include a Date Range option. The date range option can be used to filters parts displayed in the viewer by when the part changed to a status. This can be useful to run reports for KPIs. For example, it can be used to display all items that have changed to the “Fabricated” status in the last month. All Tracking statuses are displayed in the list even if they do not have matching parts in the viewer.

---
The Models, Packages, and Assemblies viewers include a Date Range option. The date range option can be used to filters parts displayed in the viewer by when the part changed to a status. This can be useful to run reports for KPIs. For example, it can be used to display all items that have changed to the “Fabricated” status in the last month. All Tracking statuses are displayed in the list even if they do not have matching parts in the viewer. 

-   1[Viewer Tracking Date Range](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2120187905/Viewer+Filters+Tracking+Date+Range#ViewerFiltersTrackingDateRange-ViewerTrackingDateRange)

## Viewer Tracking Date Range

1.  By default, the Tracking date range option is disabled and unchecked.  
    ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/attachments/2120187905/image2023-7-28_16-8-24.png?version=1&modificationDate=1690578505688&cacheVersion=1&api=v2)
2.  Click the **Changes** checkbox to enable the feature.
    
    1.  All tracking statuses will be displayed in the list since dates change, different parts can be included and the counts for each will also update.
        
    2.  By default, the date range end date is set for today and the start date is set for 30 days in the past.
        
3.  Set the dates as needed.  
    ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/2120187905/image2022-9-21_11-47-54.png?version=1&modificationDate=1690578529239&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=400&height=597)
    
4.  Hover over either date to display the number of days, including the end date, that are in the date range.  
    ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/2120187905/image2022-9-22_13-58-28.png?version=1&modificationDate=1690578529362&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=359&height=250)
    
5.  Disable the Tracking date range option by unchecking the Changes checkbox.

# Viewer Settings and Search - STRATUS Knowledge Base - Confluence

> ## Excerpt
> The viewer Settings and viewer Search are common to all viewers (Models, Packages, and Assemblies) although some settings are specific to one viewer as noted.

---
The viewer **Settings** and viewer **Search** are common to all viewers (Models, Packages, and Assemblies) although some settings are specific to one viewer as noted. 

-   1[Viewer Settings](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2011136001/Viewer+Settings+and+Search#ViewerSettingsandSearch-ViewerSettings)
    -   1.1[Hidden Parts Shaded](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2011136001/Viewer+Settings+and+Search#ViewerSettingsandSearch-HiddenPartsShaded)
    -   1.2[Multiple Part Selection](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2011136001/Viewer+Settings+and+Search#ViewerSettingsandSearch-MultiplePartSelection)
    -   1.3[Assembly Selection](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2011136001/Viewer+Settings+and+Search#ViewerSettingsandSearch-AssemblySelection)
    -   1.4[Dynamic Tags](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2011136001/Viewer+Settings+and+Search#ViewerSettingsandSearch-DynamicTags)
    -   1.5[Decimal Inch (Feet Inch) Toggle](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2011136001/Viewer+Settings+and+Search#ViewerSettingsandSearch-DecimalInch(FeetInch)Toggle)
-   2[Viewer Search for Parts, Assemblies, and Packages](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2011136001/Viewer+Settings+and+Search#ViewerSettingsandSearch-ViewerSearchforParts%2CAssemblies%2CandPackages)
    -   2.1[Settings](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2011136001/Viewer+Settings+and+Search#ViewerSettingsandSearch-Settings)
    -   2.2[Search](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2011136001/Viewer+Settings+and+Search#ViewerSettingsandSearch-Search)
    -   2.3[Working with Search Results](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2011136001/Viewer+Settings+and+Search#ViewerSettingsandSearch-WorkingwithSearchResults)

## Viewer Settings

Viewer Settings are accessed by clicking the **Change Settings** gear icon.

![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/attachments/2011136001/image2022-12-8_8-35-26.png?version=1&modificationDate=1670510128265&cacheVersion=1&api=v2)

## Hidden Parts Shaded

The **Hidden Parts Shaded** checkbox toggles between displaying only the selected parts and non-selected parts so that the selected parts can be viewed within the context of surrounding parts.

**Viewers:** Available in all viewers (Models, Packages, and Assemblies).

To use the **Hidden Parts Shaded** toggle:

1.  Click the **Click to Change Settings** gear icon.
2.  When the **Hidden Parts Shaded** checkbox is **unchecked**, on the selected or filtered parts filtered to will display.![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/attachments/2011136001/image2022-12-7_14-26-3.png?version=1&modificationDate=1670444764984&cacheVersion=1&api=v2)
3.  When the **Hidden Parts Shaded** checkbox is **checked**, non-selected parts are visible in light gray so that the selected parts can be viewed within the context of surrounding parts.![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/attachments/2011136001/image2022-12-7_14-27-11.png?version=1&modificationDate=1670444832721&cacheVersion=1&api=v2)

## Multiple Part Selection

The **Multiple Part Selection** toggle checkbox is used primarily by tablet and iPad users who can't use the Ctrl or Shift key along with the mouse click to select multiple parts or assemblies. This feature tells STRATUS that any part or assembly selected should remain selected until a non-object like canvas white space is selected.

**Viewers:** Available in all viewers (Models, Packages, and Assemblies).

To use the **Multiple Part Selection** feature, under the Settings icon:

1.  Click the **Click to Change Settings** gear icon.
    
2.  Click the **Multiple Part Selection** checkbox.
    
3.  Click either a part or space on the canvas and the sub-menu will disappear.
    
4.  Click multiple parts and they will all be selected.
    
5.  Or, click the first part, the last part, and then the **Select Connected** tool to select all parts between the 2 initially selected parts.
    
6.  Once parts or assemblies are selected, Tools like those under **Actions** can be used.
    
    ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/attachments/2011136001/image2022-12-7_14-30-53.png?version=1&modificationDate=1670445054548&cacheVersion=1&api=v2)
    
7.  Click in empty space to clear your part selections.
    

## Assembly Selection

When used in conjunction with the **Tab** key, **the Assembly Selection** toggle actions change, giving users the flexibility to use the Tab key to override either the Select assembly or the Select Part action depending on whether Assembly Selection is checked or not.

**Viewers:** Available only in the Packages Viewer and Models Viewer.

1.  **Check** the **Assembly Selection** option.
    1.  Hover over an assembly and click. The whole assembly is selected.  
        ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/attachments/2011136001/image2022-12-7_14-54-2.png?version=1&modificationDate=1670446443636&cacheVersion=1&api=v2)
    2.  Hover over an assembly, **press the TAB key, and then click.** The individual part you are hovering over is selected.  
        ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/attachments/2011136001/image2022-12-7_14-55-56.png?version=1&modificationDate=1670446557185&cacheVersion=1&api=v2)
2.  **Uncheck** the **Assembly Selection** option:
    1.  Hover over a part and click. The part you are hovering over is selected.  
        ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/attachments/2011136001/image2022-12-7_14-56-45.png?version=1&modificationDate=1670446607043&cacheVersion=1&api=v2)
    2.  Hover over a part, **press the **TAB** key, and then click**. The assembly that contains the part is selected.  
        ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/attachments/2011136001/image2022-12-7_14-57-27.png?version=1&modificationDate=1670446648223&cacheVersion=1&api=v2)

## Dynamic Tags

The **Dynamic Tags** toggle checkbox can be used to declutter tags by removing tags that overlap other tags from the display.

**Viewers:** Available in all viewers (Models, Packages, and Assemblies).

**To use the Dynamic Tags feature:**

1.  Click the **Click to Change Settings** gear icon.
    
2.  When the **Dynamic Tags** checkbox is **unchecked**, all of the tags display, overlap, and can be difficult to use.
    
    ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/attachments/2011136001/image2022-12-7_14-35-25.png?version=1&modificationDate=1670445327065&cacheVersion=1&api=v2)
    
3.  When the **Dynamic Tags** checkbox is **checked**, overlapping tags no longer display and continue to not display when zooming and orbiting views.
    
    ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/attachments/2011136001/image2022-12-7_14-35-42.png?version=1&modificationDate=1670445343209&cacheVersion=1&api=v2)
    

## Decimal Inch (Feet Inch) Toggle

For Imperial models, dimensions can be displayed in **Decimal Inches** or **Feet Inches** in the Assemblies > Viewer.

**Viewers:** Available in all viewers (Models, Packages, and Assemblies).

To toggle between **Feet Inch** and **Decimal Inch** dimensions:

1.  Click the **Click to Change Settings** gear icon.
    
2.  When **Decimal Inch** is unchecked, dimensions display in **Feet Inch**.
    
    ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/attachments/2011136001/image2022-12-7_14-37-22.png?version=1&modificationDate=1670445443472&cacheVersion=1&api=v2)
    
3.  When **Decimal Inch** is checked, dimensions display **Decimal Inch**.
    
    ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/attachments/2011136001/image2022-12-7_14-37-48.png?version=1&modificationDate=1670445469076&cacheVersion=1&api=v2)
    

## Viewer Search for Parts, Assemblies, and Packages

The **Viewers Search** is available in the Models, Packages, and Assemblies Viewers and provides the ability to search for parts, assemblies, and packages using various properties. The viewer **Search**  function is accessed by clicking the **Search** icon.  
![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/attachments/2011136001/image2022-12-8_8-37-34.png?version=1&modificationDate=1670510255899&cacheVersion=1&api=v2)

## Settings

1.  Check the Settings to be used for the search. **Note**: The page does not need to be refreshed for the settings to be changed; Settings are sticky and will be retained from one viewer to the next and from one model to the next.
    
    ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/2011136001/image2022-3-25_9-50-21.png?version=1&modificationDate=1670448819511&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=340&height=281)
    
    1.  **Match On** \- **Note**: The properties searched may depend on object type (Package, Assembly, or Part) as noted below.
        
        1.  **All** \- Each **Match On** checkbox will be checked.
            
        2.  **Cad ID**
            
            1.  Package - None
                
            2.  Assembly - STRATUS.Part.AssemblyCadId
                
            3.  Part - STRATUS.Part.CadId
                
        3.  **Description**
            
            1.  Package - Order(Package).Description
                
            2.  Assembly - None
                
            3.  Part - STRATUS.Part.Description
                
        4.  **Element ID**
            
            1.  Package - None
                
            2.  Assembly - None
                
            3.  Part - ElementId in Revit models
                
        5.  **Name**
            
            1.  Package - STRATUS.Package.Name
                
            2.  Assembly - STRATUS.Part.AssemblyNamee
                
            3.  Part - None
                
        6.  **Number**
            
            1.  Package - None
                
            2.  Assembly - None
                
            3.  Part - Number in the CinxProperties (I believe it will be listed under Properties as Number), if it exists
                
        7.  **QR URL**
            
            1.  Package - STRATUS.Part.PackageQRCode
                
            2.  Assembly - STRATUS.Part.AssemblyQRCode
                
            3.  Part - STRATUS.Part.QRCode
                
        8.  **Web ID**
            
            1.  Package - STRATUS.Part.WebId of parts in the package
                
            2.  Assembly - STRATUS.Part.WebId of parts in the Assembly
                
            3.  Part - STRATUS.Part.WebId
                
    2.  Settings:
        
        1.  **Replace Selection** \- When clicking Item A in the search results, Item A will highlight both in the viewer and in the search results. When Item B is clicked in the search results, Item B will be highlighted, but Item A will no longer be highlighted. Selecting Item B replaces Item A. For example, assembly DMV-ROOF-0001 was selected, but then assembly DMV-ROOF-0002 was selected and is now highlighted in the viewer.
            
            ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/2011136001/image2022-2-7_11-44-10.png?version=1&modificationDate=1670448819597&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=1000&height=295)
            
        2.  **Keep Open After Selecting** \- When clicking in the search results, Item A will highlight both in the viewer and in the search results. When Item B is clicked in the search results, both Item A and Item B will be highlighted. For example, assembly DMV-ROOF-0001 was selected and now assembly DMV-ROOF-0002 has been selected and both are highlighted in the viewer.
            
            ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/2011136001/image2022-2-7_11-44-49.png?version=1&modificationDate=1670448819704&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=1000&height=399)
            
            iii. **Checked Exact Match (Case Sensitive)** \- When checked, the search criteria will only display results when the entire **Match On** value is matched exactly.
            
            1.  In this case, where the search criteria is (Ex. QA), **No search results** match the **Exact Match** search criteria.
                
                ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/2011136001/image2022-3-25_9-55-35.png?version=1&modificationDate=1670448819785&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=345&height=311)
                
            2.  In this case, where the search criteria is (Ex. QA-001), search results that exactly match the **Exact Match** search criteria display.
                
                ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/2011136001/image2022-3-25_9-56-10.png?version=1&modificationDate=1670448819888&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=343&height=335)
                

## Search

Search criteria can be entered using any of the following three methods:

1.  **Type text** into the text box.
    
    1.  For example, enter search characters (Ex. H). As characters are entered matching Packages, Assemblies, and Parts will display in the list.
        
        ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/2011136001/image2022-2-7_11-45-32.png?version=1&modificationDate=1670448819987&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=300&height=305)
        
2.  **Scan a QR Code using a handheld scanner**. **Note**: The **QR URL** settings must be checked under Match On.
    
    1.  Before scanning, the Viewer Search page must be the active page (Ex. the last mouse click must be on the page).
        
        1.  (Optional) - The **Scan QR code using handheld scanner** button does not have to be clicked to scan a QR code. The purpose of this button is to remind users that a handheld scanner can be used to enter a QR code URL. If the button is clicked the following message will display.
            
            ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/attachments/2011136001/image2022-2-7_11-46-11.png?version=1&modificationDate=1670448820074&cacheVersion=1&api=v2)
            
    2.  Use the handheld scanner to scan the QR code.
        
    3.  The QR code will display in the search text and in the search results.
        
        ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/2011136001/2022-03-25_09-42-14.png?version=1&modificationDate=1670448820168&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=700&height=407)
        
3.  **Scan a QR Code using a tablet camera. Note**: The **QR URL** settings must be checked under Match On.
    
    1.  Click the **Scan a QR Code using a tablet camera** button. The **Scan QR Code with Camera or Reader** dialog will display where the camera will be selected.
        
        ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/2011136001/image2022-2-7_11-47-32.png?version=1&modificationDate=1670448820247&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=485&height=250)
        
    2.  Point the camera to the QR code until the **Scan Successful** popup message displays in the bottom left corner.
        
    3.  The QR code will display in the search text and in the search results.
        

## Working with Search Results

After search results display:

1.  **Expand/Collapse View Matches**
    
    1.  Items under Packages, Assemblies, and Parts can be expanded by clicking the View # Matches link (Ex. View 7 Matches).
        
        ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/2011136001/image2022-2-7_11-49-9.png?version=1&modificationDate=1670448820352&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=300&height=283)
        
    2.  Click the **Collapse** button ( left of the Assemblies heading) to return to displaying the list Packages, Assemblies, and Parts subset.
        
        ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/2011136001/image2022-2-7_11-50-9.png?version=1&modificationDate=1670448820452&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=309&height=250)
        
2.  **Zoom on selection(s)**
    
    1.  Select one or more items in the search results.
        
    2.  Click the **Zoom** button to zoom in on the selected Packages, Assemblies, and Parts in the viewer. Zoom results depend on where these items are located in the model.
        
        ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/2011136001/image2022-2-7_11-51-10.png?version=1&modificationDate=1670448820534&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=750&height=422)
        
3.  **Search Results Outside the Current Packages / Assemblies Viewer** \- Since the search searches the model, parts, assemblies, and packages outside the current Packages or Assemblies Viewer will display in the search results annotated with an icon to distinguish it in the list.
    
    1.  Currently, Package 123-FP-ROOF-0003 is open in the viewer.
        
        ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/2011136001/image2022-2-7_11-51-55.png?version=1&modificationDate=1670448820617&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=1000&height=435)
        
    2.  In this example, the search for 38358-FP-0003 is a different package name.
        
        ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/2011136001/image2022-2-7_11-52-39.png?version=1&modificationDate=1670448820702&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=1000&height=421)
        
    3.  Click package 38358-FP-0003 in the search results and it will display highlighted in the current viewer. This shows package 38358-FP-0003 in relation to the currently opened package.
        
        ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/2011136001/image2022-2-7_11-53-16.png?version=1&modificationDate=1670448820849&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=1000&height=441)
        
    4.  Click anywhere else in the model or unselect package 38358-FP-0003 and it will no longer display.

# Viewer Stratus Sheet for Assemblies and Packages - STRATUS Knowledge Base - Confluence

> ## Excerpt
> This article documents the Stratus Sheet tab functionality. The Stratus Sheet is a Report and a Template that can be formatted to print as a PDF. When the Stratus Template includes a View (Iso, Front, Top) the parts in the 3D viewer will display in the Stratus Sheet and if displayed will also include tags and dimension labels. Tags and Dimensions can be modified in the Stratus Sheet. The Stratus Sheet tab functionality is almost identical between the Assemblies > Viewer and the Packages > Viewer.

---
This article documents the Stratus Sheet tab functionality. The Stratus Sheet is a **Report** and a **Template** that can be formatted to print as a PDF. When the Stratus Template includes a View (Iso, Front, Top) the parts in the 3D viewer will display in the Stratus Sheet and if displayed will also include tags and dimension labels. Tags and Dimensions can be modified in the Stratus Sheet. The Stratus Sheet tab functionality is almost identical between the Assemblies > Viewer and the Packages > Viewer.

-   1 [Create a Template](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2136506865/Viewer+Stratus+Sheet+for+Assemblies+and+Packages#Create-a-Template)
-   2 [Create a Report](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2136506865/Viewer+Stratus+Sheet+for+Assemblies+and+Packages#Create-a-Report)
    -   2.1 [Packages Viewer Notes](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2136506865/Viewer+Stratus+Sheet+for+Assemblies+and+Packages#Packages-Viewer-Notes)
    -   2.2 [Assemblies Viewer Notes](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2136506865/Viewer+Stratus+Sheet+for+Assemblies+and+Packages#Assemblies-Viewer-Notes)
    -   2.3 [Default Assembly Report](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2136506865/Viewer+Stratus+Sheet+for+Assemblies+and+Packages#Default-Assembly-Report)
        -   2.3.1 [Method 1 - Packages > Categories > Default Assembly Report](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2136506865/Viewer+Stratus+Sheet+for+Assemblies+and+Packages#Method-1---Packages-%3E-Categories-%3E-Default-Assembly-Report)
        -   2.3.2 [Method 2 - Report > Assemblies Filter](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2136506865/Viewer+Stratus+Sheet+for+Assemblies+and+Packages#Method-2---Report-%3E-Assemblies-Filter)
-   3 [Tags, Dimension Labels, and Orientation](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2136506865/Viewer+Stratus+Sheet+for+Assemblies+and+Packages#Tags%2C-Dimension-Labels%2C-and-Orientation)
-   4 [Generate PDF](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2136506865/Viewer+Stratus+Sheet+for+Assemblies+and+Packages#Generate-PDF)
-   5 [Print Stratus Sheet](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2136506865/Viewer+Stratus+Sheet+for+Assemblies+and+Packages#Print-Stratus-Sheet)
-   6 [Full-Screen Mode](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2136506865/Viewer+Stratus+Sheet+for+Assemblies+and+Packages#Full-Screen-Mode)
-   7 [Pan](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2136506865/Viewer+Stratus+Sheet+for+Assemblies+and+Packages#Pan)
-   8 [Zoom](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2136506865/Viewer+Stratus+Sheet+for+Assemblies+and+Packages#Zoom)
-   9 [Extents](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2136506865/Viewer+Stratus+Sheet+for+Assemblies+and+Packages#Extents)
-   10 [PDF Issues](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2136506865/Viewer+Stratus+Sheet+for+Assemblies+and+Packages#PDF-Issues)
    -   10.1 [Chrome](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2136506865/Viewer+Stratus+Sheet+for+Assemblies+and+Packages#Chrome)
    -   10.2 [Firefox](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2136506865/Viewer+Stratus+Sheet+for+Assemblies+and+Packages#Firefox)

## Create a Template

For information on how to create a Template, see the [**Create a Report Template**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/157974589/Templates+Admin#Templates(Admin)-CreateaReportTemplate.1 "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/157974589/Templates+Admin#Templates(Admin)-CreateaReportTemplate.1") article on the Templates (Admin) page.

## Create a Report

For information on how to create a Report, see the [**Report (Admin)**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/200998967 "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/200998967") article. For the report to be available in the:

## Packages Viewer Notes

For a Report to display in the Packages > Viewer > Stratus Sheet > Reports drop-down, the report must include the following:

![](blob:https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/0b4b7896-def9-499d-be4a-a51d8702b807)

-   **Format** = PDF
    
-   **Item Type** = Package Details 
    
-   **Template** = Any template 
    
-   **Package Viewer** = Checked
    
-   **Report Fields** = Valid report fields
    

**To display the report in the Packages > Viewer > Stratus Sheet:**

1.  In the Stratus Sheet tab, select the Report and the **Stratus Sheet** will generate using the report.
    

## Assemblies Viewer Notes

For a Report to display in the Assemblies > Viewer > Parts > Reports drop-down, the report must include the following:

![](blob:https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/217c5a5f-aa54-4e69-95ea-bd06b5f3849b)

-   **Format** = PDF
    
-   **Item Type** = Part 
    
-   **Template** = Any template 
    
-   **Assembly Viewer** = Checked
    
-   **Report Fields** = Valid report fields
    

**To display the report in the Assemblies > Viewer > Parts tab:**

1.  Select the Report in the **Parts** tab and then click the **Stratus Sheet** tab to generate the Stratus Sheet using the report.
    

## Default Assembly Report

When the Assemblies > Viewer loads an assembly for the first time, there are 2 methods that can be used to select the default part report. Method 1 requires that the assembly be within a package. Method 2 has been in Stratus for a long time and can still be used. 

**Note**: Using either method, if a different report is selected after the assembly loads for the first, the system will select that same report the next time you view that particular assembly.

### Method 1 - Packages > Categories > Default Assembly Report

**Default Assembly Report**  - Under Admin > Company > Package Categories, the **Default Assembly Report** option enables administrators to select a default Parts report when loading an assembly for the first time in the Assemblies > Viewer. The selected report is associated with a specific Package Category. Therefore the default report will only apply to assemblies included in packages within the Package Category.

See the [**Default Assembly Report**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/166199351/Package+Categories+Admin#DefaultAssemblyReport "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/166199351/Package+Categories+Admin#DefaultAssemblyReport") article for more information. 

This method was added to Stratus in v6.3.1.

### Method 2 - Report > Assemblies Filter

**Assembly Filter** - Under Admin > Company > Reports, an Assembly Filter can be set to select a default Parts report when loading an assembly for the first time in the Assemblies > Viewer. When the assembly loads, the selected Assembly Filter will compare the parts in the assembly with the Assembly Filter for each relevant Report. The Assembly Filter that matches the most parts will be selected as the default Report.

This was the only method to select a default report until v6.3.1.

The ability to move and hide Tags and update Dimension labels is the same for Stratus Sheets in Packages and Assemblies. The orientation set by the View can also be overridden.

To move or hide tags/dimension labels in the Stratus Sheet:

1.  If neither the **Dimensioning** or **Display - Item Numbers** tool is turned on in the 3D viewer:
    
    1.  Neither Dimension or Item Numbers will display in the 3D Viewer.  
        **Note**: In the example below, the Stratus Sheet Report > Template > View Style settings for **Render Dimensions** and **Render Item Numbers** is checked, therefore, these display in the Stratus Sheet but are not editable.  See the [**View Styles (Admin)**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/8749081 "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/8749081") article for more information.
        
    2.  Click the **Adjust view orientation and annotation** button.  
        
    3.  Neither Dimension or Item Numbers will will be editable in the Stratus Sheet.
        
    4.  Notice the orientation can be changed using the cube or a click/drag with the mouse.
        
2.  When either **Dimensioning** and **Display - Item Numbers** tools are turned on in the 3D Viewer:
    
    1.  Either Dimensions, Item Numbers, or both, like in the example below, will display in the 3D Viewer.
        
    2.  Click the **Adjust view orientation and annotation** button.  
        
    3.  Either Dimensions, Item Numbers, or both, like in the example below, will be editable in the Stratus Sheet.
        
    4.  Notice the orientation can be changed using the cube or a click/drag with the mouse.
        
3.  To Move or Hide Stratus Sheet dimensions and/or Item Numbers, with either **Dimensioning** and **Display - Item Numbers** tools are turned on in the 3D Viewer, click the **Adjust view orientation and annotation** button
    
    ![](blob:https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/e3f65016-9e74-4e78-b9a2-d515332f90db)
    
    . 
4.  The Item Number tags and Dimensioning labels will display. **Hover** over a tag or label and the **Move** and **Hide** buttons display.
    
    1.  **Move** - Note: Moving a dimension or a tag will affect all viewports as well as the 3D viewer. As a result, after moving a dimension, the Cancel button does not move the dimension back to a previous position, rather it is saved.  
        To move the tag/label:
        
        1.  Click the blue move button and let go of the mouse.
            
        2.  Move your mouse toward where you want to place the tag. The tag will disappear as you move your mouse. A leader will display and will follow your mouse.
            
        3.  Click the mouse when you are ready to place the tag. The tag will display.
            
        4.  Click **Save** or **Cancel**. When the viewer refreshes, the dimension is moved in the Stratus Sheet and the 3D viewer.
            
    2.  **Hide** - Click the hide button. The tag will change to be semi-transparent with gray text on the viewport being edited.
        
    3.  Click **Save**. When the viewer refreshes, the dimension is hidden in the Stratus Sheet, but remains visible in the 3D viewer.
        
5.  **Note**: If you try to set the orientation on a view placeholder with all parts filtered out (the assembly will not display if all parts have been filtered out) based on the view style set on the template, you will get a message saying that there is nothing visible to be oriented and the operation will be canceled.
    

## Generate PDF

1.  To generate a PDF, click the **PDF** button. The option to open or save the PDF will display.
    
    ![](blob:https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/e5322a6e-6aa2-4887-83f3-e2a71c1528f9)
    
    1.  The PDF will be downloaded to the computer.
        
    2.  The PDF will be opened in a separate browser tab.
        
    3.  The PDF will be added to the Attachments tab.
        
        1.  The file name syntax will be \[Assembly Name\]-\[Report Name\].pdf
            
2.  On an iPad:
    
    1.  Click the **PDF** button. The PDF button text changes to Please Wait.
        
    2.  At the download prompt, click **Download**. 
        
    3.  In Safari, the download icon button displays in the top toolbar while the document is being downloaded. Click this icon to open the file.
        

## Print Stratus Sheet

The Stratus Sheet can be printed using the Print button.

1.  Click the **Print** button.
    
2.  Select the printer.
    
3.  If you have an issue printing, see below for browser-specific configurations.
    

## Full-Screen Mode

Click the full-screen mode button to view the Stratus Sheet in full-screen. To exit full-screen mode, either click the Exit full-screen button or press the Esc key.  

![](blob:https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/3421b17e-3d0e-46c7-8201-51f8bfa412e7)

## Pan

To pan the Stratus Sheet, either click the Pan button or press and hold the mouse middle button while panning.

![](blob:https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/a6fefa9e-07b4-43be-8c4b-6332ea8d15ce)

## Zoom

Zoom within a Stratus Sheet can be accomplished either with the Zoom- and Zoom+ buttons or using the mouse scroll wheel.

![](blob:https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/173c086c-d083-409b-8935-6c5fad7f7ccb)

## Extents

To return to the default Stratus Sheet zoom level, click the **Extents** button.  

![](blob:https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/d369659b-9717-497e-93dc-a3fcd65e9c40)

  
 

## PDF Issues

## Chrome

There may be some configuration required depending on your web browser settings.

1.  If you are using Chrome and you get the following message:
    
2.  In Chrome, go to Customize > Settings
    
3.  Search for PDF and click Site Settings.
    
4.  Scroll to the bottom and click **Additional content settings** and then click PDF documents.
    
5.  Disable the **Download PDF files instead of automatically opening them in Chrome** button.
    
6.  Try to Print the Stratus Sheet again.
    

## Firefox

There may be some configuration required depending on your web browser settings.

1.  In Firefox, click Open Menu, then click Options.
    
2.  Search for PDF and then change the Portable Document Format (PDF) setting to Open in Firefox.
    
3.  Try to Print the Stratus Sheet.

# Watts 3DPP - STRATUS Knowledge Base - Confluence

> ## Excerpt
> This article describes the integration between Stratus and Watts 3DPP.

---
This article describes the integration between Stratus and Watts 3DPP.

-   1 [Configure Tool](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/343769721/Watts+3DPP#Configure-Tool)
-   2 [Configure App Key](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/343769721/Watts+3DPP#Configure-App-Key)
-   3 [Configure Station](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/343769721/Watts+3DPP#Configure-Station)
-   4 [Configure Pipe Cuts](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/343769721/Watts+3DPP#Configure-Pipe-Cuts)
-   5 [Configure Watts 3DPP Software](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/343769721/Watts+3DPP#Configure-Watts-3DPP-Software)
-   6 [Send Cut List to Watts 3DPP](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/343769721/Watts+3DPP#Send-Cut-List-to-Watts-3DPP)

## Configure Tool

1.  Configure a **Tool** under Admin > Company > Tools. Note the generated Tool Id. See the [**Tools**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/215220225 "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/215220225") article for more information. Below is an example. 
    
    ![image-20250527-172152.png](blob:https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/5225b524-9c83-4b33-86bf-72e23a162054#media-blob-url=true&id=92397eda-256f-490a-879e-0ad6b7559027&collection=contentId-343769721&contextId=343769721&mimeType=image%2Fpng&name=image-20250527-172152.png&size=23340&width=1414&height=181&alt=image-20250527-172152.png)
    

## Configure App Key

1.  Configure an **App Key** selecting the **WattsMueller** Partner App under Admin > Company > App Key. See the [**App Keys (Admin)**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/201654303 "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/201654303") article for more information. Below is an example. 
    
    ![image-20250527-172242.png](blob:https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/bf3d3e72-fc9f-464e-a21f-34e495a2666b#media-blob-url=true&id=fc8fc6f7-3e85-4e3c-b946-c1bead968a0e&collection=contentId-343769721&contextId=343769721&mimeType=image%2Fpng&name=image-20250527-172242.png&size=17962&width=1131&height=176&alt=image-20250527-172242.png)
    

## Configure Station

1.  Configure a **Station** under Admin > Company > Stations. See the [**Stations**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/215220408 "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/215220408") article for more information.  
    

## Configure Pipe Cuts

1.  Configure **Pipe Cuts** under Admin > Company > Pipe Cuts. See the [**Pipe Cuts**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/201490457 "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/201490457") article for more information. These Pipe Cuts settings ensure that cut lists correctly use Stratus Part Templates.
    

## Configure Watts 3DPP Software

1.  Open the Watts 3DPP software.
    
2.  Go to the **Integrations** configuration panel.
    
3.  Enter into the Tool ID the Stratus **Tool Id** from the [**Configure Tool**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/343769721/Watts+3DPP#Configure-Tool "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/343769721/Watts+3DPP#Configure-Tool") section.
    

## Send Cut List to Watts 3DPP

Once all configurations are complete, a cut list can be sent to the Watts Station.

1.  In Stratus under Packages > Viewer > Cut Lists:
    
    1.  Click the **Generate a Cut List** button. Select the Station configured to handle the Watts cut list. See the [**Configure Station**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/343769721/Watts+3DPP#Configure-Station "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/343769721/Watts+3DPP#Configure-Station") section.
        
    2.  Click the **Send Cut List to Station** button.
        
    3.  Cut List Actions
        
        1.  **Delete** \- Before the Watts 3DPP process begins importing cut lists, the **Delete** button can be used to delete a cut list from the import. However, once Watts 3DPP updates information from Stratus, the cut list can only be deleted within the Watts 3DPP software.
            
        2.  **Unassign from Station** - Before the Watts 3DPP process begins importing cut lists, the **Unassign from Station** button can be used to exclude a cut list from the import. However, once Watts 3DPP updates information from Stratus, the cut list can only be deleted within the Watts 3DPP software.
            
        3.  **Print Labels** - Labels are created using the Watts 3DPP software.
            
    4.  **Note:** Once a cut list is sent from Stratus to the Watts 3DPP station, there is no further communication or status update from Watts 3DPP back to the Stratus Cut List page. In addition, cut list tools like Delete, Unassign from Station, and Print Labels cannot be used.
        
2.  In the Watts 3DPP software:
    
    1.  Select import from Stratus whenever cut lists need to be imported from Stratus. When clicked, Watts 3DPP software uses the Tool Id to load cut lists from Stratus.
        
    2.  Continue work in Watts 3DPP and create labels.

# sPoint.rfa for Revit - STRATUS Knowledge Base - Confluence

> ## Excerpt
> The sPoint .rfa can be loaded into one or more Revit families and enables snap point control of dimensions in STRATUS. Without the sPoint .rfa, STRATUS will detect all of the different points and vertices across all the geometry in your families which is both a performance inhibitor and makes it difficult to pull the correct dimensions.  Use case examples includes the ability to pull dimensions from hanger to hanger, or, from rod to rod, from equipment pad corners, from stubs, and from sleeves. Note: sPoint is not yet available under Packages > Point Exports.

---
The sPoint .rfa can be loaded into one or more Revit families and enables snap point control of dimensions in STRATUS. Without the sPoint .rfa, STRATUS will detect all of the different points and vertices across all the geometry in your families which is both a performance inhibitor and makes it difficult to pull the correct dimensions.  Use case examples includes the ability to pull dimensions from hanger to hanger, or, from rod to rod, from equipment pad corners, from stubs, and from sleeves. Note: sPoint is not yet available under Packages > Point Exports. 

-   1[STRATUS 08-15-19 Implementation Webinar - (sPoint for Revit 15:13)](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/256409602/sPoint.rfa+for+Revit#sPoint.rfaforRevit-STRATUS08-15-19ImplementationWebinar-(sPointforRevit15%3A13))
-   2[sPoint.rfa Download](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/256409602/sPoint.rfa+for+Revit#sPoint.rfaforRevit-sPoint.rfaDownload)
-   3[sPoint Family Summary](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/256409602/sPoint.rfa+for+Revit#sPoint.rfaforRevit-sPointFamilySummary)
-   4[Working with the sPoint.rfa in Revit](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/256409602/sPoint.rfa+for+Revit#sPoint.rfaforRevit-WorkingwiththesPoint.rfainRevit)
-   5[Publish a Model and Pull sPoint Dimensions](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/256409602/sPoint.rfa+for+Revit#sPoint.rfaforRevit-PublishaModelandPullsPointDimensions)

## sPoint.rfa Download

Download the **[sPoint.rfa](https://gogtp.sharepoint.com/:f:/s/CustomerSharedFiles/EoX0mw_waSRIrupJPSFqcn0BJf4SJZOQmo0hTKB8eCFTeQ?e=ZNdFvG)**.

## sPoint Family Summary

The sPoint family is a cube.  The family includes:

1.  **Detail lines** that have visibility settings that are visible in Coarse and Medium views.  
    ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/256409602/image2019-8-16_13-57-1.png?version=1&modificationDate=1565981822748&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=353&height=346)
2.  **Outer cube geometry** that is visible in all views but is controlled by a visibility parameter.  
    ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/256409602/image2019-8-16_13-58-26.png?version=1&modificationDate=1565981908589&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=624&height=639)
3.  **Line work** in the middle includes Cross Visibility and Cube Visibility settings.  
    ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/256409602/image2019-8-16_13-59-10.png?version=1&modificationDate=1565981952707&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=555&height=530)

## Working with the sPoint.rfa in Revit

1.  Load the sPoint family into a hanger project, for example, and place it where the rod intersects with the face of the strut, or the edge corners, or at the top of the rod.  
    ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/256409602/image2019-8-16_14-0-25.png?version=1&modificationDate=1565982026592&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=487&height=650)
2.  In the Family Editor, in Plan view place the point so that it is aligned (AL) to the reference plane and constrained. Now the point will shift when the family dimensions change.  
    ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/256409602/image2019-8-16_14-0-50.png?version=1&modificationDate=1565982051921&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=624&height=329)
3.  One key to linking visibility controls for a point where extractions are from deeply nested layers, they have to be made into a **Shared Family** which enables you to run a schedule and extract out the data. So that you can still control the visibility of the point when looking at a project view of the hanger and retain the point origin for the API extraction, set the sPoint Cube Visibility and sPoint Visibility as follows:  
    ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/256409602/image2019-8-16_14-1-38.png?version=1&modificationDate=1565982100195&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=624&height=323)
4.  Load the hanger into the project where you can see all the points.  
    ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/256409602/image2019-8-16_14-2-3.png?version=1&modificationDate=1565982124792&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=432&height=447)
5.  In the model, control how points are visible.  
    ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/256409602/image2019-8-16_14-2-33.png?version=1&modificationDate=1565982155064&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=624&height=263)

## Publish a Model and Pull sPoint Dimensions 

1.  Publish the model and manually pull the points in a STRATUS Viewer.  
    ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/256409602/image2019-8-16_14-4-2.png?version=1&modificationDate=1565982243128&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=624&height=397)
